1b1: shin tu rgyas po chen pa mang sangs rgyas phal pa zhes bya ga/ zab pa dang ga jubacu
1b2: bzhi pa/ / de nas byang chub sems dpa' tshogs chen po de'i nang nas byang chub sems dpa' kha cig 'di snyam du sems
1b3: te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom
1b4: ldan 'das rnams kyi sngon gyi smon la ma rang 'byung ba rnam par dag pa ni ji tsam pa zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab/ / sangs rgyas bcom lda
1b5: 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
1b6: kyi sangs rgyas skye ba ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin
1b7: gshegs pa'i sku ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin ga
1b8: pa'i gsung ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i

2a1: jimam zhig dra bsam gyis mi lhag/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyid bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul ba nang nam zhanag du bas ma rgyas ma khyag/ sangs rgyas
2a2: b com ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa mi mnga' ba'i rnam par spyod pa na jo tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa ni ji tsam zhig bsam gyis ma
2a3: khyab snyam pa dang / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' de dag gi sems mkhyen pas thugs su chud nas/ byang chub sems dpa' ud dpa' la'i snying po// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs
2a4: kyis byin du brlabs so/ / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyis byin dang ldan par mdzad do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od kyis snang ba mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi gzi brjid kyis yongs su rgyas par mdzad de/
2a5: sangs rgyas kyi mi 'jigs pa la rab tu bzhag go/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi dbyings la 'dug pa khong du chud par mdzadado// sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba nyid dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi yul rab tu rtogs par
2a6: mdzad do/ / chags pa med pa'i rgyud 'byam klas pa la rab tu bzhag go// sangs rgyas thams cad gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa'i rigs rab tu rtogs par mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi tshul
2a7: gnas brjod du med pa la rab tu gzhag pa mdzad do/ / de nas byang chub sems dpa' ud pa la'i snying pos chos kyi dbyings la bajug pa rig cing khong du chud pas chags pa med pa'i dbyings su bsgrubs par
2a8: yid dang / chos thams cad la bsgribs pa med par gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang ldan pa'i yang dag par 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjes su song ba'i sas

2b1: rgyas pas ba dang / snying pos lta ba'i sems can thams cad yongs su spyod pa'i gca chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yid ma dang / spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor thun 'chad pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas rgya la shes
2b2: mngon par bsgrub pa skad cig gi chags pa rnam par spyod pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sgo mdza ba mi zad pa dang / so so yang dag par rig pa'i rnam pa gzungs thams cad kyis sdang bar byas pa dang / ldan pas
2b3: sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' pad mo'i snying po la 'di skad ces smras so/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ tshad med pa la rnam par spyod pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras//
2b4: sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par 'phrul pa chen po la rnam par spyod pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa thams cad la/ sku'i mtshan
2b5: thams cad rab tu brnyas pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'khor la 'khor ba ni ting nge 'dzin dang / dgongs pas sbyar ba'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis so yang
2b6: dag par rig pa bzhin brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa shin tu bstan pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la bsam gyis mi khyab par spyod pa'o//
2b7: sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi gsung dang dbyangs ni tshad med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis chos kyi dbyings thugs su chud pa ni brjod du med pa'o// sangs
2b8: rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba ni thams cad mkho par mkhyen pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis chos kyi dbyings thugs su chud cing

3a1: bstan pa na bslabs pa ma pa' mthar thag pa'o/ / kya rgyal ba'i sas/ bcu pa 'ang dgan sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams thams kyi dbyings mtha' da dbus med pa'i sangs rgyas
3a2: rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku gzugs kyi rnam par dag pa na rnyog pa med par rgyud thams cad du byung bas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
3a3: kyi chags pa med pa'i spyan ni chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi spyan mngon par sangs rgyas pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa med pa'i snyar ni 'gro ba thams cad
3a4: kyi sgra bsgribs pa med par thugs su chud pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shangs kyi skye mched ni sangs rgyas kyi mnga' thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas
3a5: mtha' dang dbus med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shangs kyi skye mched ni sangs rgyas kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ljag
3a6: shin tu yangs pa ni chos kyi dbyings thams cad dra gsung gi dbyangs rjes su 'gro bas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i chos nyid ni sems can thams cad ma lus pa
3a7: sems kyi rnam pal de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba rnam par dmigs pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku dang tha mi dad cing dus gsum chags pa meng par thugs
3a8: sa chud cing rnam par shes pa dang rnam par dag pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam par thar pa bsgrubs pa mi mnga' ba la rnam par spyod pa ni sangs rgyas kyis

3b1: 'bar dang rnam par 'phrul pa dang / cho 'phrul mi zad pa yang dag par ston pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rnam par dag pa ni brjed
3b2: du med pa'i rgyan byin kyis brlabs pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa yang dag par bstan te/ bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par dmigs par mdzad pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs
3b3: rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i khyad par dang / smon lam thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa ni rnam par rol pa'i ye shes kyi chos yongs su rdzogs te/ chos thams cad rdzogs par
3b4: byang chub par bya ba la mtha' dang dbus med pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med pa'i sangs rgyas/
3b5: kyi chos rnams so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi skad cig la ye shes mngon par bsgrubs pa yang dag par bstan pa'o// bcu gang zhe na/
3b6: skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du dga' ldan gyi gnas nas 'pho ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i che ba yongs su bstan pa
3b7: dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du mngon par 'byung ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byang chub kyi shing drung du bzhugs shing mngon par
3b8: 'tshang rgya ba yongs su bstan pa dang / / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du chos kyi 'khor lo skur ba yongs su bstan pa dang // skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du

4a1: 'dul ba'i sems can yongs su smin pa'i tshul ji lta ba bzhin du/ dus la dbab pa shes pas sangs rgyas bsnyen bkur ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams
4a2: thams cad du sems ji ltar 'dul ba'i tshul bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa brjod du med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi sku sna tshogs rnam par dmigs pa yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi
4a3: khams thams cad du/ rgyan sna tshogs dang rgyan brjod du med pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i mdzod yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig
4a4: rten gyi khams thams cad du rnam par dag pa gcig ma yin na/ thams cad yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi kham thasas na du 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs
4a5: rgyas skye ba thams cad du dbang po dang / brtson 'grus rnam pa tha dad pa byung ba dang / mos pa dang / spyod pa rnam pa tha dad pa byung ba las dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyud mngon par 'tshang rgya ba yongs su bstan pa ste/
4a6: kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi skad cig la ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa yang dag par bstan pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas
4a7: bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'da' ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mngon par 'tshang rgya ba ni/ de'i dus las mi mnga' bas dus la bab pa yin/
4a8: sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis dge ba rnam par smin pa dang / rnam par smin pa mnyam pa nyid ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems

4b1: can gyi bsapa pa yongs su smin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams lung bstan pa de de'i dus la phab pa yin/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can gyi bsam pa'i rgyud ngu/ cho 'phrul yongs su bstan pa ni de /
4b2: dus la mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yid// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can mos pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sku yongs su bstan pa de ni de'i dus las ma 'da' bas dus la bab pa yani/ sangs rgyas
4b3: bcom ldan 'das rnams btang stobs su bzhugs pa ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams yul dang / grong dang / grong rdal du gshegs pa de ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas
4b4: dus la bab pa yin/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dad pa dza lta bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can yongs su 'dzin pan/ de'i dus las pa 'da' bas dus las bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
4b5: rnams sems can kun nas nyon mongs pa dang ldan zhing gdul dka' ba la gzhan la ltos pa mi mnga' bar 'dul ba ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas
4b6: kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas/ rnam par 'phrul pa bstan pa ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
4b7: kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'da' ba'o/ / skye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dab med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa de/ bcug she na/ 'jig rten gyi
4b8: khams thams cad ma lus par skyil mo krung gcig gis rgyas par dgang ba dang / dus cig tu sangs rgyas thams cad yongs su bstan pa dang / 'od gzer gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad snang

5a1: par bya ba dang / sku gzugs gcig gis lus dang / gzugs thams cad yongs su bstan pa dang / gnas gcig na bzhugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par byed pa'i skar 'gyur/
5a2: ba dang / ye shes gcig rtogs pa sa thos thams cad la bsgribs pa med par 'gyur ba dang / thugs gcig bskyed pas chos kyi dbyings thams cad ma lus par rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi ba nyid cad
5a3: med pa dang ldan pa'i gshegs stabs gcig gis de kho na nyid yang dag par bstan pa dang / dus gsum thams cad sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang gis rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad dang ma 'dres par bzhugs
5a4: shing 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang / mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis rgyud kyi tshul gcig pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
5a5: rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dpe med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi byin kyis rlabs mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes te/ bcu gang zhe na/
5a6: 'jug pa med pa'i chos thams cad la 'jug pas/ smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / lus med pa la lus mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad mi gnyis pa la mngon par 'tshang rgya
5a7: bamangon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / sems can gyi mthar thug par bdag med pa la sems can 'dul ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad mtshan ma sna tshogs mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang /
5a8: 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul ma skyes pa la 'jig rten gyi khams 'dra ba dang / 'jig pa mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / yul thams cad mngon par 'du bya ba med pa la/ las kyi rnam par smin pa mngon par sgrub

5b1: pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad brjod du med pa la/ chos kyi dbyings su gsung mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang bas 'jug pa med pa la kun nas
5b2: nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad ma skyed pa la skye ba dang / 'jig pa'i mtshan nyid rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes te/ kye rgyal ba'i
5b3: sras bcu po de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes so/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshad med pa'i khongs su chud pa dag ste/ bcu
5b4: gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku ni dus gsum thams cad kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i khongs su chud pa yan/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can thams cad 'dul ba mdzad pa ni/
5b5: cho 'phrul chen po gsum gyi khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams tshig rab tu dbye ba thams cad la mkhas pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi gzungs thams cad kyi khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas
5b6: bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo thams cad ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i so so yang dag par rig pa bzhir khongs su chud pa yi ni/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can thams cad yongs su me tong
5b7: ba ni thugs rje chen po'i khongs su chud pa yin/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams rtag tu mnyam par gzhag pa ni dus thams cad du sems can thams cad la rnam par gzigs pa'i khams su chud pa yin/
5b8: sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba ni sems can rnam par 'dus pa thams cad khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi chags pa mi mnga' bar spyod pa ni chos kyi dbyings thams cad

6a1: khong du chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi skad cig gcig tu na 'das pa dang / ma byed pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba thabs cad khangs su chung ba yan// sangs/
6a2: rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi nyi ma gcig tu ni dus gsum gyi bskal pa'i grangs khong du chud par bstan pa thams cad khongs su chud pa yin// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
6a3: 'das rnams kyi tshad med pa'i khengs su chud pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ bdud
6a4: kyi dkrugs ma rab tu 'joms zhing rnam par 'thob pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par bka' ba'o/ / mu stegs can gzhan dang / pas kyi rgol ba tshar gcad pa ni sangs
6a5: rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par bka' ba'o/ / 'dul ba'i sems can thams cad rab tu tshim par mdzad pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par
6a6: dka' ba'o/ / sems can 'dul ba'i dbang gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gshegs pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// chos kyi dbyings thugs su chud pa'i
6a7: shes ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par skus khyab cing sangs rgyas kyi sku rnam par bye pa sna tshogs thams cad
6a8: du me gnyis pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya chen po'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// gsung gi yan lag thams cad la sems can mos par bya ba dang / thos par bya ba dang / gdul bar bya ba don yod

6b1: yod par so so yang dag par rig pa thogs pa med pas bstan pa'i tshul du so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi 'byung ba ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// sangs
6b2: rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi baspu'i bug gcig nas de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bsam gyis mi khyab cing / thogs pa med pa'i tshul du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
6b3: rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi thabs kyis 'byung zhing de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi sku'i ba spu'i bu ga thams cad nas 'byung ba ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ / de bzhin
6b4: gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdul shin tu phra ba cig la sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yongs su ston cing / sangs rgyas kyi rkyen dang rang
6b5: bzhin gyi lha ba sgrub dang / mos kyi 'khor lo skor brgyun mi 'chad cing sems can rnam par 'dul ba thogs pa med pa 'jig rten gyi khams da dag tu gtogs pa rnams la'ang mi bde ba dang / gnod pa med kyang rdul
6b6: shin tu phra ba de'ang yangs par ma byas/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag kyang chud par ma byas par ji ltar gnas pa'i chos kyi dbyings kyang thugs su chud pa'i ye shes mnga' ba ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
6b7: rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ / mun pa med pa'i khams de bzhin gshegs pas mngon par sangs rgyas te/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mun pa med cing bsgribs pa mi mnga'
6b8: la sems can pha rol gyi bsgribs pa sna tshogs kyi gnas rnam par sel na/ de la de bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang ldan pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams shin tu rgya che ba'i chos

7a1: bzod par bka' ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shan tu rgyache ba'i chos bzod par dka' bab/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag bcu pa'ang dgan/ sangs rgyas
7a2: bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba rnams thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu dag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yang dag par bsgrubs pa bdag nyid che ba ni sngon gyi mtha'
7a3: nas rnam par thams cad du kha na ma thob med cing rnam par dag pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi rgyud du rigs dang ldan par
7a4: 'byung ba'i bdag nyid che ba ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rnam par dag pas/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par she
7a5: pa la mi gnas pa ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug par gnas pas/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas
7a6: bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dus gsum la mi gnas par rnam par spyod cing chos thams cad la rten par yang dag par bcom pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams
7a7: cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dngos po rnam pa tha dad pa la rnam par gzhag pa gcig gis len pa med pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag
7a8: nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mthar chos kyi dbyings la gnas pas/ mnyam pa'i bsod

7b1: nams mi zad pa dang ldan pas mi zad pa'i bsod nams mnga' ba ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam par thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cang shin du rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
7b2: ldan 'das rnams ni sku gzugs dang kha dog mtha' yas pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na sems can 'dul ba'i dus dang dbang gis chags pa med par bzhugs pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
7b3: bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams mdu' na ma thob med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mi 'jigs pa bzhi brnyes pas bag tsha ba mi mnga' bar bzhugs shing / khyu mchog dang ser rgo
7b4: ra ro 'byin te rgol ba'i nang na stag lta bu mthu dang ldan pa la chos thams cad bstan pa la thugs sgron ma lta bu mnga' bas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu
7b5: rnam par dag pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa zhig lon yang mtshan gyi tshig thos pa tsam gyis bzhugs pa dang 'dra bar sems
7b6: na rnams kyi yon tan shin tu song zhing mya ngan las 'das nas/ de srid kyi yun ring po 'das kyang sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i yon tan zad par mi 'gyur bas// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad
7b7: kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dag na bzhugs shing 'jig rten gyi khams rgyang ring po na bzhugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams 'di
7b8: sems can rnams kyis rjes su dran par byas nas sku mngon par ston pa 'dzin pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag

8a1: ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyad cha ba na rnam pa thams cad du lan ma thob med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag pan po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shan rnam pa dag pa
8a2: ste/ bcu gang zhen// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi tshangs pa'i spyod pa rnam par dag pa la sngon gyi smin lam gyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dmas ni chags pa med pa'i tshul ma/
8a3: kyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa sel bas shin ka rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing gis shin na
8a4: par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'khor gyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rigs rnam par dag pas shin turnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na
8a5: gzugs kyi bu'i mtshan dang / dpe byad bzang po rnam par dag pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi su rnyog pa med pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thams ca
8a6: mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi phung po bsgribs pa med pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa thams cad la mthu chen po brnyes shing / pha rol tu phyin pa dam pa brnyes pas shin
8a7: rnam par dag pa yin te/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag de sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sas bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'byung zhing
8a8: dus thams cad du gnas pa ste/ bcu gang zhen/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa thob pa'i sems can rnams la ngas thams cad du sangs rgyas bstan pa dang sems can sems can shes dang ldan pa rnams la/ dus thams cad du chos bsan pa dang / sems

8b1: can sangs rgyas la dang pa'i sems dang ldan pa'i dag pa'i rtsa ba dus thams cad duskyed pa dang / rdzas kyi sbyin med par 'das pa'i sems can rnams dus thams cad du la shes khang du chud par bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad dusangs rgyas
8b2: mdzad pa dus thams cad rgyun ma 'chad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du dus thams cad du/ chags pa mi dmanga' bar gshegs pa dang / sems can thams cad la thugs rje chen pa
8b3: thams cad dum gtong ba dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi stsal pa dras thams cad du grags pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul
8b4: pa sna tshogs dus thams cad du thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos kyi dbyings gnas pa'i sangs rgyas dus thams cad 'byung ba ste// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs
8b5: rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gnas du gnas pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs
8b6: rgyas rnams kyi yeshes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'i tshul rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgras ye shes rgya mtsho ma zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
8b7: rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi phrin las tshad med pa brnyes pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi yul mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas
8b8: bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho ma zad pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi char mngon par 'bebs pas ye shes rgya mtsho

9a1: mi zad pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang legs pa mang po mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
9a2: ni sngon gyi mtha'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i smon lam dang khyad par mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni phyi ma'i mtha'i mur 'gro ba thams cad sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
9a3: rgyun mi chad par bsgrubs pas ye shes rgya mtshom zad pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na sems can gyi rigs thams cad ma lus pa'i sems dang spyod pa la ye shes rgya mtsho ma zad pa'o// sas
9a4: rgyas bcom ldan 'dis rnams ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams zil gyis minon pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
9a5: pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshul rnams dang / bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste pha rol tu phyin
9a6: pa thams cad kyis mngon par 'byung ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ / 'di lta ste chos thams cad la mi mkhyen pa gang yang mi mkha' ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
9a7: rgal yin no/ / 'di gas thams cad kyang thugs rje chen po dang ldan pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di ga sa thams cad kyang stobs bcu cad med pa dang ldan pa 'din
9a8: sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rgya yinan/ / 'di sa ste thams cad kyang than ma pa'i chol kyi 'khor po btu bskor ba na sangs rgyas bcam ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul shi'o// di sa sa thams /

9b1: kyang sems can 'dul ba la yang dag par zhugs pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste thams cad kyang 'gro ba thams cad kyi don du mngon par sangs rgyas pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan
9b2: 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ / 'di lta ste 'dul ba'i sems can rnams 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste mi gnyis par yang dag par spyod pa'i mtshan
9b3: nyid kyis chos la rab tu gzhol ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ / 'di lta ste ji ltar yong su smin par gyur pa dang / dul bar gyur pa'i sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi yul mu med
9b4: pas sangs rgyas kyi yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba ston pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi tshul yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshul lo// kye rgyal
9b5: ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgo rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi khams shin tu bstan pa'i
9b6: sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi spyod pa sna tshogs shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad
9b7: kyi las dang rnam par smin pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad la gdams dag dang man ngag shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ / sangs rgyas
9b8: bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can mtha' yas pa rnam par spyod pa'i nan tan gyi sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad la gdams dag dang man ngag gis yongs

10a1: su gzhog pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa' khyad par gyi smon lam rnam pa tha dad pas 'byung ba shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs
10a2: rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus pa'i 'du ba dang 'jig pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa ni byang
10a3: chub sems dpa'i bsam pa dang mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du 'das pa dang / ma byon
10a4: pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa ni bskal pa yangs pa de dang de dag du bstan cing brjod pa dang / yongs su bshad pas/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes thams cad khong du chud par
10a5: bya ba'i sgor mtha' yas pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgo'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dgan
10a6: sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sems can rnams la sgrub pa ste/ bcu ga shen/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rga yangs su bstan pa nisems can
10a7: lasangs rgyas kyi bran las spruHpa/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsang pa rnams can nams sa sangasargyas marnalas sgrug go/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na payang pa yang sams
10a8: can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi dran las sgrub bo/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mi mdzad pa yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub bo// sa dang rtsed me dang / rlung gas kyang sangs rgyas

10b1: bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub sa/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byin kyis rlabs kyis sa dngas dmigs pathams cad yul du mdzad pas kyang sems/
10b2: can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrini las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mtshan kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las snu ga// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni nangs
10b3: dmigs par mdzad pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub pa/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi nang rnam par dag pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas
10b4: kyi phrin las sgrub bo/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mi gsung bar bzhugs pa yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
10b5: kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sems can rnams la sgrub pa'o/ / bam tha gnyis pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'ad /
10b6: ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos te/ bcu gang she na/ smon lam chen po la rab tu brtan zhing smon lam zhig pa mi mnga' bas ji skad du gsung ba de ltar mdzad cing gnyis su ma
10b7: gsung ba 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos dang po'o/ / phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la yon tan thams cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad pas rab tu brtson 'di spyang
10b8: lug pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos gnyis pa'o/ / sems can 'dul bar 'gyur ba gcig gcig gzigs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par gshegs shang 'jig rten

11a1: gyi khams thams cad du gshegs pa la thags thogs med pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos gsum pa'o/ / zhe sdang ba'i sems can rnams la thugs rje chen pos snyoms pa dang / dang pa'i sems
11a2: can rnams la thugs rje chen pos snyoms pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bzhi pa'o/ / gang gi tshe bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzog
11a3: pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas kyi bar du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su mi 'gyur ro/ / snyam du byang chub kyi sems ma nyams pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos
11a4: lnga pa'o/ / dag pa'i rtsa ba thams cad yang dag par bsgrub cing / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su sngo bas 'jug gi/ 'jig rten pa'i rgyud lam yin pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos drug pa'o// sangs
11a5: rgyas thams cad kyi rjes su sngon sangs rgyas kyis spyad pa'i sems su las kyi las dang / ngag gi las dang / yid kyi las kyis slob cing nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi spyod pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs
11a6: su sngo ba med pas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bdun pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i sems rnam par dag cing 'od gsal ba dang / thams
11a7: cad du snang zhing kun tu 'od 'byung ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la snang zhing thams cad du snyoms pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yongs su rdzogs par byed pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos brgyad pa'o// /
11a8: 'jig rten pa'i bde ba thams cad yongs su spangs te/ 'jig rten pa'i dga' ba thams cad la ma chags pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyis gos pa med pa'i smon lam thams cad du mnyam pa nyid kyis/ 'jig rten thams

11b1: cang bde ba thams cad dang ldan par byas te/ sdug bsngal dang smos pa thams cad rab tu 'joms pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso ba'i chos dgu pa'o// sdug bsngal gyi mi bde ba thams cad nyams su bab ste/ 'gro ba thams
11b2: cad kyi don du dka' thub gyis shin tu gdungs kyang blang bar sems bskyed pas/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs kyi ngas su srung ba dang ldan pa dang / stobs bcu'i sa'i bar du sangs zas kyi yul la mos pas mthar thug pa
11b3: 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bcu pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos so// kye rgal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas
11b4: bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chags pa med pa rnams te/ / bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du gshegs pas chags pa/
11b5: mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad ni bzhugs pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
11b6: 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na bzhugs pa dang bzhengs pa dang / bzhud pa chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du chos
11b7: ston pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi dga' ldan gyi gnas na bzhugs kyang chags pa mi mnga'
11b8: bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad ni sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar byung ba'i mtha' la chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par

12a1: gad pa man/ sangs rgyas bamam ldan 'das rnams rnargyas kyi dbyings sa byas pa thams cadacas byal bar gyi dkyil 'ab na bzugs kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar spyod pa yin// sangs rgyas ba
12a2: ldan 'das rnams ni sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems dang sprod pa la gzigs shing / thugs kyi skad gcig cig la chos 'phrul chen po gsum gyis sems can rnam par 'dul yang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par
12a3: stong pa yin/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na sku gcig gis kyang tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chen por rnam par spyod kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par
12a4: spyod pa yin/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi khams 'byam klas pa ma lus pa thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos ma lus pa thams cad kyi mthar thug pa bsam gyis mi khyab par ston cing
12a5: gsung yang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chags pa med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras
12a6: bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa rnams te/ / bcu gang she na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po sna tshogs kyis rnam
12a7: par brgyan pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung yan lag gi mchog dam pa drug bcu dang ldan zhing yan
12a8: lag lnga brgya sa yongs su bzang ba dang / rgyan brgya stong du mas rab tu brgyan pa dang / dbyangs kyi yan lag mtha' yas mu med pas rnam par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi don dang tshig dang yi ge brjod du med pa'i

12b1: yang brjod du med pas rab tu tshim par mdadzad pa dang / bag chab mi mnga' bar seng ge'i ngaro chen po sgrogs pa dang / 'jigs pa med pa chen pos bstangs pa mi mnga' bar gyur pa dang / rdzas kyi dbyings ma lus pa thama?/
12b2: cad dumams thamams cadas zagasayong nga chad pa 'gyur ba dang / semasas na pasam pa pa dang / nga ya pa rnam pa sngags pa gas pa dod pas rgyas ma na
12b3: 'das rnams kyi gsung ga rgyan mchog dam pa than ma dpa'/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi srini las ni stobs bcas brtan pa sangs rgyas kyi ting 'dzizhi chen po thams cad kyi mo tog gnas rgyas pa
12b4: sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'das pa bcwo brgyad kyi rgyan kyis gan rtsa brgyan cing btubs pas chags pa med pa'i stod bral dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi gnal rab rten / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gding ma pa brnas
12b5: pa/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi rgyan du gyur pa/ dus gsum gyi chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can kun gyi sems dang spyod pa thams cad skad cig gcig dang ldan pa'i shes rab kyis rab tu
12b6: mkhyen pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dgongs pa'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'od zer bye ba brjod du med pa rab tu 'gyed par mdzad de/ 'od
12b7: zer de dag re re la yang 'od zer gyi 'khor kyi dra ba brjod du med pa dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus par byed cing 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud thams cad mun pa med par ston pa/ sangs
12b8: rgyas skye ba dang / mi 'bral bas/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las phyir mi ldog cing don yod pa/ sangs rgyas skye ba brjod du med pa rang bzhin rnam par dag cing kun tu snyoms par 'byung ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas

13a1: bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi'ang zer gyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams pa'ang ma 'dum par ston na/ zhal gyi sgo nas 'od zer kha dog sna tshogs kha dog
13a2: dra ba dang ldan pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad snang bar byed pa sems can gyi khams tshad med grags med bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnam par sbyin pa/ than med
13a3: yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur bar lung ston pa/ 'gro ba thams cad du shin tu gsal bar 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gzhad ma 'dzum pa bstan pa'i rgyan
13a4: mchog dam pa blan med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku ni tshad med pas/ bsgribs pa med pas rnam par dag pa chos thams cad chags pa med pa nyid kyis mthar thug pa mtha' dang dbus med pa'i
13a5: chos kyi dbyings la gnas pa/ 'jig rten thams cad dang ma 'dres pa 'jig rten thams cad dang 'dre ba med pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi de kho na nyid la yang dag par zhugs pa/ 'jig rten thams cad las byed du
13a6: 'phags pa/ 'jig rten thams cad las 'das pa'i chos kyis yang dag par spyod pa/ tshig gi lam dang bral ba/ brjod du med pa'i mthar phyin pa/ phung po dang khams dang / skye mched bral ba ste/ 'di ni sangasargyas
13a7: bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'od tshad med pa mnga' ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du'angam 'dris shing /
13a8: rgyan du ma dang ldan pa kha dog sa tshogs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa 'od kyi gang bkun tu thogs pa med cing / thams cad du chags pa med pa 'od kya dkyi'i 'khor bsgribs pa med pa tshad med pa'i mdzad du/

13b1: k+Shang ba/ 'a thams cad kyi 'byung gnas sa gyur pa ste// 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rgyan mchog dam pa than padapal/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na 'dag mtha'ams pam ba /
13b2: kha dag yid du 'ang ba mnga' ba'o// kha dog 'ad gsal ba mang 'a ba'o// sems can gyi khams pa lus pa thams cad kyis bsam pa dang / mos pa bzhin du rnam par dmigs pa'i bdag mang 'a ba'o// de ma yin pa'i
13b3: kha dog gzhan khams gsum du gtogs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pa'i kha dog mnga' ba'o/ / kha dog thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni kha dog blan med
13b4: mnga' ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi kha dog gyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge bas shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/ 'das pa dang ma byon par
13b5: daltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs dge ba rin po che'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa la shin tu byung ba'o/ / chos nyid kyi rnam pa thams cad du khyad par yod pa dang khyad par med pa'i spyod pas rnam par dag
13b6: pa'i rgyan gyis ye shes skye ba thams cad kyi nang du gtogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs bsgribs pa med pa'i rgyud rnam par dag pas/ 'jig rten gyi mi snyan pa thams cad kyis mi snyan par brjod du med pa ste/
13b7: 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang / rgud rnam par dag pa'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla ni med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byams pa chen po'i mthu dang rang bzhin gyi
13b8: rkyen mnga' ba ste/ shin tu dad pas yongs su rtog pa'i rnyog pa mi mnga' ba sgo'i phrin las yongs su bstsal pa lta bas mi skyo ba/ dgongs pa shin tu rnam par stsal ba thugs rje chen po mnga' za/ 'gro ba thams cad skyob pa

14a1: yon tan gyi gnas kyi dam pa bla na med pa yongs su 'dzin pa'i nang na thugs brtse ba can phan par mdzad pa sems can thams cad kyi don tu ye shes chen po byin gyis brlabs te/ bsod nams chen pos yangs
14a2: su 'phags pa 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing du gyur pa sems can rnams kyi yon tan dang / ye shes phung po thams cad rnam par 'phel bar mdzad pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
14a3: byams pa chen po dang / thugs rje chen po'i mthar thug pa'i bsod nams kyi rkyen mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyan
14a4: mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
14a5: 'das rnams ni chos thams cad la mnga' ba dang / chos thams cad snang ba mdzad pa'i mnga' sbyar bas/ tshig dang yi ge mtha' yas pa la thogs pa mi mnga' ba'i spobs pa mnga' ba dang / chos thams cad ma
14a6: lus par yongs su brjod pas mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos dang po'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems
14a7: can ji ltar yongs su smin pa dang / smon lamaji ltar btab pa'i tshul bzhin du/ 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mnga' bas mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos gnyis pa'o// sangs
14a8: rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad sems can gcig la yang gnod pa med par rnam pa drug du rab tu bskyod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgyan rnam par bkod pa grangs med tshad med pa

14b1: dang ldan pa nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' sa gtugs pa thams cad gcig nas gcig tu 'bang pa dang / gcig nas gcig tu bsdu ba dang / tsag nas gcig tu bsre bas 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan dang / gzhan dag gzhan
14b2: gyi phyogs su rab tu bzhag kyang sems can gyi khams rnams 'khor zhing rmongs par mi 'gyur la/ the tsom du mi 'gyur bar mdzad pas mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos gsum pa'o//
14b3: sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad byin gyis rlob pa'i ye shes kyis 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyan phan tshun du byin gyis brlab pa dang / dgongs pa'i skad gcig gis 'jig rten gyi
14b4: khams thams cad kyi rgyan yang dag par bstan pa dang / bskal pa grangs med par brjod kyang yi ge shin tu bstan pa zad mi shes pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad rgyan thams cad kyis rnam par brgyan pa
14b5: dang / mi mthun pa med cing nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig tu yongs su 'du bar sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa thams cad byin gyis brlabs pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas
14b6: bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' chen sgyur ba'i chos bzhi pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i sems can gzigs na sems can gcig gi don
14b7: du bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par skyil mo krung gcig gis bzhugs na yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku la mi bde ba mi mnga' 'angadi thugs la mi bde ba mi mnga' ste/ gang zag de yang mi snyel bas 'dul
14b8: ba'i dus las mi 'da' ba dang / gang zag gcig la ji ltar ba de bzhin du rim pa rim pas 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i sku tshe la mnga' bar byin gyis rlabs te bzhugs kyang /

15a1: sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la skyob mi mnga' ste/ 'di ltar sems can gyi khams thams cad mthar gyis rim pas sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i gang zag gi don du yongs su spyod pa mdzad pa la
15a2: mnga' che ba ste/ / 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos lnga pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du yang dag
15a3: par gzhol ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i bzhud pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du bzhud pa la thags thogs mi mnga' ba dang / phyogs bcu'i chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi chung /
15a4: rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa dang / phyogs kyi dri ba'i rgyud thams cad du dgongs pa'i skad cig gcig dang ldan pa'i bzhud par byin gyis rlob cing / chos kyi dbyings shin tu bstan pa khong du chud par bya bas chos kyi 'khor lo thogs
15a5: pa med pa rab tu bskor ba la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos drug pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'dul ba'i sems can gyi khams
15a6: thams cad kyi don du dgongs pa'i skad cig re re la/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bar mnga' che ba ste/ de la chos thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas pa gang yang med la/ gang mngon
15a7: par sangs rgyas pa gang yang med la/ gang mngon par sangs rgyas pa'ang med de/ mngon par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ba med kyang slob pa'i sa la gnas shing / mngon par 'tshang rgya bar yang mi brjod pa dang / sangs rgyas
15a8: kyi chos thams cad kyang bsgribs pa med par rtogs par thugs su chud pas/ sems can thams cad gdul ba'i don du ye shes tshad med pa'i tshul gyis sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa chen po'i yul yongs su rgyun

15b1: mi gcod pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' skur ba'i chos bdun pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sman gyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin
15b2: las gang bsgrub par spyan gyi snya ma med kyis yongs su grub par mdzad/ / snyun gyi snyem ched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang bsgrub pa da gangs kyi skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdza // gangs kyi skye ra
15b3: kyis sangs kyis kyi phrin las gang bsgrub pa de ljags kyi skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do/ / ljags kyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang bsgrub pa de ni sku'i skye mched kyis yongs su grang
15b4: par mdzad do/ / su'i skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang bsgrub pa de thugs kyi skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do// thugs kyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrini las bsgrub pa de 'jig rten gyi
15b5: khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi dmigs pa 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa sna tshogs rnam par phye ba thams cad grub par mdzad do// de bzhin du dmigs pa thams cad re re la yang snrel bzhir
15b6: bsgrub pas sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mda' chen pos mnga' skur ba'i chos brgyad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rang
15b7: gau sku'i ba spu'i phrag gcig gi nang du sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad gzung bar mdzad cing khongs su chud par mdzad pa dang / sems can re re zhing yang lus sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa tsam du
15b8: yangs par med pa kyang sems can de dag la gnod pa dang mi 'gyur ba dang / de dag du yang sems can re re zhing 'jig rten gyi khams gcig tu brgyud pas bskal pa grangs med pa zad par gnas par bya ba dang / 'jig

16a1: rten gyi khams grangs med par dgom pa gcig gis byin pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag du sangs rgyas byung ba rnams kyi spyan sngar 'gro bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas de dag blang ba'i tshe bar
16a2: brjod du med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgud dang / gleng de dag na sems can gyi gtso bo brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar bya ba dang / ba spu'i bu gdenas sangs rgyas gcig nas
16a3: gcig tu brgyud pas brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa 'byung bar bya ba dang / sems can gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa 'byung bar bya ba dang / chos kyi 'khor lo gcig nas gcig tu brgyad pa
16a4: brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa bskor bar bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings bstan pa gcig nas gcig tu rgyud pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa shin tu bstan par bya ba dang / 'das pa gcig nas
16a5: gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa dang / ma 'ongs pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjed du med pa dang / de ltar byung ba'i gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa yongs su brjod par bya ba dang /
16a6: nam mkha'i dbyings mtha' dang dbus med par bstan pa kun tu mtshams med par sems can thams cad 'ong zhing 'gro ba dang / skye ba'i skye mched thams cad du 'dod pa'i longs spyod rgya chen po bgegs med pa
16a7: thams cad 'byung bar bya ba la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos dgu pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi
16a8: d byings ma lus pa thams cad pad mo'i rgyan pa'i seng ge'i khri pad mo'i snying po can la de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa thams cad du khyab pa'i skus byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs

16b1: rgyas te/ / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongs su bstan par mdzad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi/ jig par 'dzag rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba sad kyi sems cad gyi/
16b2: gtso bo thams cad kyang de bzhin du dgongs pa skad cig ma re re'i byin gyis rlabs kyis brlabs pa dang / dgengs pa skad cig la ji lta ba de bzhin du dgongs pa skad cig ma thams cad la yang / pad mo'i rgyud kyis yongs su
16b3: dag par mngon par 'tshang rgya bar bya ba dang / de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings thams cad ma lus pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa rnam par dag pa/ rgyad sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams su dmigs pa
16b4: rnam pa sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i zhing rnam par dag pa 'byam klas pa/ brjod du med pa mtshan nyid tha dad pa rnam pa tha dad pa'i rgyud tsha de med cing 'byam klas pa/ dus kyi rgyud grangs med pa dang ldan pa/ bstan pa ma 'dras
16b5: pa dang ldan pa/ blo tshad med pa dang mos pa shin tu yangs pa dang ldan pa/ mtshan nyid sna tshogs kyi gnas med pa/ mtshan nyid bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa/ tshad med pa thams cad dgongs pa skad cig ma las
16b6: dgongs pa skad gcig ma gcig gse thams cad yongs su bstan kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ched du bsgrub pa mi mdzad pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas
16b7: kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos bcu pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag gi sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi ba 'a chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos so// kye rgyal ba'i sras
16b8: bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su rdzogs pa tshad med pa bsam gyis ma khyab pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ mtshan re re zhing bsod napas brgya pa'i mtshan

17a1: yongs su dag par 'gyur ba 'di ni yongs su rdzogs pa dang po ste/ des sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu bangon par 'tshang rgya'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams yongs su rdzogs pas
17a2: sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dpas byang chub tu bangon par 'ar gyig/ / dge pa'i tsha pathams cad yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu ba dpa 'chang rgyag/ phan ta thams
17a3: Sh+Ta gnas pa ma gas pa'i stong pa yangs thadag pa yongasas rdzogs pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldad das rnams byang chub tu bangon par 'dzang tsag/ sems can yangs su sun par bya ba dang / #
17a4: ba yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'chang rgya'o/ / sangs rgyas kyi mda' 'gro ba thams cad kyis zil gyis minon pa/ yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
17a5: rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'dang u0f7fga/ nang yongs su dag par bya ba yongs su rdzogs par sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu bangan par 'chang rgyag/ thams cad mkhyen pa chags
17a6: yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ / mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang gzugs kyi sku blta ba don yod pa yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan
17a7: 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya ste/ sangs rgyas kyi brid las
17a8: yongs su rdzogs par mdzad nas yongs su mya ngan las 'da'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su rdzogs pa tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab

17b1: pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thabs mkhas pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos thams cad byin gyis brlabs pa med cing spros
17b2: pa thams cad med par yang thugs su chung la/ dge ba'i sgo nas sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyang shin tu stod cing brjod de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa dang po'o//
17b3: sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad la gzigs pa med cing phan tshun du mkhyen pa med de// ma bcings ma grol ba dang gzung ba med cing bstsags pa med de/ yongs su rdzogs pa med par
17b4: yang thugs su chud la sangs rgyas kyis chos thams cad la mnga' dam pa'ang brnyes te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos thams cad la ma 'a skur ba de yang / yang dag pa de khon nyid pan ba rnam pa
17b5: gzhan du mi 'gyur ba dang / chos thams cad bdag gi med cing yongs su 'dzin pa med la de kho na nyid kyi mtha' las rnam par mi 'da' yang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mnga' chen pos chos kyi
17b6: dbyings thams cad snang ba la yang / rab tu mkhyen pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi/ sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa gnyis pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mtshan ma'i
17b7: mtha' thams cad mi mnga' ste/ mtshan ma thams cad dang mi 'grogs shing / mtshan ma'i mngon par shes pa thams cad dang ma 'dres la de'i rang bzhin du de banyid med pa dang / ji ltar ngo banyid med pa'i sgrar
17b8: tshul thams cad thugs su chud pas kyang gzugs kyi mtshan ma'i sku gzugs rnam par dag pa grangs med pa dang / zhing gi mtshan ma dang rnam par spyod pa'i mtshan ma zad mi shes pa rnam pa sna tshogs yang dag par

18a1: bstan cing bshad pa'i ye shes kyi phung po mun pa med pa 'gro ba thams cad kyi sgron ma chen por gyur pas/ mun pa med pa'i snang ba ston pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi
18a2: thabs mkhas pa gsum pa'o/ / chags pa med pa'i mtha' ni sngon gyi mtha' yang ma yin/ phyi ma'i mtha' yang ma yin/ da ltar byung ba yang ma yin te/ chos kyi dbyings su gnas pa ni 'das pa 'am/ ma 'ongs pa dang /
18a3: da ltar byung ba yang ma yin pas de bzhin nyid kyis mtshan nyid kyis 'byung ba med kyang / sangs rgyas 'byung ba rnams kyi rigs tshad med pa'i phyir shin tu bstan pa brjod du med pas 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang
18a4: ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba yang rab tu brjod cing kun tu gzigs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi yul gyis de bzhin du gzigs pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas
18a5: pa bzhi pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku'i phrin las dang gsung gi phrin las dang / thugs kyi phrin las kyis mngon par 'du mdzad pa yang mi mnga' la/ yongs su blang ba mi mnga' bas
18a6: bzhugs shing / rnam par phye ba med pa'i mthar thug pa ste/ dor ba med pa'i chos kyi gnas kyi pha rol tu phyin la/ bgrang ba'i tshul las rnam par 'das kyang tshul nges pa med pa'i mdzod du gyur cing / bkra
18a7: dang mngon par bsgrub pa mtha' yas pa dang / 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa rnam pa sna tshogs tha dad pa'i grangs gi tshul thugs su chud pa ye shes bsgribs pa med pas gzigs pa rnams te/
18a8: chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi/ sems can gdul ba rnam par dmigs pa la/ rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs tshad med bu med par mngon par bsgrub pa mdzad pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thabs

18b1: mkhas pa lnga pa'o/ / chos thams cad lta ba med pas tha mi dad pa dang bye brag med pa dang / 'byung ba med pa dang mtshan nyid med pa dang / sna tshogs med pa dang / blang ba med pa dang / dor ba med pa dang / rang bzhin
18b2: med par rab tu mkhyen kyang / chos kyi mun gan drangs pa yang dag par bsgrub cing / 'jig rten gyi tshul dang 'gal ba ma pa dang / rang bzhin med pa yang dag par gzigs pas thams cad mkhyen pa/
18b3: thams cad gzigs pa/ mkhyen par bya ba thams cad ma lus par gzigs par chos la mnga' sgyur ba thams cad kyang rab tu ston la/ de bzhin nyid kyi rang bzhin las kyang mi nyam pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom
18b4: ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa drug pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs su chud pa'i rnam pa gcig gis gzhan dang gzhan mkhyen par bya ba chos de'i skyon med pa las rnam
18b5: par 'das pa gnas med pa dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par dag pa mnyam pa nyid kyi chos skyon med pas/ dus thams cad du gnas pa rab tu mkhyen te/ de la yang nyi ma gcig gam/ zla ba phyed dam/ le cig gam/ lo
18b6: brgya'am/ bskal pa cig pa dang / 'du bas rjes su bsnyag pa dang / phyir phyogs pa mi mnga' bar dus tshad med pa dang / nyi ma gcig dang / yud tsam gcig gi dus dang snga dro nas nyi ma bya'i dus dang / phyi
18b7: dro nas snga dro'i dus dang / nyi ma gung nas phyi dro'i dus dang / nyi ma bgrangs pa'i dus dang / nyi ma bdun dang / zla ba phyed kyi dus dang / zla ba dang / lo dang / lo brgya'i dus dang bskal pa gcig gyi dus dang / tshad
18b8: med grangs med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dus nas/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i dus su chos bstan pa dang / chos kyi 'khor lo thogs pa med cing phyir mi ldog/ rgun 'chad par mi 'gyur/ bral bar mi 'gyur/

19a1: par chad par mi 'gyur/ med par mi 'gyur/ 'jig par mi 'gyur g.yo bar mi 'gyur/ ring du mi 'gyur/ 'khor de la gnas pa nyid du yang rgyun 'chad par mi 'gyur te/ 'din sangs rgyas
19a2: bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bdun pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du rtag tu dus la bab par bzhugs pa ste/ sangs rgyas
19a3: bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mi 'jigs pa tshad med mnga' ba'o/ / so so yang dag par reg pa grangs med pa mnga' ba'o// so so yang dag par rig pa tshad med par mnga' ba'o// so so yang dag par rig pa
19a4: zad pa mi shes pa mnga' ba'o/ / so so yang dag par rig pa thogs pa med pa mnga' ba'o// so so yang dag par rig pa mtha' yas pa mnga' ba'o// thun mong ma yin pa'i so so yang dag par rig pa mnga' ba'o//
19a5: so so yang dag par rig pa mthar thug pa med pa mnga' ba'o// so so yang dag par rig pa de khon dang ldan pa mnga' ba'o// so so yang dag par rig pa tshig gi tshul thams cad rab tu rtogs pa mnga' ba'o// chos thams cad so so
19a6: yang dag par rig pa mnga' ba'o/ / bsam pa dang mos pa dang dbang po ji lta ba bzhin du chos kyi tshul dang nam grangs tshul ji ltar rnam par bkod pa bzhin du sa 'tshams med par ston te/ mdo sde bye ba khrag khrig brjod du med
19a7: pa'i yang brjod du med pa rnams mdo sde de dang de la thog ma dang dbus gi tshul gyis yang dag par ston to/ / 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa brgyad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
19a8: ldan 'das rnams ni meng med kyang ming dang rigs su byung ba'i chos thams cad tshig dang yi ges shin tu dbyangs mngon par sangs rgyas pa ste/ ming 'das pa ma yin pa dang / mde ma 'ongs pa ma yin pa dang / ming

19b1: dkyur blang ba ma yin pa dang / mngasams can pa ya pa dang / bang ni ma yin pa dang / mang yin bayin pa dang / ming byang bas ngas pa' ma yi pa dang / ma ma
19b2: yin pa dang / pade grangs med pa ma yin pa dang / ming skye ba ma yin pa dang / ming 'gag pa ma yin pa dang / ming med pa ma yin pa dang / mang yod pa ma yid pa dang / mang gcig sa pa yin pa dang / pang tha dad pa ma yin pa dang /
19b3: ma thams cad ma yin pa dang / chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis brjod du med pa dang / phyogs med pa dang brda' med pa dang / tshig gi lam med pa sgra dang bral ba dang / sgrab rnam pa thams cad mi 'byung ba/ yongs su
19b4: bsgrubs pa med pa/ byas pa dang rnam par byas pa med pa rnam pa gcig ma yin pa/ rnam pa mang po ma yin pa yang thugs su chud la/ brjod pa dang spyod pa thams cad la yang pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog brnyes pa dag
19b5: ste/ rnam par rtog pa'i yul mi mnga' ba dag go// mngon par 'du mdzad pa med pa la rab tu brtson pa dag go// rtog pa dang kun tu rtog pa yang yongs su rtog pa 'gags pa dag go// spyod pa thams cad la mi gnas
19b6: par spyod pa dag ste/ 'din sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams cad kyi gzugs pa skyes pa rab tu mkhyen pa
19b7: tshor ba'i spros pa med pa dang / 'du shes kyi grangs med pa dang / 'dra byed kun tu chub med pa dang / rnam par shes pa nye bar len pa med pa dang / rang bzhin sa dpe rab tu mkhyen te/ chos thams cad skye mched kye rgyud mer
19b8: pa dang / khams rnams me dmigs pa dang / chos thams cad mi 'jigs pa dang / chos thams cad bskyed du med cing / rang bzhin gyis nam mkha' lta ba dang / chos thams cad dben pa dang / las bed pa dang / rnam

20a1: par smin pa med pa dang / spyod pas 'byung ba med pa dang / ma grub pa dang / ma byung ba dang / grangs kyis mi brjod pa dang yod pa ma yin pa dang / ma skem pa dang ma 'gags pa dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa
20a2: med pa dang / rnam par byang ba med pa dang / skye ba med pa dang gnas pa med pa dang / yongs su gnas pa med pa dang / yongs su smin par byas pa dang / rnam par gtum pa med pa dang / sems can med pa dang / sems can med pa
20a3: ma yin pa dang / srog med pa dang / srog med pa ma yin pa dang / rkyen med pa dang / rkyen med pa sa yin pa dang / rten pa med pa dang / rten med pa ma yin par chos thams cad thugs su chud kyang chos kyi dbyings thams
20a4: cad shin tu bstan pal pha rol tu phyin pa'i dam pa brnyes pa dag ste/ nges pa dang ma nges pa dang / log par nges pa'i phung po gsum rnam par dgod pa rnams la stobs bcus thugs su chud pa'i ye shes mi 'jigs pa badz+ra
20a5: nam par dag pa'i sangs rgyas kyi yul chen pa dang ldan pas seng ge'i sgra srog pa 'din sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bcu ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcwa pa da dag nas
20a6: bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa'o/ / / shan tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo sangs rgyas rmad gcad ces bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo// bam po gsum pa/
20a7: rgyal ba'i sras bcwa bang dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi marnalas rgya chen po tshad med pa bsas kyis mi khyab pa rnams te/ de dag na sangs rgyas kyi can gyirlabasas gnas
20a8: mapa tan dang / da / mas pa dang / dag nga man sa dang / rangs mas mas cad kyi 'jug #// pag/ gsas

20b1: dbyings kyi mtha' sa gtugs pa'i chas kyi dbyings thams cad 'jig rten khams ma lus pa thams cad du dga' ldan du skye ba bstan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mu med pa dag la sangs rgyas kyi phrin pas
20b2: mdzad de/ bdog tshad med pa gzi brjid tshad med pa snang ba tshad med pa/ dbyangs tshad med pa dbyangs kyi yan lag rnam par dag pa tshad med pa gsung brjod pas rnam par migs pa tshad med pa/ ting nge 'dzin chad med
20b3: pa la spyad pa/ shes rab dang ye shes kyi yul tshad med pa mad ba'i rnams lnga dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten la phan 'dogs pa mdzad de/ bdud dang bcas pa tshangs pa dang bcas pa/ dge sbyong dang bcas pa/ bram ze'i skye
20b4: dgu dang bcas pa/ lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// byams pa chen po'i spyod yul thogs pa med pa dang / thabs thugs rje chen po'i sgo'i mthar thugs pas sems
20b5: can la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do/ / bsod nams kyi stobs dang / mnga' phun sum tshogs pa dang / dbang po rnam par sbyangs pa dang / cang shes kyi sems yongs su dag pas kyang sems can rnams la phan
20b6: bdags par mdzad do/ / theg pa sna tshogs rnam par dag pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// theg pa chen po yongs su rdzogs par bya bas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do//
20b7: 'gro ba thams cad gnon pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las dang po'o// dga' ldan gyi pho brang nas 'phos pa med kyang
20b8: yum gyi skur gshegs shing / byang chub sems dpa'i sku tham skye bar ston pa/ sbru ma lta bur yongs su spyod pa/ sprul pa lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gyi mthar thug pa/ mag yong la bur rnam par dmigs pa/ rnam

21a1: mkha'i yul tshad med par khyab pa/ bzhed pa bzhin du skye ba yang chags pa mi mnga' ba smig smra ba lta bur bstan pa/ nyon mongs pa med pa'i chos la yang dag par gzhol ba/ gnas med pa'i ye shes
21a2: laganas pa/ rang bzhin gyis 'dod chags dang bral bas rnam par dag pa/ rgyan shin tu rgya che ba'i mdzod kyis sangs rgyas kyi bran las mdzad do// khang pa brtsegs pa rin po che las byas pa'i pho brang chen po rin po che'i rgyan
21a3: mang po dang ldan pa na bzhugs pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ / rdzu 'phrul gyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// yid la bya ba'i byin gyi rlabs chen pos kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrini las mdzad do// nas
21a4: par 'phrul pa'i mdzod chen po yang dag par bstan pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ / ye shes kyi nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen pos kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrini las mdzad do// yum sku skyed pa'i sku na bzhum/
21a5: pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi spyod yul chen po brnyes pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis 'jig rten byin gyis brlabs pa mtha' yas
21a6: pas sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ / ting nge 'dzin chen po grangs med pa la rnam par spyod cing / snyoms par 'jug pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// ting nge 'dzin las bzhengs pa de dang de dag
21a7: kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ / spyod pa'i thog ma la yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po'i mthar thug pa'i bar du thog ma dang dbus dang tha ma'i tshul gyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sa 'dil
21a8: gnyis su med pas thams cad mthar phyin par byas nas tha mar 'jig rten gyi grangs kyis skye ba yongs su ston te/ skye bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi bran las mdzad do// gzhon nur gyur pas

21b1: da ya / na A du/ sa
21b2: cad du sangs rgyas kyi srid las mdzad do/ / mngon par 'tshang rgyabs kyang 'jig rten thams cad nga sangs rgyas kyi phrini las mdzad do// ris kyi 'khong la bas bas kyang 'jig ted thams cad du sangs
21b3: rgyas kyi bre las mdzad do/ / babs mkhas pa sna tshogs kyis kyang 'jig rten sna tshogs 'jig rten med medang/ 'jig rted kun byam par yas pa phyogs kyang ba'i d+had dang / ras thams dadakyi 'jig rten pa'as
21b4: pa thabs cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ / zhing gi rgyud ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// las kyi rnam par smin pa ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi phrin
21b5: las mdzad do/ / sems can gyi rgyud ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// skye ba dang sha 'phos pa'i drud ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sprul pa chen po'i rgyur/
21b6: dang / sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang / chos dran pa'i sgo'i 'khor los kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gnyis pa'o// dge bar spyod
21b7: pa'i las rnam par dag cing gdung rabs thams cad du ye shes kyi tshul rnam par dag pas/ sku tshe'i rgyud kyi tshul dang ldan pa sems can thams cad gdul ba thugs su chud pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs
21b8: su rdzogs par mdzad do/ / btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang du bzhugs pa ston kyang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba'i tshul gyis gnas la bzhugs pa rnams sgra dang / tshig thams cad dang bral bar

22a1: btags pas/ dang ma pa thams cad dngas po med pa las byung bang kheng sangan pa bya ba dang / dngas pa thams cad gas pa la gnang bar bya ba dang / tshul khrims thams dmakhyen pa nyid kyimathapa
22a2: par yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / snying rje chen pos bgro ba mu med pa la rnam par blta bar bya ba dang / byams pa chen pos sems can med pa'i yul la rab tu rtog par bya ba dang / dga' ba chen pos 'jig rten gyi brjod du/
22a3: med par khong du chud par bya ba dang / btang snyoms chen pos sems la dbang sgrub la gnas par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan gyis rang yongs su rgyas par byed par bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi lus/
22a4: ma lus par mngon par bsgrub par bya ba dang / thams cad du gnas med pa'i lus yongs su rdzogs par byed par bya ba dang / 'khor thams cad rnam par dag par nan tan tu byed par bya ba dang / chos bstan pa rnam
22a5: par rjod pa rab tu brjod par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi dngos po la smod par bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi nyes pa la rtog par bya ba mdzad cing spyod pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa bas rnam par smin pa yang dag par bstan pa dang /
22a6: ji ltar bkod pa'i tshul du sems can gdul ba dang / yongs su ma smin pa'i sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang / yongs su smin pa'i rnams tshul bzhin du gdul ba dang / grangs med pa'i thabs mkhas pa mngon par
22a7: bslab pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las phyir mi ldog pa yongs su bstan pa dang / sgo sna tshogs pa nas chos kyi spyod pa rab tu brjod pa dang / sems can rnams kyi bsam pa sna tshogs par rnam par sbyad pa dang /
22a8: thugs rje chen po las byung ba'i chos kyi sman gyis mngon par spang ba dang / thams cad la skyob pa'i byams pa chen po bskyed pa'i cho 'phrul gsum gyis yongs su brlan pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad mngon pa dang /

22b1: rnam par dmigs par btsun ma'i 'khor gyi nang du bstan pa yan chad du 'jig na mtha' dang dbus med par sangs rgyas kyi phrin las yongs su bstan pa mdzad cing / ye shes kyi mthu chen po thegs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi
22b2: mngon par mkhyen pa bsgribs pa med pa bsgrubs pa dang / chos rnam pa gsum gyi thabs mkhas pa dang ldan pa'i bran las kyi mtha' dang / sru'i phrin las kyi mtha' shin tu rnam par dag pa dang / gsung gi phrini pas ye shes nyams
22b3: pa med pas rnam par dag pa dang / thugs kyi phrin las kyi mtha' zab cing chags pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i thabs la mkhas pas sems can rnams kyi don mdzad de 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi
22b4: brani las gsum pa'o/ / rnam par rgyal ba chen po mnga' ba rnams ni btsun mo'i 'khor rgyan rnam par phye ba tshad med pa dang ldan pa yid du 'ong ba spangs te/ mngon par 'byung ba'i spyod pa yongs su bstan pas sems can
22b5: rnams 'jig rten gyi gnas las skyod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi mngon par zhen pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'jig rten du gtogs pa thams cad mi rtag par shes par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi tshul la mngon par zhen sa
22b6: rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'jig rten gyi dga' ba la sred pa yongs su gcad pa dang / 'jig rten gyi nyon mongs pa byang zhing nub pa la yang dag par spyod par bya ba dang / sems can gyi don rjes su dran par bya ba'i phyir/
22b7: mngon par 'byung ba'i don pa rab tu gzhol ba dang / khyam pa'i tshul yongs su spang bstan pa dang / nyon mongs pa med pa'i chos kyi sbyor ba la yang dag par gnas par bya ba dang / sngon gyi smon lam yongs su rdzogs
22b8: par bya ba dang / yon tan gyi dkyil 'khor tshad med pa yongs su snang bar bya ba dang / ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor chen po brnyes pas sems can rnams kyi mi shes pa'i sgrib pa rab tu bstsal ba dang / bdag nyid bsod nams

23a1: kye nang blan med par gyur bar 'gro ba thams cad la bstan pa dang / dag pa'i rtsa ba thams cad sangs rgyas la bskyed pa' dag pa'i rtsa ba'i nang du 'dus par 'gro ba thams cad la yang dag par brjod pa dang //
23a2: bdag nyid kyis ye shes kyi don gzigs par bstan pa dang / sems can rnam rnam par dag pa'i sgor brjod pa dang / sems can rnams kha na ma tho ba med pa'i sgor bsgrub pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad du 'byung ba'i
23a3: sgo rab tu bstan pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rgyal mtshan yang dag par bskyed pa mdzad cing mngon par 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi phrin las bzhi pa'o// don gcig ma yin pa mkhyen pa
23a4: pa dang ldan pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi mthar thug pa rnams ni chos thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya bar bya'o zhes byang chub kyi shing drung du byon te/ byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bas kyang bdud kyi dpung thams
23a5: cad rab tu gzhom pa dang / sku'i byin gyi brlabs kyi mdzod kyis chos kyi dbyings kyi ma lus pa thams cad du rgyas par dgang ba'i phyir byan gyi rlabs zad mi shes pa'i mthar thug pas mtha' rnam par spangs pa spyod pa tshad
23a6: med pa rab tu brnyes pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i yul gyis rnam par rol pa'i ye shes kyi don dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan yang dag par bsgrub pa yongs su rdzogs pa 'jig rten gyis khams ma lus pa thams
23a7: cad du gdan rnam par bkram pas yongs su rgyas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing ma lus pa thams cad du byang chub sems dpas rnam par dmigs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dam pa thob pa rnams kyis zhal du blta ba/ byang chub
23a8: sems dpa' thams cad kyi rnam pa dang / smon lam khyad par can dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyis yang dag par bsam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo zab mo rab tu skor ba/ sangs rgyas kyi

23b1: yul tshad med pa brtsams pa/ byang chub sems dpa' brjod du med pa'i babyung gnas su gyur pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa sna tshogs spyod pa la yang dag par gzhol pa'i byang chub sems dpa' 'khor gyi dkyil
23b2: 'khor rnam par dag pa mnga' ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis byini du brlob pa'i yul mnga' ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa'i sems can gyis rnam par dmigs pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams
23b3: cad tha mi dad pa dang ldan pa 'byung ba'i sa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mtha' yas pa'i mthu'i gnas la yon tan gyi khyad par thams cad rab tu brnyes nas bzhugs pa/ 'jig rten gyi rnam pa thams cad ma lus
23b4: pa'i mthar thug pa/ sems can gyi rnam pa thams cad dang / zhig gi rnam pa thams cad dang / chos kyi rnam pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam pa thams cad dang / yongs su smin par bya ba'i rnam
23b5: pa thams cad dang / dus kyi rnam pa thams cad dang / gdul ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul ba'i rnam pa thams cad ma lus pa'i mthar thug pa'i rnams 'gro ba ma lus pa thams
23b6: cad du mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par 'tshang rgya bas sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi pra ni las lnga pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
23b7: kyi chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba mdzad pa'i phyir mi ldog pa'i tshul gyis phyir mi ldog pa'i 'khor lo dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyis khong du chud par 'gyur ba'i tshul gyis tshad med pa'i 'khor lo dang / mi 'jigs pa'i
23b8: seng ge'i nga ro chen po'i tshul gyis thams cad ma lus par mngon par sangs rgyas pa'i 'khor lo dang / chos kyi mdzod mu med pa'i sgos snang bar byed pa'i tshul gyis chos thams cad mkhyen pa'i mdzod kyi 'khor lo dang

24a1: ye shes nam mkha'i dbyangs ltar tshad med pa'i tshul gyis chags pa med pa'i 'khor lo dang / chos thams cad kyi dngos po med pa'i rang bzhin rab tu rtogs par bya ba'i tshul gyis bsgribs pa med pa'i
24a2: 'khor lo dang / sems can thams cad kyi chos kyi mge rnam par spyad pa'i tshul gyis 'jig rten thams cad kyi ston ma'i 'khor lo dang / 'jig rten thams cad du rgyas par 'gengs pa'i tshul gyi sa thams cad mkhyen
24a3: pa'i chos brjod pa'i 'khor lo dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad dang mi 'gal ba'i tshul gyis sangs rgyas thams cad 'dab 'dres par gyur pa'i 'khor lo dang / de dag la sogs pa rnam pa bye ba khrag khrigasargya
24a4: gong du/ chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas sems can thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa'i rnam pa la/ chos kyi 'khor lo skor te/ de ltar chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas
24a5: kyi phrin las bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las drug pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni grong dang grong khyer dang grong rdal dang /
24a6: rgyal po'i gnas su gshegs pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi brani las mdzad de/ mi'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / lha'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / klu'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po'i gnas dang
24a7: dra ze'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / lha ma yin gyi rgyal po'i gnas dang / nam mkha' lding gi rgyal po'i gnas dang / mi'am ci'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / lto 'phye chen po'i gnas dang / srin po'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / sha zer
24a8: rgyal po'i gnas dag tu gshegs pas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ 'di lta ste/ grong khyer gyi sgor byon nas g.yo ba dang / 'od gzer snang ba dang / long ba rnams mig 'thob pa

24b1: dang / 'on pa rnams sgra thos par 'gyur ba dang / smos pa rnams dran pa thob par 'gyur ba dang / gos med pa rnams gos thob par 'gyur ba dang / sdug bsngal ba rnams bde ba 'thob pa dang / rol mo'i cha spyad ma dkrol ma brdungs
24b2: par sgra yad du 'ong ba rang 'byin pa dang / rgyan stod na 'dug pa dang / gnas nas ma phog pa dang / ma bskyod ma dkrol bar bskyod cing dkrol ba'i sgra 'byung ba dang / bya sna tshogs mang po'i sgra skad yid du 'ong ba 'byung ba dang / bldan
24b3: gtang mi bri zhing mi 'thun pa med pa'i sku mthong ras kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// mtshan dang dpe' byad bzang po bstan pas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
24b4: sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrini las mdzad de/ yongs su gzigs pa dang / rnam par gzigs pa dang / brkyang ba dang / bskum pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do//
24b5: gshegs pa dang slar bzhud pa dang / bzhengs pa dang / chags pa dang / bzhugs pa dang / gzims pas kyang sems can la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// chos bstan pa dang / mi gsung
24b6: bzhugs pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ / rdzu 'phrul gyi tshe 'phrul dang / yongs su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul dang / rjes su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul gyis kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan
24b7: 'das rnams 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul sems can bsam pa sna tshogs rgya mtsho dang ldan pa 'jig rten gyi spyod pa thams cad rgyu zhing 'byung ba dang ldan pa dge ba'i rtsa ba chen pos shin tu brtan pa/ sangs rgyas rjes su
24b8: dran pa dang ldan pa/ sngon 'grogs 'grogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' dang gnas pa'i sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams ni sku gzugs pa

25a1: nam khams pa'o zhes bya bar gzhol ba dang / sangs rgyas rnams skye bar bkon na zhes bya bar yid ches par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mthong dang / dbazhin gshegs pa'i gsung thab pan ras/
25a2: nams kyi chos dkar po'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa'o// zhes sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa yid la byed pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad rnam par dag pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa skye ba yin no zhes bya bar khong du chud par byed pa dang /
25a3: sangs rgyas kyi yon tan bsngags pa ni mtha' yas pa'o zhes bya bar yang dag par lta ba dang / mabyon pa'i sangs rgyas 'byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs yang dag par bsgrub pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba dang mos pa'i
25a4: tshul thams cad kyis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mnyes par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams ni yon tan mtha' yas pa'o zhes khong du chud par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni sems can
25a5: thams cad mngon tu gyur par rtog pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni sems can gyi rasi bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gnas su gyur par sems pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni zhing thams cad na snang bar khong du chud pa dang
