25a6: de lta bu'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad 'byung bas 'jig rten thams cad na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ / dad par bya ba dang / phyag bya ba dang /
25a7: thal mo sbyar bar byas pa dang / rjes su bston pa dang / spyan drangs pa dang / mchod pa dang / mngon du mthong ba dang 'dzum pa bya ba dang / sangs rgyas la dga' ba'i sems kyis mos par bya ba'i dge ba'i
25a8: ba'i sgo nas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ / sangs rgyas rjes su dran par gyur pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams

25b1: ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ / sangs rgyas mthong bar 'dod par byas pas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las brjod do//
25b2: de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku kha dog dang dbyibs kyi rnam pa tshad med pa bstan pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i
25b3: gsung thob par bya bas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ de dag la stsogs pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
25b4: rnam pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa dag/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / mthu dang 'dul ba ji lta ba'i tshul las mi 'da' bar 'gyur ro// de ltar
25b5: sangs rgyas kyi phrin las 'jig rten thams cad kyi sems cad kun gyi sems dang spyod pa dang bsam pa la gnas/ dge ba rgya che ba tshad med pa dag phyir mi ldog pa'i yul dang / snying rje chen pos rab tu bskul ba dang /
25b6: sngon gyi smon lam gyis yongs su skyo ba med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mkhyen pa'i stobs dang / shugs kyis 'jig rten thams cad 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs
25b7: rgyas kyi phrin las bdun po'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dgon pa la bzhugs sems zhi bar bzhugs sam/ dben par bzhugs sam/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa la bzhugs sam/ ting nge
25b8: 'dzin chen po'i gnas la bzhugs sam/ gcig pu dgyes par bzhugs sam/ sku mi snang bar bzhugs sam/ ye shes zab mo'i gnas la bzhugs sam/ sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi stobs tshad med pa la bzhugs sam/

26a1: sku'i yongs su spyod pa mi mthong bar bzhugs kyang rung ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas/ phran las gzhan gyis mtshugs pa'i ye shes dang / smarnalapa kyi yul byas pas pa can/
26a2: du 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la rgyun mi 'chad par 'byung ste/ sangs rgyas lha yongs su tshol bas kyang / sangs rgyas kyi phrini las rgyun mi 'chad do// sangs rgyas klu yongs su tshol bas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
26a3: dz+nyAn mi bcad do/ / sangs rgyas gdod spyan yongs su tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas pa'am ni yongs su tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas s+ho 'byichen pa yongs su tshal pa dang / sangs rgyas phran pa yongs sa rtsol pa dang / sangs cas
26a4: bdang ma ma yin pa yin pa yongs su rgyal ba dang / sangs rgyas nyan thos dang / sangs rgyas rang sangs rgyas dang / sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' yongs su tshol bas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun pa 'chad
26a5: do/ / chos ston pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do// sangs rgyas gcig brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrini las rgyun mi 'chad do// sangs rgyas thams cad brjod pas kya
26a6: sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do/ / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i khyad par dang / smon lam thams cad gcig tu brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrani las rgyun mi 'chad do// byang chub sems dpa'i snod/
26a7: pa gcig rnam par bya ste/ spyod pa tha dad pa brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do// 'jig rten gyi yul sangs rgyas kyi yul du bzod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi brani las rgyun pa'ang do// sangs
26a8: rgyas kyi yul 'jig rten gyi yul dri brjid pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun pa 'thad do/ / yul ma yin pa sangs rgyas kyi yul du brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las nanas 'chad do// nyan mtshar dang

26b1: tha ba ya ra kham mar kham dang / zla ba dang / lo bsgrangs par bzhugs pa dang / yongs su bzhugs pa nas/ de bzhin du bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa 'bar du bzhugs pa dang / yongs su bzhugs pas
26b2: kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ / 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi phrin las brgyad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na
26b3: dag pa'i rtsa ba rnams la 'byung gnas lta bu/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa kun la rnam par spyod pa lta bu/ sangs rgyas rnams la dad pa lta bu/ sems khong du chud par bya ba la shin tu mos pa lta bu/ dbang
26b4: rnams la bsgrub pa lta bu/ sems can skye dgu thams cad la 'dul ba lta bu/ 'gro ba thams cad la mos pa lta bu/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la 'byung ba lta bu/ byang chub tu zhugs pa rnams la skul ba
26b5: lta bu/ gzhan gyi drid mi 'jog pa rnams la ye shes kyi snang ba lta bu dag ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten mi rtag par ston pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad par brjod pa dang / pra ni las
26b6: mdzad pa'i mthar thug par bstan pa dang / chos kyi rgyun tu nyams pa med pa'i dngos por brjod pa dang / srid pa'i tshul rtsa ba nas chad par rjod pa dang / sems can thams cad skyo bar bya bar bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas
26b7: kyi rjes su 'gro ba'i sems su mthun par bya ba dang / sku tshe'i mtha' lta bur sems can rnams kyis shes par bya ba dang / sems can rnams kyis 'jig rten thams cad du dga' bar bya ba med par bstan pa dang / sems
26b8: can rnams la ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig du brgyud pa mnyes par gyis shog par bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba bstan du mi rung bar khong du chud par bya ba dang

27a1: 'jig rten rnams kyi rtsol ba bskyed pa dang sangs rgyas la dmigs par brtson pa'i sems la dgod pa dang / yun tu dran pa rnam par dag pas de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba'i rnam par rtog pa skyed pa dang / skye ba'i/
27a2: dbang po phyir bzlog cing yongs su dag par mdzad pa dang / sangs rgyas la mos pa skyed pa dang / skyo bar gyur pa'i sems can rnams la byin gyis brlab par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas la dmigs pa'i rkyen 'jig rten gyi khams ma
27a3: lus pa thams cad du phyin par dgongs pa mdzad pa dang / sku thams cad bshig ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gdung gis sems can rnams yongs su gzung ba mdzad pa dang / 'jig rten rnam par 'khrug pa dang /
27a4: dregs shing mos pa'i sems can rnams sdom pa la bkodad pa mdzod cing / yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba ston pas kyang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi
27a5: phrin las dgu pa'o/ / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshe/ 'jig rten thams cad na sems can rnams smre sngags 'don cing ngu ba dang / mya ngan byed pa dang / 'chi ma 'byin pa dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
27a6: sangs rgyas zhe'am/ thugs rje chen po zhe'am/ ded dpon chen po zhe'am/ phan par bzhed pa thugs brtse ba can zhe'am/ lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi sems can thams cad kyi skyabs su gyur pa/ mgon du gyur pa/ rten
27a7: du gyur pa/ bla na med pa/ bsod nams kyi zhing / nub par gyur to zhes 'am/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'byung bar dka'o zhes rnam pa de lta bur smre sngags 'don cing / mya ngan byed pa dang / sangs
27a8: rgyas mthong ba rjes su dran pa'i sems can rnams kyi bsam pa dang / yid la bya ba de dang de dag gi sgor sangs rgyas kyi phrin las tshad med pa rgyun mi chad do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams yongs su mya ngan las

27b1: 'das pa'i tshe/ 'di lta sa sems can rnams kyi sems dad par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams dad pa'i mchod par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams cag pa'i bsam pa rnam par sbyang bar bya ba'i dbang dag
27b2: sems can rnams yongs su smi par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams yongasu sbyang bar bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnam gdul ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams kyi bsod nams kyi tshogs yongs
27b3: su rdzogs par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod pas dmigs par bya ba'i dbang dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod rten rnam pa sna tshogs su brgyan pas/ grogs dang yul
27b4: sna tshogs su sems can rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsab bsugs par bya ba'i dbang gis sems can rnams kyi bsam pa dang mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du su gdung dang / ring bsrel byin gyis rlob ste/ lha dang klu dang / gnod sbyin
27b5: dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am/ ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi'i gnas thams cad du 'dul ba dang / mos pa'i tshul ji lta ba bzhin du/ sku gdung dang ring bsrel byi gyis rlob po//
27b6: rang gi sku rnam par phye ste/ sku gdung dang / rang srel tshad med pa grangs med pa dpag tu med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa bya ni gyis rlob// de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod rten gyis sangs rgyas
27b7: kyi sku gdang / 'jig rten thams cad du rnam par phye ba de'i yul dang / phyogs kyi klu'i gnas dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' ldang dang / mi 'am/ ci dang lto 'phye chen po'i gnas dang /
27b8: mi'i gnas dang / srin po'i gnas dag tu sku gdung dang / ring bsrel mchod pa byed par 'gyur bas/ sku gdung gi ring srel dang dbu dang / phyag sen gyi mchod rten dang / sangs rgyas bzhags pa'i mchod rten la 'gro ba

28a1: thams cad nges par sangs rgyas dran par 'gyur te/ chos la rab tu rten par 'gyur ro// dge 'dun la dad pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// yul dang phyogs kyi gnas de dang de dag tu yang rgyun mi 'chad
28a2: par sangs rgyas mchod pa la brtson pa'i bsam pas sbyin pa yongs su gtong bar 'gyur ro/ / bsod nams byed par 'gyur ro// mtho sa de dang de yongs su dag pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// rigs dang rgyud kyi bdag
28a3: nyid che ba rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro/ / longs spyod chen po dang / 'khor rnam par dag pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// lha dang mi'i phun sum tshogs pa nyams su mnyer bar 'gyur ro// log par lhung ba med pa'i
28a4: lam yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro/ / sangs rgyas byung ba don yod pa rab tu sgrub par 'gyur ro// chos dkar po la gnas pa yongs su rdzogs par byed par 'gyur ro// khams gsum pa las 'byung ba'i
28a5: las yongs su spyod par 'gyur ro/ / theg pa gang la dad pa'i smon lam gyi nges par 'byung bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa de dag de dag la drin du gzo ba rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas
28a6: bcom ldan 'das rnams la rten pa dang / skyabs bcol ba dang / mgon tsam pa dang / dpung nyen btsam pa'i sems bskyed par 'gyur te/ de ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yongs su mya ngan las 'das kyang
28a7: yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab par spyod pa/ bsod nams zad mi shes pa'i yon tan gyi gnas dag ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten du 'byung na de ltar sems can rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa
28a8: ba rnam pa mang po rab tu bstsags pas bsod nams kyi tshogs rab tu rdzogs par gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bcu po'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag

28b1: ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgya chen po tshad med pa bsam kyis mi khyab pa rnams so/ / de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi byan rlabs ma gtogs par lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis tshad gzung
28b2: bar mi nus so/ / 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis 'jug par mi nus pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
28b3: gnyis su med par spyod cing / dngos po rnam pa gnyis su med pa'i chos kyi dbang phyug gi chos rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sangs rgya bcom ldan 'das rnams ni lung bstan pa thams cad ston pa la gnyis su med par spyod do//
28b4: sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can sangs rgyas kyi rjes su dran pa la brtson pa'i rnams kyi sems dang bsam pa brjod du med pa 'byam klas pa rnams la gnyis su med par spyod do// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad
28b5: kyi don ma lus par mngon par sangs rgyas pas gnyis su med pa'i sku rnam par mdzad do/ / 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la rang bzhin gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga'
28b6: ba'o/ / 'byung ba dang byang ba'i mtha' gnyis su med pa dang / sngon gyi mtha' dang / da ltar byung ba gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o// sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad gnyis su med pas dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi
28b7: zhing thams cad gcig par rab tu mkhyen cing ston pa thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o/ / sangs rgyas gcig dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsung gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams
28b8: cad kyis thugs su chud pa dang / 'dul ba mdzad pa'i rnam par dmigs su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o// 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o//

29a1: 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dge pa'i rtsa ba thams cad dge pa'i rtsa ba gcig ste// gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag/
29a2: ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gnyis su med par spyod cing // dngos po gnyis su med pa'i chos kyi dbang phyug gi chos so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin
29a3: gshegs pa bzhugs pa chos thams cad la rab tu zhugs pa rnams so/ / bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dbyings gnas pa'i ye shes thugs su chud pa la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
29a4: ldan 'das rnams ni thugs rje chen po mi mnyam pa la bzhugs pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni smon lam ji lta ba bzhin du 'byung ba la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'dul ba'i
29a5: sems can yongs su mi gtong ba la bzhugs pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dngos po med pa la gnas pa'i chos nyid la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku
29a6: skal ba mnyam pa tha mi dad cing don yod pa la bzhugs pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rtag tu mnyam par bzhag pa'i thugs la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad
29a7: nyams pa med par gzhol ba la bzhugs pa'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chags pa med pa'i dgongs pas rnam par spyod pa la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad kyi
29a8: mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pas grub pa med pa'i yang dag pa'i mtha'i mtshan nyid la bzhugs pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa chos thams

29b1: cad la bzhugs pa rnams so/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas com ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams cad ma lus par mngon par mkhyen pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhen 'di ltas/ chos kyi dbyangs ma lus pa/
29b2: thams cad kyi 'das pa 'grangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / ma 'ongs pa 'grangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / da lta byung ba 'grangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang /
29b3: gil ma mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / 'jig rten gyi chung mtha' dag thams cad pan par byen pa dang / sems can gyi bsam pa dang shes pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / byang chubs mas dpa' dag
29b4: rtsa ba chu ru dang 'bring dang chen po dang / rnam pa sna tshogs su rnam par gnas pa'i mtshan nyid kyis dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams la bsam pa tshad med pa yongs su mi gtong bas sangs rgyas kyi ye shes 'bar bar bya ba dang /
29b5: yongs su rdzogs par bya ba mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / chos thams cad 'tshang rgya ba'i mkhyen pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / 'jig rten gyi rgyud thams cad rnam
29b6: par dbye ba'i ye shes gzigs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi bzhi mig 'phrul gyi rnam pa lta bur dbye ba thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa ste// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni
29b7: sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams cad pa lus par mngon par mkhyen pa'o/ / /
29b8: bam po bzhi pa// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi stobs chen po// stobs dam pa stobs da med pa stobs bdag nyid che ba stobs

30a1: thug pa med pa/ stobs mnyam pa stobs snying po dang ldan pa/ stobs mi shigs pa/ stobs 'jig rten thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ stobs sems can thams cad kyis ma
30a2: 'phrog pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rgyal mtshan stobs po che/ dpa' ba chen po'i stobs rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi sku ni pha rol gyi gnod pa thams cad kyis mi shigs mchod pa'o//
30a3: 'jig rten gyi yul thams cad kyis sku tshe'i dbang po nyams par mi nus pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi bskal pa'i me'i gdud pas 'tshog par mi nus pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
30a4: 'jig par gtogs pa'i chu'i phung por 'grongs par mi 'gyur ba'o/ / bdud thams cad dang / bdud kyi sde thams cad dang / lha thams cad kyi dpung dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lham
30a5: yin dang / nam mkha' lnga de dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang / mi ma yin pa thams cad kyi dpung dang / sha za dang / srin po thams cad kyi dpung dang / sems can ma lus pa thams cad
30a6: kyi dpung gis brgal bar dka' ba'o/ / rdo rje ri rab kyi ri tsam gyi char ba dang / khor yug gi ri chen po tsam 'am/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i tsam gyi rdo rje'i char ba bkyang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin/
30a7: gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi ba spu gcig kyang 'gul bar mi 'gyur/ g.yo bar mi 'gyur te/ bag tsha ba'i shas mi mnga'o// bzhugs sam bzhengs sam
30a8: bzhud dam/ gzims kyang rung ste/ spyod lam 'gyur ba med do// de bzhin gshegs pa gang na bzhugs pa'i yul de dang de'i 'khor dag du yang de bzhin gshegs pa dgyes na kun tu 'bab par mi 'gyur ro//

30b1: sangs rgyas kyi nam rang ba rnams la yang gnod par mi 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi byin kyis brlabs pa'i sems can rnams la yang gnod par mi 'gyur zhing / ma gsan de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku la spos kya
30b2: dgos te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos dang po'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dpyas na/ chos kyi dbyings
30b3: thams cad kyis klas pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ri rab kyi ri dang bcas pa/ khor yug dang khor yug chen po'i ri dang bcas pa/ rgya mtsho dang / ri dang nags tshal thibs po dang / sems can gnas pa'i gan
30b4: tha dad pa kun dang / bcas pa da lta bu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i baspu'i bu ga gcig tu btsud de/ phyi ma'i mtha' bskal pa'i mur thug par bzhag kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi
30b5: rlabs ma gtogs par sems can rnams kyis shes par mi nus so/ / de bzhin gshegs pa de dag na de snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams sku'i ba spu'i khung bu gcig gis bzung ste/ phyi ma'i mtha' bskal pa'i mur thug
30b6: par bsnams shing / gshegs sam// bzhugs sam/ bzhengs sam/ gzims kyang rung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs skad cig tsam yang skyo ba mi mnga'o// chud cing dub par mi 'gyur ro// mthu dang
30b7: stobs la yongs su nyam par 'gyur ba mi mnga'o/ / spyod lam rnam par 'gyur ba mi mnga'o// spyod las rnam par 'gyur ba mi mnga'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di lta ste dper na/ nam mkha' ni chos kyi dbyangs ma lus
30b8: pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'dzin kyang skyo ba med do/ / du ba med do// gnod pa med do// med par mi 'gyur ro// mi g.yo mi 'byung mi 'jig go/ de bzhin du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyang ba

31a1: spu'i khung bu gcig du 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad bsdams kyang / de'i rgyas thugs skad cing tsam du yang mi bde ba'i sku nyams mi 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
31a2: kyis bo che chen po'i stobs/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos gnyis po'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams gshegs skabs gcig tu bzhug pas/ sangs rgyas kyi ning de brjod du med pa'i
31a3: yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi khams yongs su 'da' zhing / dgongs pa bskyed pa gcig gis bskal pa tha dad pa'i rim par sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
31a4: dbyung ba mdzad do/ / de lta bur gshegs pas bskal pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyad du gshegs shing / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems kyi rgyud ji snyed pa'i bskal par bdud
31a5: 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi/ 'jig rten gyi khams tsam du 'khor kun tu rgya che zhing yangs pa'i khor yug chen po'i rdo rje'i ri dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gyi rnam pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjodadu
31a6: med pal bsres pa snyed kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyang / de la bsres pa de snyed pa spu'i khang bu gcig tu btsud de/ ba spu'i khung bu gcig tu ji lta ba bzhin du/ sku'i ba spu'i khung bu thams cad du btsud de/ ba spu'i khung bu
31a7: yang sems can thams cad de snyed du gyur la/ de dag thams cad bsdams te/ de srid kyi baspu'i khung bu tshul de bzhin du bshams te/ thugs bskyed pa de la zas/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig
31a8: khams thams cad du chu zhing gshegs sam/ phyogs kyi dra ba thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs sam/ nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs sam/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud 'grangs pa sngon gyi mthar

31b1: gtogs pa nas bzung ste/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par/ de bzhin gshegs pas bskal pa thams cad zad par gyur kyang de bzhin gshegs pa bzhud pa la brtson pa ni nyams par mi 'gyur ro//
31b2: surnams chud par mi 'gyur ro// dgongs pa rnams par 'khrug par mi 'gyur ro// ting nge 'dzin nyams par mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku yongs su nyams par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan
31b3: 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos gsum pa'o/ / gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bsod snyoms gcig pazhes nas bskal pa brjod du med
31b4: par skyil mo krung gcig bcas pas/ nyin mtshan gyi tshun tu sdoma'i mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha'i mur gtogs pa'i bskal pa 'das par bzhugs kyang / sku mi g.yo zhing bde ba'i dam pa la spyod pa dang / sangs rgyas
31b5: kyi rnam par spyod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas rnam par spyod kyang / sems can 'ga' tsam la yang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun 'chad par mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku de la 'jig rten gyi khams thams
31b6: cad yongs su bkod de/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi sems can gcig gi lus kyang 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed tsam du che ba de lta bur
31b7: gyur la/ sems can gcig gi lus kyi tshad ji tsam pa de tsam gyi lus su sems can thams cad gyur la/ sems can de dag re re'i gzugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi lcid ji tsam yod pa de tsam du gyur
31b8: te/ sems can gcig gi lci ba bzhin du sems can thams cad re re'i lcid kyang de tsam du gyur te/ sems can de dag thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag sor kyi rtse mo gcig la/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i sur

32a1: thug par bsdams te/ phyags ma ma gcagags ji ltar bskams pa banan du phyag sar thams cad kyim ma la'ang / denam rang bsnams kyang / da' myor de bzhin gshegs pa la sumanyam
32a2: 'am/ dgongs badrub par mi 'gyur te/ thugs bskyed pa'i cha shas shin tu phra ba gcig tsam du yang sdug bsngal mi bde bskye par mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams la 'jug pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings
32a3: la 'jug pa dang / phyogs kyi dra ba'i rnam pa la 'jug pa re ra dang de lta bu la 'jug ba nam mkha'i khams ma lus pa'i dbyings kyis klas pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyi mtha' gtugs pa skra'i rtse mo'i gzhal pa'i 'jig
32a4: rten gyi khams la 'jug pa thams cad re re zhing yang / skra'i rtse mo'i cha shas kyis gzhal te/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyis kun tu khyab pa thams cad ma lus pa'i sgra'i rtse mo'i cha shas kyi tshad kyis nam mkha'i dbyings la
32a5: 'jug pa thams cad du zhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod lam 'di'i tshul dang / skyil mo krung gcig tu bzhugs pa'i spyod pas/ sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa zad par mdzad de/
32a6: bskal pa 'da' bar mdzad cing / bskal pa la rab tu 'jug ste// 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bzhi pa'o// gzhan
32a7: yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku cig la/ dbu sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis byin brlabs te/ dbu re re yang ljags sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du
32a8: med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyad byin gyis brlabs nas/ de dag re res kyang dbyangs kyi yan lag dang sgra skad kyi gsung / sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra/

32b1: bsnyed re re brjod de/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i sems can gyi khams thams cad go bar mdzad cing byangs kyi yan lag dang sgra skad kyi gsung re res kyang mdo sde sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i
32b2: rdul shin tu phra ba skad bkad la mdo sder re yang chos bstan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra bsnyed rab tu gzhol bar mdzad de/ chos bstan pa gcig las kyang chos kyi
32b3: dang yi ge sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang rjod du med pa'i rjod rdul shin tu phra ba snyed brjod par gyur la/ chos bstan pa gcig las ji lta ba de bzhin du chos bstan pa thams cad las kyang de snyed kyi chos kyi tshig
32b4: dang yi ge brjod de/ / de ltar brjod pas bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra bsnyed du rab tu bstan pa/ bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin
32b5: tra pra ba snyed zad par gyur kyang / dadung gzhan yang bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul gan tu phra ba snyed du brgyad cing rab tu ston pa'i tshul gyis rnam grangs 'dis bskal pa 'jig rten gyi
32b6: khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du rab tu bstan la/ rnam grangs 'di 'dra bas bskal pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed zad la sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi spyod
32b7: pasnyed kyi bskal pa 'das par gyur te/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa zad cing 'das par byas kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa chos thams cad snang ba'i 'khor lo bskor ba dang / chos thams cad rab tu shes
32b8: par bstan cing / lung bstan pa dang / the tsom thams cad rab tu gcod pa'i 'khor lo bskor ba dang / chos thams cad snang bar byed cing / chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa thams cad brjod pa'i rgyun dang ldan

33a1: pa 'chos kyi 'khar la bskor ba dang / ye shes kyi nya ma'i dkyil 'khar chen pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad ma lus par ye shes kyi sngon mchen pos bcan pa'i tsha
33a2: kyi khor lo bskor ba dang / so so yang dag par rig pa dang / mi 'jigs pa chen pos bstan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor brgyan mi 'chad de/ sangs rgyas kyi sku gcig gi byin kya rlabs kyis jil ba bzhin du/ chos kyi 'a
33a3: la'i sngon chen po da ba thams cad dang / dab med par rab tu 'byung bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin du chos kyi dbyangs ma lus pa thams cad kyi nam mkha' dbyings kyi mtha' gtugs pa sna'i rnama'i chags kyis gzhan pas
33a4: lus pa thams cad chags pa med par rnam par dbye bas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod dram dpa yang brjod du med pa skad kyi sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa de snyed de snyed du dgongs pa'i gad cig ringal gyim
33a5: mtha'i mung thug pa'i bskal par sprul pa mdzad cing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa'i sku thams cad las de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku re re la'ang / de snyed de nyid kyi dbu mnga' bar gyur la gzhung de bzhin du dbu re ra la
33a6: yang de snyed de snyed kyi ljags mnga' bar gyur te/ ljags re re las kyang de snyed de snyed kyi dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / sgra skad kyi gsung chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i sems can gyi khams thams cad go bar mdzad pa byung
33a7: la/ dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / sgra skad kyi gsung de dag re res kyang de snyed de snyed kyi mdo sde bshad par gyur la mdo sde de dag re re la yang de snyed de snyed kyi/ chos bstan pa rab tu gzhol ba mdzad de// chos sman
33a8: pa de dag de re re las kyang / de snyed de snyed kyi chos kyi tshig dang yi ge brjod par gyur la/ chos kyi tshig dang yi ge de dag re res kyang chos kyi dbyangs ma lus pa thams cad dbyangs kyis rgyas par bkang ste/ sems

33b1: can gyi khams mams pa thams cad ko bar mdzad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbyangs la drab pa ma mnga'/ / rnams par ma 'gyur la thugs pa mamang 'a nang dma' bar ma 'byung ba// des tha mas kyi kha sa da /
33b2: yang bskas pa phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bar du rgyun 'chad par mi gur ta/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthub che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos lnga pa'o// gan
33b3: yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs dpal gyi be'us brgyan pa/ rdo rje chen po ltar shin tu btan par grub pa mnga' bdag ste/ de dag byang chub kyi shing drung du byon na bdud srog tocan gyis sems can
33b4: thams cad snyed kyi bdud kyi sde/ gzugs sna tshogs can shin tu mi sdug pa/ 'jigs 'jigs ltar 'dug pa/ rab tu sngar ba'i gzugs can 'jig rten thams cad shin tu 'jigs pa'i gzugs can rab tu
33b5: spyigaya' bskyed pa'i gzugs can/ bdud shin tu mi sdug pa'i gzugs 'chad par bcog por 'jigs pa/ 'jigs pa chen po bskyed pa/ 'gro ba thams cad gsod pa/ 'jig rten thams cad phung par byed
33b6: pa de lta bu sha stag gis/ byang chub kyi shing drung dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug par gang bar gzigs kyang byang chub kyi shing drung na 'azhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa
33b7: rnams la bsnyengs pa sa mnga'o/ / bag tshab mi mnga'o// ba spu gcig kyang g.yo pa med do// dgongs pa'i cha shanaHphra ba 'ga' tsam gyis kyang de ltar rnam pa tha dad pa'i gzugs la mtshan ma rnam pa zad
33b8: badzin pa mi mnga' ste/ shin tu bstan no// g.yo ba med do// mi sprul to// 'gyur ba med do// rnam par rtog pa med do// shin tu zhi'o// snyengs pa dang bgaca ba thams cad dang shin tu bral lo// sreg pa dang 'ang

34a1: pa shin tu spangs so/ / sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa rgyan pa 'chadade/ byams pa can pa'i stabs dang ldan pag// thugs rje can pa'i gnas kyis dbang por shin tu dben pa'o// bag
34a2: mnga' ba'i dgongs pa dang ldan pa'o/ / dgongs pa shin tu brtan zhing nyams pa mi mnga' ba'o// tshwas zil gyis mi don la pas zil gis gnon pa'i dgongs pa dang ldan pa ste/ bdud thams cad dang /
34a3: bdud kyi ris su gtogs pa'i lha thams cad dang / bdud kyi sde thams cad shin tu zil gyis gnon to// shin tu spa skrod do// de ltar zil gyis panan te/ spa skong pa dang / de ba'adi gshegs pa la
34a4: skyabs tshol lo/ / de dag la'ang bcom ldan 'das de dag cho 'phrul chen po gsum gyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdul ba mdzad pa nye bar sgrub ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las
34a5: phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ro/ / 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos drug pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom
34a6: ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung thogs pa med pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa de dang / de dag thams cad du sems can rnams 'dul ba'i don gyis rnam par dmigs par kun tu khyab par 'byung ste/ de
34a7: bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung de ni ri rnams la thogs pa med do/ / ri rab la thogs pa med do// rin po che'i ri rab la thogs pa med do// khor yug dang khor yug chen po la thog pa med do// lha'i khyim
34a8: mthogs pa med do/ / sla khyim la thogs pa med do// gdod spyod kyi khyim 'thogs pa med do// dri za'i khyim la thogs pa med do// lha ma yin gyi byil la phags pa med do// rnamapa'a' sngag gi kyi

34b1: thogs pa med do/ / mi 'am ci'i khyim la thogs pa med do// lto 'phye chen po'i khyim la thogs pa med do// pi dang mi ma yin pa'i khyim la thogs pa med do// gal te brgya la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na
34b2: yod pa'i sgra chen po 'jig rten rnams tha dad pa'i sgras/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad gang ste/ caco 'dres par gyur kyang / de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs pa'i gsung ni 'dul ba'i sems can rnam
34b3: kyi ba'i rnam par dmigs pa la bsgribs pa med pa yin te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung 'ba' shig de dag gi rnam par dmigs pa la/ lhang de snyam ma snyed de ste go par mdzad pa'i tshig dang / yi ge
34b4: rnams kyang rlag par mi 'gyur te/ 'din sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bathu bo che cher po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bdun pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas
34b5: bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chags pa mi mnga' bste/ bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par yongs su sbyangs pa'o// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar
34b6: byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad dang / rgyad gcig tu gyur pa'o// rnyog pa med cing rnam par dang ba sti sha ni tu gsal ba'o// bdag gi zhes bya ba mi mnga' ba'o// chos thams cad la mi gnas pa'o//
34b7: nang na gnas pa pa yin pa'o// phyi rolan gnas pa pa yin pa'o/ skyes pa'o// dmigs pa thams cad kyis dben pa'o// zhizhis gnas med pa'o// rtsom pa med pa'o// 'dra shes sna tshogs thams cad la mi
34b8: gnas pa'o/ / dngos po'i rnam par rtog pa thams cad 'gags pa'o// rang bzhin gyis 'od dang zhing gsal ba'o// yongs su dag pa'o// dmigs pa dang yid la byas pa thams cad ma 'dres pa'o// chos thams

35a1: cang nyon mongs pa med pa'i yul dang ldan pa'o/ / yang dag pa'i mtha' 'dod chags dang bral bas dag pa'o// chos kyi dbyings shin tu bstan pa'i mthar thug pa'o// chos kyi dbyings kun nas
35a2: ma zad pa dang ldan pa'o/ / 'du shes kyi rnam pa thams cad kyi tshad dang tshad med pa dang bral ba'o// 'dus byas dang / 'dus ma byas kyi brjod pa thams cad 'gags pa'o// tshig gi lam gyis brjod du med pa'i
35a3: mthar thug pa'i yal lo/ / mi zad pa dang / chags pa med pa'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa'o// ye shes sngon du 'gro ba'o// stobs bcu'i rgyun tu gyur pa'o// chos thams cad kyis rnam par dag pa'o// bas
35a4: mkhas pa 'byung ba'o/ / chos sna tshogs dang / chos du ma dang / chos thams cad shin tu bstan pa dang mi 'gal ba'o// dus gsum tha dad pa med pa'o// chos kyi dbyings thams cad du chos gzhi med pa
35a5: thams cad kyi mnga' ba'i pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pa'o/ / chos thams cad la mnga' ba'i 'byung gnas dang / mdzod du gyur pa'o// chos kyi tshul thams cad la dgongs pa khyad par du rmongs pa med pa'o//
35a6: zhing gi chung du gtogs pa thams cad dang / phyogs kyi dra ba dang / rmad 'byam klas pa ma lus pa thams cad la mi gnas pa brtan zhing mi g.yol nyams pa med pa'i ye shes kyis rab tu gzigs pa/
35a7: chos ma lus pa thams cad kyi mthar thug pa/ zag pa thams cad yongs su zad pa dgongs pa rnam par grol zhing zag pa mi mnga' ba dang / shes rab rnam par grol bas shin tu rnam par grol ba yang
35a8: dag pa'i mtha' mi zad pa'i klas pa/ chags pa med par rnam par spyod pa/ rtag tu mnyam par gzhag pa/ dus gsum thams cad du bsgribs pa med par 'byung ba/ sems can thams cad kyi dus

35b1: gsum gyi sems dang / spyod pa thams cad ma lus par thugs skad cig gis rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan
35b2: chos brgyad pa'o/ / gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku ni sa mi mnga' ba ste/ rang bzhin gcig tu gyur la/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul tshad med pa'i sku'o// mtha'
35b3: dang dpung med par yongs su grub pa'i sku'o/ / 'jig rten thams cad kyis zad par mo nus pa'i sku'o// khams gsum pas gos pa med pa'i sku'o// rten pa'i skus rnam par dmigs pa'o// lhag
35b4: pa'i bsam pa dang / rjes su dran pa'i byin gyis rlabs kyis sku'i rang bzhin yang dag par snyan pa'o// bden pa med pa dang / brdzun pa med pa'i sku mnyam pa nyid kyis yongs su dag pa'o// chos kyi sku
35b5: bzhud pa dang / byon pa med pa'i sku'o// 'dus ma byas pas 'jigs pa med pa'i sku'o// mtshan nyid med pas mtshan nyid gcig pa'i chos kyi sku'i rang bzhin no// yul na mi gnas pa dang / phyogs
35b6: na mi gnas pa'i sku'o/ / ma lus pa thams cad kyi lus kyi sku'o// sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu byung ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' yas pa sku'i rang bzhin no// lus thams cad du yongs su
35b7: bzhol ba'i sku sna tshogs su rnam par dmigs pa mdzad kyang chos kyi sgra'i tshul mi rjes su 'brang ba'o/ / ye shes kun tu snang ba'i snying stotsan no// sku yongs kyi mdzod du thar pa'o// chos kyi dbyings rnamapa
35b8: thadad pa med pa ga ni tu bstan pa'i sku'o/ / khams ma lus pa thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pas/ kun tu khyab pa'i sku'i rang bzhin no// mi g.yom dgongs pa'i skurnam par dag pa'o// yad pa ma yin med pa'

36a1: ma yin pa'i tshul dang tshul ma yin par rab tu brjod pa'i skal/ / sems can gyi mos pa rnam pa sna tshogs 'dul bar 'gyur ba'i sgra'o// 'gags pa'ang ma yin ma 'gags pa'ang ma yin pas
36a2: 'dus bsten pa'i sgra'o/ / yon tan na pa cha thams cad yang dag par ston pa'i sgra'o// yon tan na pa cha thams cad yang dag par byung bas shin tu 'phags pa'i sgra'o// chos thams cad sangs rgyas
36a3: kyi de bzhin nyid du yang dag par bsgrubs pa'i sku'o/ / rang bzhin gyis rab tu zhi zhing bsgribs pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i sku'o// thogs pa mi mnga' bas chos thams cad thugs su chud pa'i sku'o// thams cad kyi
36a4: rjes su song ba'i chos kyi dbyings kyis rnam par dag cing / 'jig rten gyi thams cad shin tu rnam par phye ba'i sku'o// phyir mi ldog cing bsgribs pa mi mnga' la/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pas ye shes thams
36a5: cad kyi rjes su 'brang zhing / yang dag par gzhol bas/ thugs su chud pa'i sku te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos dgu pa'o//
36a6: gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ye shes mnyam pa med pa dang / mnyam pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis thugs su chud pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad
36a7: kyis byung ba'o/ / mngon par bsgrub pa'i spyod pa khyad par du 'phags pa'i smon lam dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pas rnam par dag pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyis yongs su
36a8: rdzogs par byas so/ / tha dad pa med pa'o// / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyis byung ba'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya mtsho'i spyod pa'i tshul thams cad thugs su chud

36b1: pa'o/ / smon lam dang spyod pa chen pos yongs su mi 'dogs pa'o// spyod pa thams cad mi mnyam pa med pas yongs su rdzogs par byas pa'o// spyod pa'i stobs la thag par dka' ba'i spyod pa thams cad kyis
36b2: mngon par byung ba'o/ / spyod pa thams cad kyis rnam par dag pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa lags par spyad pas rgyan dma' ba med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad kyis tshad med par
36b3: spyod pa'o/ / nga nge 'dzin thams cad kyis spyod yul mtha' yas pa'o// lam thams cad kyis rab tu brjod pa ma yin pa'o// lam gyi yul med pa'o// lam thams cad las rab tu zhugs pa'o// ye shes dam pa'i stobs
36b4: kyis tshul mkhyen pa'o/ / bag tsha ba mi mnga' bas/ chos kyi char 'babs pa'i 'khor lo dang ldan pa'o// dge ba dris pa dang / ma dris pa la rjesu 'thun pa'i chos kyi tshul ston pa mkhyen pa'o// mnyam pa med pa dang / mnyam pas
36b5: shin tu dag pa'o/ / sku dang thugs dang gsung gi yang dag par spyod pa rnams la phrin las gsum yongs su dag pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi bsgom pas brnyes so// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs thams cad bskyed pa'i
36b6: don du sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyis mdzad pa thams cad rab tu 'byung ba'o/ / thams cad mkhyen pa'i gnas kyi bstan pa tshad med pa'i gnas rtsa ba med pa dang ldan pa'o// mngon par shes pa'i ye shes thams
36b7: cad kyis mthar thug par mi 'gyur ba'o/ / 'jig rten gyi sems kyi spyod pa'i shes pa thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab bo// chos thams cad ma lus par mkhyen cing gzigs pas sems can thams cad
36b8: yongs su skyob pa'o/ / dus gsum yangs pa thams cad kyi tshul shin tu phra ba mtha' dang dbus med pa ma lus par mkhyen pa'o// 'jig rten las 'das pa'i don mkhyen pa'i phyir phra ba'i ye shes thugs su chud pas

37a1: pas 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad rnam par dag pa'i phyir mi ldog pa'i ye shes kyis sangs rgyas kyi brani las brjod du med pa 'jig rten thams cad du sbyor ba'o/ / sangs rgyas kyi sku
37a2: grangs pa thams cad thugs su chud pa'i ye shes kyis yi ge med pa'i chos thugs su chud pa'o/ / yi ge sna tshogs rnam par bye ba dang / yi ge thams cad smos shing brjod pa mkhyen pas/ brjod du med pa
37a3: thugs su chud pa'o/ / kun tu bzang po'i ye shes kyis dge ba'i rtsa ba'i chos sprad pa thams cad rnam par dag pa'o// dam bcas pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can thams cad kyi lus dang skye mched ji ltar dgongs
37a4: pa'i skad cig dang ldan pa'i shes rab kyis chos thams cad khong du chud par ston pa mkhyen pa'o/ / chos thams cad kyi don du chos yongs su btang 'di rim gror bya ba sa thugs su chud pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams
37a5: thams cad ma lus par yul du gyur pa'o/ / chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad yul du gyur pa'o// dus gsum thams cad la dgongs pa'i skad cig gis chags pa med par mkhyen cing thugs su chud pa'i yul
37a6: dang ldan pa'o/ / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas 'byung ba ma lus par yul du gyur pa'o// 'jigs pa med par 'dul ba thams cad yul du gyur pa'o// thams cad kyi rjes su song zhing rnam par dag
37a7: pa'i yul thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas pa'o/ / sa mtshams med cing thug pa med pa'i mngon par shes pa rnam par sangs rgyas pa'o// sems can thams cad kyi sems dang yid dang rnam par shes pa'i rnam
37a8: pa dus gsum du brjod pa ma lus pa thams cad dgongs pa'i skad cig gis mkhyen cing thugs su chud pa'o/ / sems can gyi rnam pa thams cad las mtshams ma bcad pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rnam pa thams cad la/

37b1: mu med pa'o// dus gsum gyi rnam pa thams cad la mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu byung ba'i rnam pa thams cad la tshad med pa'o// shes bya'i rnam pa thams cad la lha ma ma lus pa ste/ de dag
37b2: thams cad lhag ma mar par mngon par sangs rgyas pas sangs rgyas kyi ye shes sangs rgyas kyi rdzu 'phrul dang rnam par 'phrul bas byung ba thams cad thugs su chud pa dang / mkhyen pa thams cad kun 'chad pa ma
37b3: de la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu byung ba'i skus/ mtha' dang dbus med par spyod pa yin/ chags pa med pa'i dgongs pas spyod pas mtha' dang dbus med par spyod pa yid
37b4: thugs rjes chen po'i sbyor bas dus thams cad du rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par chos bstan pa la spyod pas mtha' dang dbus med par spyod pa yin te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mthu
37b5: po che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bcu pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i
37b6: rgyal mtshan gyi chos rnams te/ 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sems can thams cad dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab cing dpag tu mi nus pa dag
37b7: go/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thogs pa mi mnga' ba rnams te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dga' ldan gyi tshe/ ji srid par bzhugs nas 'pho ba la
37b8: thogs pa mi mnga'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni zla ba bcur bltam pa bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mngon par 'byung ba'i dgyes pa'i dgongs pas

38a1: mngon par 'byung ba la thogs pa mi mnga'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub kyi shing drung du bzhugs nas sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya ba la thogs pa mi mnga'o//
38a2: sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dgongs pa'i skad cig gis sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas nas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa
38a3: thams cad yongs su bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dus bzhin du 'dul ba rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba la thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'dra
38a4: rnams na dge ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa'i tshul bzhin du dus la bab par bshad cing lung bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dus la bab pa'i tshul bzhin du sangs rgyas
38a5: kyi phrin las mdzad pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa' yongs su grub pa rnams lung bstan pa la thogs pa ma mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
38a6: 'das rnams ni skad cig gcig tu sems can thams cad kyis dri ba yongs su dris pa skad cig gcig gis lung bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga' ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan
38a7: 'das rnams kyi thogs pa mi mnga' ba'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ma thag tu myur du 'byung ba'i chos rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/
38a8: sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du ngan song dang bral bar 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du bsod

38b1: nams yongs su rdzogs pa 'thob par 'gyur ro/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du dge ba'i rtsa ba la yongs su sman par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
38b2: rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du mtho sa su skye ba yongs su dag pa 'thob par 'gyur ro/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du yid gnyis dang / nem nur yang dag
38b3: par bstsal ba 'thob par 'gyur ro/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du byang chub kyi sems bskyed nas phyir mi ldog pa 'thob par gyur te/ sems can mos pa yangs pa dang ldan pa
38b4: sangs rgyas kyis 'dral ba las byang chub tu sems ma bskyed pa'i rnams kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed do/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu skyon med par ma
38b5: 'das par dmigs pa'i lta ba can rnams myur du skyon med par 'da' ba'i rgyu rab tu 'dzin to/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du 'jig rten dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dbang po rnam
38b6: par dag par 'gyur ro/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du bsgribs pa thams cad byang ba thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu
38b7: sems can rnams myung du snang ba 'thob cing mi 'jigs pa zhum pa med pa'i spobs pa rab tu rtsom ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ma thag tu mungadu
38b8: 'byung ba'i chos rnams so/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rjes su dran pa rnam par dag pa ste/ bcu ga she na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi sbyar bas kyang

39a1: byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni spyod pa rnam par dag pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas/
39a2: bcom ldan 'das rnams ni pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon la mchen po 'angs su rdzogs pas
39a3: byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rjes su dran pas bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yang dag par bsgrubs pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
39a4: rnanarnams ni sngon gyi mthar sangs rgyas kyi tshangs par spyod pa la spyad pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yan/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i sgonas kyang byang
39a5: chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gzugs kyi sku tshad med mu med pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom
39a6: ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi yul gyis rnam par 'phrul pa tshad med mu med pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni stobs ban dang
39a7: ma 'jigs pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rjes su dran pa rnam par dag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i
39a8: sras bcu po 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rnam par spyod pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar chos dbyings thams cad dang / dus gsum gyi sems can thams cad kyi sems

39b1: sna tshogs dang / sems du ma dang spyod pa dang g.yo ba'i rgyud thams cad ma lus pa dgongs pa gcig gis thugs su chud pa dang / dus gsum gyi sems can thams cad kyi las dang las kun nam blangs pa sna tshogs cham
39b2: tshe dgra rnam pa tha dad pas mngon par 'gro nang bar stsogs pa mang nyung dang / rnam par smin pa tha dad pa ma lus par dgongs pa gcig gis thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can gyi ris rbA/
39b3: tshogs dang / sems can gyi ris du ma'i sems can ma lus pa thams cad 'dul ba'i dus ji bzhin du yongs su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul dang rjes su bstan pa'i chos 'phrul dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi cho 'phrul gyis byin gyi chub
39b4: yang dag par bstan pa ma lus pas thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / phyogs dra ba'i rgyud thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud thams cad kyi sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi mtshan ma
39b5: bzung ba ste/ sangs rgyas bstan pa dang / skye ba dang rnam par dbye ba ma lus par thugs su chud pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams na thams cad kyi sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba dang / mos pa ji lta ba dang 'dul
39b6: ba ji lta ba bzhin du rnam pa tha dad pa tshad med par skad cig du sangs rgyas pa bstan pa dang / rnam par dmigs par bya ba dang / byin gyis brlabs pa ma lus par thugs su chud pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi
39b7: sems can pha rol gyi bsam pa la/ sangs rgyas kyi byin kyis rlabs yang dag par bstan pa ma lus par thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can rnams 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du nye bar len pa
39b8: med pa'i sangs rgyas nyid du 'gyur gdams ngag dang rjes su bstan pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba snyan pa ma lus par thugs su chud chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can thams cad kyi thams

40a1: da du 'gro ba dang / de dang dang 'gro ba'i lam ma gus par dgangs pa'i ma cag gagags thugs sa chud pa dang rgyas kyang byangs thams cad kyisems can rnams kyis/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa rgyags
40a2: rnams cad du btang ba'i rnam mkhas par dgongs pa'i skad cig gcigags thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can rnams kyi mos pa dang / sems kyi tshad dris pa bzhin du sangs rgya
40a3: kyi sku kha dog mu med pa dbyibs mtha' yas pa bstan pa ma lus par dgongs pa'i skad cig gcig gis thugs su chud pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par
40a4: rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rnam par spyod pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi sangs rgyas
40a5: kyi ting nge 'dzin tshad med bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad
40a6: kyi sems can rnams la'ang skad cig gcig tu chos ston pa mdzad do/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can thams cad la mnyam par gzhag kyang skad cig/
40a7: gcig gis sems can gyi khams sku chags rnam pa dad pa rnams kyang bdag med pa'i mtha' la gnas par yongs su ston to// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi dus
40a8: gsum la mnyam par gzhag kyang dgongs pa'i skad cig gcig gis cha shas la'ang mnyam par bzhag cing rnam par spyod do/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi

40b1: phyogs 'byam klas pa'i dra ba thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing gyi rgyud dang / rnam pa thams cad la mnyam par bzhag kyang mi zad pa'i zhing gi mtha' la'ang bzhugs shing rnam par spyod do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
40b2: 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi sgyu mu med pa la mnyam par bzhag kyang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi sku tshogs rnam par dmigs par yang
40b3: dag par ston pa mdzad do/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad sku dang gsung dang thugs kyis yongs su rgyas par rtag tu mnyam par gzhag kyang sems can thams cad kyi
40b4: sems 'byung ba'i mdzod ma chags la yang mos pa dang yid la byed pa jig ba bzhin du rnam par spyod do/ / sangs kyis bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi chos thams cad
40b5: rang bzhin la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang 'dod chags dang bral ba'i mtha'i mur thug pa la bzhugs pa yang yongs su mi gtang ngo / / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams
40b6: da kyi 'jig can thams cad kyi rten thal rtag tu mnyam par gzhag kyang dgongs pa skad cig gis rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba brjod pa yang rab ston to/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dzas
40b7: kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'jig rten pa dang 'jig tan mas 'das pa ma/ klas pa la rtag tu mnyam par gun ga byung / dgongs pa sa migags sems can thams cad la sangs rgyas ma mad
40b8: bstan pa nam par bshad pa'i tshul ma med pas sangs rgyas bstan pa skrun mi gcad do/ / sangs kyis bcom ldan 'das rnams nings kyi byings ma lus pa thams cad du bsgribs pa med par rtag mnyam par banag

41a1: kyang dgongs pa sa cag gis sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyang rtogs par thugs su chud cing sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa sremed pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa mchog brnyas par bzhugs te/ kye
41a2: ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams so/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas
41a3: bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam par thar pa rnams te/ bcug she na/ rdul shinaH phra ba gcig la sangs rgyas skye ba brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul gnaHphra
41a4: ba gcig la chos kyi 'khor lo brdod du med pa yang brjod dri med pa bskor ba yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul gan tu pra bcig la sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du
41a5: med pa yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa/ rdul shan tu phra ba gcig la zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang / mabyon pa dang / dasang
41a6: byung ba'i sangs rgyas sra pa thams cad yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang / mabyon pa dang / dkang byung ba'i zhing gi chud yongs su bas na pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / dul shin tu phrab
41a7: gcig la 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / rnam par 'phrul pa yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang / mabyon pa
41a8: dang / dgrang byung ba'i sems can gyi khams thams cad yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul gan tu phra ba gcag la 'das pa dang / mabyon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi phrini las thams cad yongs/

41b1: sra bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa ste/ kye brgyal ba'i sras bcu pa de dag na sangs rgyas rnams kyi rnam par thar pa'o// gan thargyas pa can pa mad sangs rgyas pal pa che zhes bya ba las/ sangs rgyas byangs
41b2: bsam gyis myi khyab pa bstan pa'i le'u ste/ sum bcu dgu pa'o// /
41b3: bam po lnga pa/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos// mtshan rgya mtsho brjod du med pa'i don tu byang chub sems dpa' de dag la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag
41b4: de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul mi chen po'i mtshan chos kyi rgyan rin po che sna tshogs sum cu rtsa gnyis mnga' bas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu de ni 'khor yug nas/ 'od gzer gyi dra ba shin tu 'byung zhing rgyas par gang
41b5: bste/ de la mi chen po'i mtshan rini po che'i dang po/ dbu'i dbu mtshams na rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi rgyal po'i las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du snang ba kye ba/ dpal gyis yongs su rgyas shing yan
41b6: lag dang nying lag thams cad nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprin rnam par bkye ba yongs su 'khyal ba'i glong gi dbyibs kyis phyogs thams cad 'od kyis rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi dbu
41b7: la 'phro ba'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor klong gi 'phreng ba lta bur 'byung bas/ phyogs mtshams thams cad de de bzhin gshegs pa'i snang po byang chub tu bzhugs pa ston cing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rnamam pa'i seMn can

42a1: 'das pas/ chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i rgyal po sna tshogs mdzod spu g.yas phyogs su yongs su 'khyil pa'i dbyibs las gser gyi kha dog bzang por 'od zer
42a2: 'bar bar 'jig rten gyi khams su gyur pa'i 'od kyis chos kyi dbyings thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan gsal ba'i 'od kyis ni ces bya ba mnga' ba de bzhin gshegs
42a3: pa'i dbu la rin po che'i 'od kyi glong g.yas phyogs su yongs su 'khyil pa/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsod nams dang ye shes kyi sgron ma snang bas/
42a4: 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi sprin rnam par 'dal ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i mchog rnams la snang bas chos kyi dbyings rgyas par khyab pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs
42a5: pa'i mtshan gser ya du 'ong ba'i sprin sna tshogs kyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang / rab tu 'bar bas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od zer rnam par sdang bar byas pas/ sangs
42a6: rgyas kyi zhing bsam gyis mi khyab pa snang bar bstan pa'i 'od kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che bai dUr+ya'o// zer dang / me tog gi mdog gis chos kyi dbyangs
42a7: thams cad snang bar rnam par 'phrul pa'i spu ni nor bu rin po che rgyal po'i mtshan nyid lta ba'i dbu skra rin po che sna tshogs sdang ba'i mtshan nyid kyi 'od chags pas/ phyogs thams cad rnam par snang bar byed pa/ sangs rgyas
42a8: kyi sngon gyi dka' thub dang / dpal gyi ye shes las rnam pa de lta bu byung ba'i rin po che'i 'od zer rab tu bkye ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dang /

42b1: dang / ran pa cha' 'ang zer gapas phyogs sul rjes cing 'gro bas byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul par na ba chabacad pan bya 'do bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyis rnam par rgyas pas 'jig rten gyi khams
42b2: thams cad du rin po che'i 'od tshad med par de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi rang bzhin gyis rnam par 'phrul pa yang dag par ston pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan
42b3: rin po che rnam par 'phrul pas/ / nor bu rin po che rgya mtshos bkye ba'i 'od dang / 'od zer drim med par rab tu 'phros pas byang chub sems dpa'i chos bstan pa rgya mtshonam par sdang bar 'das pa dang / ma byon par
42b4: da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi ye shes kyis rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pas/ chos kyi dbyings kun tu de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung gi sprin 'byung ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul
42b5: rin po che'i rgyal po sems kyi rgyal po dang / in 'dra ni las 'od bkye ba g.yas phyogs su 'khyil pas 'jig rten gyi khams dang / chos kyi dbyangs thams cad du snang ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'od 'phro ba sgron ma'i sprin de bzhin
42b6: gshegs pa thams cad kyi yon tan rgya mtsho rab tu sgrogs pas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad nga ro 'byin cing sangs rgyas kyi stobs rnams yongs su dag pa/ rgya mtsho dang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho 'byin pa'i spos shin tu yangs
42b7: pa'i 'od ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i me tog sna tshogs dang / rin po che'i rgyal po bai dUr+ya'i 'od zer rin po che'i thams cad kyi 'od zer kun tu 'byung ba'i dra ba mngon par 'phags
42b8: pa las/ / chos kyi las dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dang // phyogs rgya mtshor de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa yang dag par ston cing / sangs rgyas kyi stobs chos kyi

43a1: byangs la mngan tugyu bar btu gan par bzhugs pa/ sems can thams cad ma yangs su ldan sa/ danan gshegs pa'i sa yang dag pa pa nas shi yangs su dag sa ngas ba dasasangs sun/
43a2: rin po che thams cad kyi 'od kun tu snang ba'i rang bzhin rab tu bkye ba'i 'od gzer dkyil 'khor gyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan 'jig rten gyi khams cad dmang pan bzhugs par
43a3: bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi mtshan rin po che las 'od rab tu bkye bar zhing thams cad kun nas yo ga cing bsgribs pa med de/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad sangs rgyas kyi gsung rin po che'i me tog shin tu rgyas pa'i 'odag
43a4: 'gro ba rab tu babyed pas/ chos kyi rgya mtsho chen po rab tu sbyar ba las/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyi snying po dang snang ba can gyi sprin langs pa'i 'od ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin
43a5: che bai dUr+ya dang / ani dra ni la dang rdo rje mang po las nor bu rin po che rnam par ston te/ rab tu bkram pa'i kha dog mtha' yas pa'i 'od rnam par dag pa rin po che rnam par dag par ni po che bai dUr+ya'i 'od kun tu 'byung ba las
43a6: sgra skad rgya mtsho thams cad kyis chos kyi dbyings su sangs rgyas kyi snang ba rnam par ston pa'i chos rgya mtsho'i ye shes sangs rgyas sprul pa'i 'od kun tu 'gyed pa'i sgra ni rab tu snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / sangs rgyas
43a7: d bu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan ni po che'i g.yas phyogs su 'phro ba'i me tog rarini po che'i lhab lhub kyis bstan pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po byang chub kyi rgyan gyi smon
43a8: mngon par 'thon pa/ chos kyi dbyings dang / 'jig rten gyi khams tham cad du chos thams cad du chos rnam par dag pa ste/ bskal pa thams cad du rnam par thar pas chos kyi dbyings rnam par sangs rgyas pa'i sprin ces bya ba

43b1: nga' ba dang / sangs rgyas ca bral ban gagags pa nanapa thasems kyirnas 'dag dam partam sa brtan mam sacan dus nanapa pa da na ma
43b2: sems dpa'i smani la spang ba zhin tu 'byung zhing ye shes kyi sku dang / chos kyi sras de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyimatshan rgya ma tshal spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'as yongs su grub pa'i spyan dang / chos kyang kyis te
43b3: sprin gyi 'od ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rdo rje'i gzhim tog dang / ldan pa'i ba dU r+ya kun tu snang bas chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi rgyan ta gyur na/ rnam par snang bas chos
43b4: k yi dbyings rgya mtsha yongs su rgyas par 'gengs shing 'jig rten gyi khams su rin po che thams cad kyi pad ma'i 'od kyi rgyan thams cad kyi brtan thams cad kyis chos kyis dbyings thams cad du khebs par byang chub sems
43b5: dpa'i spyod pa bzhis rnam par 'phrul pa dang / nga ros chos kyi dbyings thams cad du rgyas pa'i mtshan rgya mtshos thams cad brgyan pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs
43b6: pa'i mtshan chos kyi dbyings rgya mtsho'i gzhi gang chen mtsho thams cad kyi rgyan dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rgyan tshad med pa'i dgongs pa'i skad cig gis yang dag par ston cing / chos kyi dbyings dang / 'jig rten gyi
43b7: khams thams cad dubasam gyis mi khyab par 'gangs pas sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsha'i spyod pa nas par gzigs pa'i sman snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bas
43b8: gshegs pa'i mtshan pad mo'i gzhi dang / rgyan gyi me tog ri rab rgya mtsho'i 'od zer rin po che'i gzhi sangs rgyas kyi dgongs pa las byung ba dang / rnam par snang mdzad kyi sbrul pa rgya mtsho mazed pa'i 'od kun tu snang

44a1: spa cas byab mnga' ba dang / dbanan gshegs pa 'dabra' da panan gagags panam can da la gnam me dag/ sangs rgyas kya'adang / gas pa nagagags pa thams dasas gas drang /
44a2: dang / sangs rgyas kyi sku'i gzugs brnyan 'ad nas da / rin po che'i 'od 'gro ba gan rgyamamo dang sangs rgyas kyi chos lhas tog gis 'byung ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi tshul gyis rgya ma tshathams ca
44a3: snang ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rnam par grol ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhizhi gshegs pa'i mtshan bdur+ya rin pa che'i matog dang / gsar kyi bang
44a4: chos kyi 'od zed kyi sa dang / rin po cha'i rgyal ba'i sngon ma lta bur de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'do rnam par dag pas snang ba'i rgyan bstan pas/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du dmigs gang rnam par

44a7: phyogs bcu thams cad du shes rab kyi nyi ma shin tu gsal ba dang / ye shes kyi 'od chos rgya mtsho'i dbyangs dang ldan pa sangs rgyas kyi gdung rnam par dag pa'i spyan ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin
44a8: gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i phreng ba rnam par bkye ba dang / rin po che'i me tog dang / rin po che'i bai dUr+ya'i 'od du 'phro ba'i sangs rgyas kyi 'od seng ge rnam par snang ba'i

44b1: mthu dang ldan pas chos kyi dbyings thams cad du rnam par gnon pa'i macan rgya cha sprin bus cigangs sangs rgyas kyi nang thams cad kyi rdul snyed du yang dag par 'gro bas sangs rgyas kyi mtshan yang dag par sun cing / de'i dkyil 'khor gyi ye shes ston pas/
44b2: de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mtshan dang rnam par 'phrul pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan de kho na thugs su
44b3: chud pa'i mtshan nyid rin po che'i rgyan rnam par dag pas/ de bzhin gshegs pas dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi snying po med pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad du snang ba'i 'od la 'jug pa zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang /

44b5: dang / nam mkha' khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi 'od zer snabs zhing dang / 'jig rten mang por de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa'i 'od rnam par snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin
44b6: gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan sangs rgyas kyi snang ba rin po che thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba'i sgron ma chos kyi dbyings kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud kyis kun tu rnam par dag pas/ sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyi sprin phyogs bcur bkye ba kun
44b7: du snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i rin po che'i 'odod 'phro ba'i na bun gyis byang chub sems dpa'i thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying pos byang chub tu bzhugs te/ chos kyi
44b8: dbyings thams cad du dgos pa'i skad cig re re la byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun yang dag par snyan cing rgyan brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa thams cad yongs su ston pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / / de bzhin

45a1: gshegs pa gang pas byang rgyas 'byugs/ sa bya sa thams du ga sa pa na gar kya mamams da dzunas dag pa sa can da da
45a2: brjod du med pa thams cad yongs su ston pa'i sman snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin pa che rgya mtsho dang / spos ya du 'ong ba sna tshogs kyi 'od
45a3: rini po che'i 'dra ba rab tu 'phel bas sems can gyi khams kyi las rgya mtsho thams cad sgrog pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad sgrog pa'i dbyangs kyi sbyin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul
45a4: de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan yongs su dag pas zhing thams cad kyi rgyan tu snang ba rnam par bkod pa'i phyir chos rgya mtsho'i sgra bsam gyis mi khyabapa/ sangs rgyas nas 'das pa

45a6: gshegs pa'i mtshan sangs rgyas rgya mtsho'i sprini chos kyi dbyings thams cad du bsgribs pa mi mnga' ba/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du bzhugs pa'i 'od rab tu snang ba'i sman ces
45a7: bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan byang chub sems dpa' dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / sems can rgya mtsho bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i chos
45a8: kyi dbyings la 'jug pa'i tshul mang po chos kyi dbyings thams cad du snang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi sprin kun tu 'tshed pa dang / rin po che'i sprin kun tu mchod pa dang / rin po che'i sprin gyi sgron ma'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin

45b1: gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan ye shes kun tu yangs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dang / chos rgya mtsho 'a lam tshad med pa dang / nang ga
45b2: dkyil 'khor dang / byang chub sems dpa' bsngo ba sems can gyi rgyud thams cad kyi bsam pa ji bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi spyod yul gyis zhugs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i smon lam
45b3: dang smod pa'i nga ros sangs rgyas kyi ye shes gzhi kun gyi mthar thug cing thams cad mngon par mkhyen pas chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi kun tu thugs par 'byung ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs
45b4: pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan chos kyi dbyings dang nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad du rin po che snang ba'i sman yad du 'ong ba/ snying po byang chub kyi gzugs brnyan yongs su ston par mngon par 'phags pas drang
45b5: chub sems dpa' dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku yang dag par ston pa'i sprini kun tu bkye bas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du sprin gyi 'od du gnas pa zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul
45b6: bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan gtsugs tor 'od rnam par dag pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od rnam par dag pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od rnam par dag pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par gnon pa
45b7: dang / gzi chen pos chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi kun tu snang bar rin pacha'i rgyal po yar 'od kun nas 'byung ba yongs su grub ste/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du'ong ber gyi sman dang / 'od kyi rkyen phyogs thams ca sra
45b8: bas rnam par snang bar 'gyur zhing / byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs shin tu 'phel ba'i mthu dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par gnon pa'i sman gyis/ phyogs bcu'i zhing gi drab dang

46a1: nam mkha' thams cad rgyas par khyab pa'i byang chub kyi sems rin po che'i 'od gzer gyi spyan ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan gtsug gtor dbul
46a2: gtsug nas mthong ba ris gyis mngon par 'phags shing / 'dam bu chu klung gi gser dang / ra ni po che'i tshon gyis kha dog bzang po rnam pa sna tshogs kyi 'od dang ldan par gyur pa/ gsar gyi thig la drim med pa'i mig 'phrul
46a3: kyis kun nas shin tu brgyan pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dgongs pa'i skad cig re re la yang yongs su ston pa'i sprin kyis kun tu rgyas par khyab cing / zhing gi
46a4: dkyil 'khor snang bar gyur pas zhing gi dkyil 'khor byang chub sems dpa' gnas su gyur pa/ rgyan thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan pa kun tu snang ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i gtsu gtor mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis
46a5: rgyan tu gyur cing / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi rgan tu gyur pa'i spyani snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sangs rgyas kyi mdzod sprul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan sangs rgyas rgya mtsho thams
46a6: cad kyi 'od rab tu sdang ba rin po che thams cad du mdog ltar snang ba/ nyi ma dang zla ba ltar snang zhing shin tu rnam par dag pas phyogs bcur 'od gzer rgya mtsho rab tu 'gyed pa/ kun nas rin po che'i 'od zer
46a7: 'byung ba'i 'od kun tu snang ba'i dpal kun tu rgyas kyi sku rab tu 'bab pa'i sgron ma dri ma med pa'i me tog shin tu rgyas shing ri bo che'i sprin chen po shin tu 'gyed pa/ phyogs kyi 'khor thams cad du rnam par snang zhing de
46a8: b zhin gshegs pa'i chos rgya mtsho thams cad kyi dbyings thams cad du shin tu 'phags pa'i mar me rab tu snang bas rin po che'i rgyal po'i me tog kun tu rgyas shing chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas pa'i sprin

46b1: ces bya ba mnga'o/ / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprin la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan/ mtshan rin po che sna tshogs sems can gyi khams su chags pa med pa'i ye shes kyi sprin rnam par dag pas grub pa/ 'od 'gro ba'i sman
46b2: rin po cheng dral gyi mdog tu kun tu ston pas/ rnam par 'phrul ba'i sprin ces bya ba mang po// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gadral de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che sna tshogs kyis yongs su dag pas ngan pa tha
46b3: cad kyi 'od dang mdog dang / kha dog dang ldan par gyur pa de bzhin du thugs su chud pa/ rin po che'i me tog gi sprin gyis kun tu rgyas shing byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos rgyam
46b4: bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / sems can gyi 'jig rten thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// sangs rgyas kyi ljags yangs pa la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho
46b5: thams cad ljags yangs pa'i sprin kyis kun tu khyab pa'i mtshan nyid yongs su rdzogs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa bas yongs su grub pa/ rin po che thams cad kyi rgyal po'i gzhi las 'od 'phro bas chos kyi dbyings
46b6: thams cad rnam par snang bar mdzad pa'i ngang tshul can/ 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sems kyi gzugs brnyan dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi dbyings kyi rgyan
46b7: t hams cad shin tu ston pa'i gsung dang ldan pa'i sangs rgyas kyi mtshan gyi lcags yangs pa'i sgo rin po che thams cad kyi khang ga dang mdog gis rab tu brdzun pa 'od gzer rgya mtshobs ma gyis maH
46b8: ba rab tu snang ba bzhin mo 'dzum pas/ phyogs bcur rab tu kye zhing 'gro ba thams cad shin tu dang ste/ rin po che rgyal po'i 'od 'phro bas rab tu brgyan par de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung sna tshogs rnam

47a1: par dag pa rab tu brjod cing / shin tu rgya che ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du chos kyi ro 'byin pa bskal pa tshad med par sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi sgra 'byin pa dang / chos
47a2: dbyings gnas pa thams cad du dbyangs shani tu sgrog cing / snang ba yang dag par ston pa'i dbyangs kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i ljags kyi 'og gi drung na de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan
47a3: rin po ches tshogs thams cad ltar spang shing mdzod su yongs su 'khyil ba'i dbyibs 'a bru/ rin pa ni thams cad kyi rang bzhin la bu/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsang kyi / la 'khor phyogs brnanas
47a4: btan pa'i dbyangs dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi sbubs can ljags kyi mtshan nyid yongs su dag pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul gyi mtshan nyid med pa'i dang bzhin du sangs rgyas thams cad kyi
47a5: gsung rgya mtsho bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dbyangs sgrogs pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ljags kyi rtse mo la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che gser gyi 'phro bas sangs rgyas rgya mtsho'i da bangs
47a6: mas cad dran zhi 'di dra 'ong ba'i rin pa ci'i rgyal po'i byangs kyi yan lag 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du sgrogs cing / gsung snyan pa'i dmyong bas sems can la ga bar mang cing bags pa bsam byas pa rgya
47a7: nyan du yad par dbyangs kyi len lag gi yang dag par ston pa'i sbyid/ sems can thams cad la yid du 'ong ba'i chos su snang bas chos kyi dbyings rnam par snang ba'i slan ces byab par / de ban
47a8: la pa sa ma pa ses sa ga pa zhugs pa'i gsung gi paca rgyal bas 'a nas brgyan cing / chags su gyur bas/ sangs rgyas kyim

47b1: bsngags par 'jug pa rnam par bya bgan dang gan du byang chubasams dpa' rnams la yang dag par spyan pa kun margyas kya byangs kyag dang / sangs kyas dang byung chubasams dang mas na/
47b2: yang sangs rgyas kyi gsung la byang nabasams dpa' 'ad cing ga thams cad du ngan pa ca rgyal bstag nas ston pas/ chos kyi byangs sa pa ba'i san pas byabs so// dang da gshegs pa'inas da
47b3: lade bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan men 'dran la sna tshogs dang / bedUr+ya'i dbyings kyim chos kyi dbyings kyi khongs su gtogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sman yongs su byas par mdzad pa/ phyogs thams cad du
47b4: ba ci 'od 'gro dang drim med pa byung bas rnam par snang ba'i sus kyi smon ma'i sun kyi khongs su byang chub sems dnga'i tshogs 'dus par snang bas/ shing rgya mche'i ming du bya ba thams cad dranam par 'phrul ba'i tshul lo
47b5: rab tu gnas shing / chos kyi dbyings bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i chos nyid yang dag par ston pa'i spyan ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems mche ba g.yas kyi 'og ma la de bzhin gshegs pa'i
47b6: mtshan 'dir ni po che'i mtshan gyi rkyen gyis/ chos kyi dbyings yangs pa 'od gzer snang ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor la sna tshogs kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems mche ba rin po che rnam pa thams cad du mdzes pas/
47b7: byung ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bu'i 'od gsal bas 'od ci bkun brtse ba/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgyam tsho'i sems can du gtogs pa thams cad la bkra shes dang / 'khor la rnam bkun tu mdzes
47b8: pas/ rnam par sdang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi choms mche ba de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyadan ces bya ba mnga' ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems mche ba g.yas pa gong ma la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mthad rdo rje smos

48a1: da / da nam rnam tshanas dag /
48a2: na losas phyogs pargya'i sangs rgyas bams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul brgyad par ston pa/ thams cad kyi sang po kyang chub kyi can gyis ni can rkun yang / mdzad papa yo kyi na nas 'a du
48a3: kyi snying po can zhes bya ba mnga'o/ / de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems mche ba g.yon pa'ogam la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan tha dad pa'i mtshan nyid shin tu ston pas sos dang / rin ma che'i yang du 'ong ba'i me tog sa cog
48a4: thams cad dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul sna tshogs kyi 'khor lo dang / rin po che thams cad kyi 'od gzer rnam par snang ba kun tu 'phro ba'i sgron ma dri ma med pa'i sgra ni yang dag par bstan pas/ 'jig rten gyi kham
48a5: r gya mtsha thabs cad du rab tu gsal bas rnam par snang zhing de bzhin gshegs pa gang na seng ge'i khri pad ma'i snying po can drim med pa la bzhugs pa'i sprin byang chub sems dpa'i rgya mtsho'i dbyings su rin po ches

48a8: sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa yongs su ston pas/ byang chub sems dpa' yongs su smin par mdzad cing nam mkha'i dbyings su rgyan thams cad gzugs brnyan gyi sprin zad mi shes

48b1: ba'i kun tu mchad par 'gyed pas chos rgya mtsho rab tu sgrog pa'i sangs rgyas kyi gsung dang / rin po che thams cad kyi tshon du sdang ba'i sangs rgyas nam mkha'i dbyings las gsung gi sgra 'byin pa/ chos kyi sman ma
48b2: 'od de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprin du snang ba zhes bya ba mnga'o/ / de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems kyi mtshams na/ de bzhin gshegs pa mtshan gcig par me tog gi mtshan dang / rgya mtsho'i sgo'i mtshan gyi smani rin poche
48b3: thams cad kyi kha dog du 'dal ba las/ rin po che'i 'od gzer rgya mtsho rab tu 'gyed cing bzhad mo 'dzum pas sangs rgyas kyi 'od nor bu rin po che'i 'od du 'phro ba g.yas phyogs su 'khyil cing / tshes kyi dbyings rgyas
48b4: par khyab par rin po che'i 'od gzer rgya mtsho'i khongs su chud pa'i snying po can gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi tshems kyi mtshams thams cad rjes par gang bas/ skad cig tu 'od kyis rgyas par kun tu rgyu pa'i 'od gzer
48b5: sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho kun tu 'gyed pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga'o/ / de bzhin gshegs pa'i spros la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser dang pad mo'i mdog dang 'od
48b6: ltar snang ba chos kyi dbyings thams cad du mdangs rab tu snang bas dpal phun sum tshogs pas/ ran po che thams cad kyi 'od gzer dang / mdangs kyis kun tu khyab par rnam par snang zhing gser dang pad mo'i mdog
48b7: yongs su dag pas kun tu sbyangs pa/ rin po che thams cad kyi mdangs dang mdog tu snang ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i mgur la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dung gi mgur sangs rgyas thams cad kyi
48b8: 'od lan med lam mer yongs su snang bas/ mdog shin tu gsal zhing gzhi thams cad rin po che'i rgyal pos rnam par snang bar byas pas phyogs thams cad rnam par gsal ba'i 'od gzer rab tu 'gyed cing / 'jig

49a1: rten gyi khams thams cad snang bar mdzad pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku phrag pa g.yas pa la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan nas thams cad kyi 'od dang gser gyi kha dog
49a2: rabatu 'phel bas/ pad mo'i mngog rnas par snang ba dang / rin po cha'i 'od kyi parab cad ste/ kun chags pa par chos kyi yongs drang bar ma da/ byang chub sems dang thams cad khongs su cad pa'i spen
49a3: rla bas/ sangs rgyas rab tu mngar ba thams cad snying por byas pa/ rin pa mthams cad kyigani dang ldan pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku phrag pa'i dbus na de bzhin gshegs
49a4: pa'i mtshan shin tu 'phags shing yongs su rgyas la 'dzam bu chu klung gi gsar gyi 'od dang / mdog yongs su dag pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor lo rab tu snang bas/ chos kyi dbyings snang ba rin pa
49a5: rgyal po mchog tu kun tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku phrag pa g.yon pa la sangs rgyas kyi dbu'i mdzod spu'i dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i gzhi las rin po che'i 'od zer gyi dra ba sna tshogs
49a6: shin tu bsgrubs pa/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser dang / pad mo'i mdog ltar gsal zhing bzang ba rab tu bkye bas chos kyi dbyings dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rnam par 'phrul pa'i 'od ston cing /
