187b8: 'ang mgo rmongs pa med pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu rnam par spyod pa rin po che lta bu gsum pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' chos gcig

188a1: la rnam par spyad pas chos thams cad shes gang chas thams cad don gcag pa dang / don tha dad pa ma yin pa'i mthar thug pa'i nal zas don tha dad pa yang dag par bsnan pa yang ba tugs pa na/
188a2: ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu rnam par spyod pa rin po che ltabu bzhi pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa rnam par bzlog pa
188a3: yang rab tu shes/ nyon mongs pa'i rgyun gcod pa rab tu shes/ nyon mongs pa rnam par gzhal ba yang rab tu shes te/ nyon mongs pa spong ba la shin tu gnas kyang byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa las yang
188a4: dag pa'i mtha' mngon tu mi byed cing yang dag pa'i mtha' yang pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog kyang thob la thabs mkhas pa'i bslab pa la shin tu byed pas/ sngon gyi smon lam yongs su bskrad pa'i spyod pa yod
188a5: su rdzogs par byed kyang lus dub par mi 'gyur ba 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu rnam par spyod pa rin po che lta bu lnga pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan
188a6: yang byang chub sems dpa' ni 'gro ba thams cad sems kyis brtags pa yul mi gnas pa phyogs na mi gnas par shes shing 'jug la yul dang gnas kyang ston te/ rtog pa dang mngon par 'du byed pa'ang med
188a7: la sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba'i phyir mngon par 'du byed pa'i sa la yang spyod pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub
188a8: tu rnam par spyod pa'i rin po che lta bu drug pa'o/ / rgya rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad rang bzhin med pa dang / sna tshogs ma yin pa dang / rnam pa tha dad pa med pa dang

188b1: grangs med pa dang mtshungs pa med pa dang / kha dag med pa dang / mtshan nyid padapas rang bzhin gcag pa rab tu shes te/ gcig tu yang ma dmigs la mang ba' rang bzhin du yang yod pa ma yin par rab tu
188b2: shes te/ byang chub sems dpas chos 'di dag ni sangs rgyas kyi chos so// 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa'i chos so// 'di dag ni rang sangs rgyas kyi chos so// 'di dag ni nyan thos kyi chos so// 'di
188b3: dag ni so so'i skye bo 'chos so/ / di ga ni dge ba dang mi dge ba'i chos so// 'di dag ni 'jig rten gyi chos so// 'di dag ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos so// 'di dag ni kha na ma tho ba dang bcas pa'i chos so// 'di dag
188b4: ni kha na mtho ba med pa'i chos so/ / 'di dag ni zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos so// 'di dag ni zag pa med pa'i chos so// 'di dag ni 'dus byas kyi chos so// 'di dag ni 'dus ma byas kyi chos so zhes bya bar rab tu shes pa 'di
188b5: byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu rnam par spyod pa rin po che lta bu bdun pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das nas
188b6: kyang mi dmigs/ byang chub sems dpa' yang mi dmigs chos kyang mi dmigs/ sems can yang mi dmigs te/ 'di ltar sems can thams cad gdul ba dang / chos thams cad rtogs par bya ba'i phyir smon lam
188b7: kyi rgyun kyang mi gcod do/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de ni byang chub sems dpa' sems la mkhas pas sems can gzhan gi rab tu rtogs pa la mkhas pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi dmigs pa la
188b8: mkhas pas/ sems can thams cad gdams ngag rjes su ston pa la mkhas pa dang / sems can thams cad yongasu mya ngan las 'das par bya ba la mkhas pa'i phyir te/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa de yang

189a1: spen lam yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i byar spyad pa 'dan byang chub sems dpa' blan med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub turnam par spyod pa rin po'i lha tha brgyad pag/ / kye rgyal ba'i sas gnad dang /
189a2: byang chub sems dpa' ni 'du shes kyi byin gyi rlabs thams cad la mkhas pas/ chos rab tu ston cing rnam par 'byed de shes par yang byed la thabs mkhas pas mya ngan las 'das pa yang yongs su ston te/ de yang
189a3: phyin ci log med pa dang nor ba med par rab tu shes te/ byang chub sems dpa' des de bzhin nyid mi g.yo ba'i phyir chos thams cad dus gsum mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yang dag pa'i mtha' la rab tu rten par
189a4: yang yang dag par shes te/ sems can gang dul ba'am 'dul ba 'am 'dul bar 'gyur ba de lta bu'i sems can gang yang rjes su mi mthong la/ byung rgyal du bdag gis bskyed do snyam du'ang mi sems te
189a5: chos gang skye ba 'am 'gag par 'gyur ba de lta bu mi dmigs te/ chos thams cad la mi gnas pas de na yod par 'gyur ba 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub
189a6: tu rnam par spyod pa rin po che lta bu dgu pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa re re las kyang rnam pa tha dad du bgrang ba'i
189a7: tshul gyis bskal pa grangs pa sna tshogs mang tha dad pa gzhan dang gzhan bskal pa de dang de dag tu bdags pa'i bskal pa gcig bzung ba nas brjod du med pa shin tu bstan pa'i bar du lung bstan pa nyan cing / lung bstan pa

195a1: sum tshogs par gyur cig/ bran sum tshogs par 'gyur ram 'gyur zhen rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur bar de ltar bran rgya ma tshogs par gyur cig/ bdag gi dge ba rtsa ba 'dis dge ba' ga

195a3: 'dis dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams dang / gcig cing mnyam pa phun sum tshogs par 'gyur cig/ phun sum tshogs par 'gyur zhe na/ rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur bar de ltar phun sum tshogs par 'gyur
195a4: cig/ bdag gi dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams dang / yid la bya ba gcig pa phun sum tshogs par gyur cig/ phun sum tshogs par 'gyur ram 'gyur zhe na rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur bar de ltar phun sum tshogs par
195a5: gyur cig/ bdag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams dang / yongs su dag pa gcig pa phun sum tshogs par gyur cig/ phun sum tshogs par 'gyur ram 'gyur zhe na rnam pa bzhan
195a6: du mi 'gyur bar de ltar phun sum tshogs par gyur cig bdag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams dang / gcig tu rnam par spyod pa phun sum tshogs par 'gyur cig/ phun sum tshogs par 'gyur
195a7: ma 'gyur zhe na rnam pa bzhin du mi 'gyur bar de ltar phun sum tshogs par gyur cig/ bdag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis dge ba shes gnyen rnams dang / gcig cing mnyam par 'jug pa yongs su rdzogs pa phun
195a8: rgyam tshogs par gyur cig/ bran sumatshogs par 'gyur ram 'gyur zhe na/ rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur bar phun sum tshogs par gyur cig/ bdag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba nga dge ba'i gshes gnyen rnams dang /

195b1: tha mi dang phun sum tshogs par gyur cig/ phun sum tshogs par 'gyur ram 'gyur zhe na rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur bar de ltar phun sum tshogs par gyur cig ces bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chu
195b2: sems dpa' rnams kyis dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su bsngo ba ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su sngo ba blan med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di
195b3: ngag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes khong du chud pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar gtong ba'i sems kyis rnam par 'phrul ba'i ye shes khong du chud par dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad lams
195b4: pa'i ye shes khong du chud pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes mtha' dang dbus med pa la 'jug pa'i ye shes khong du chud pa dang / dris pa thams cad kyi the tsom gcod pa'i ye shes 'a
195b5: du chud pa dang / don shes pa la 'jug pa'i ye shes khong du chud pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsungs la mkhas pas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la yid ches par 'jug pa'i ye shes
195b6: khong du chud pa dang / sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba chung yang rung ste/ thams cad de bzhin/ zhegs pa'i ye shes tshad med par 'gyur bar yid ches par byas shing / chos dkar po thams cad yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i ye shes
195b7: khong du chud pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par spyod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i ye shes khong du chud pa dang / sems skad cig gtsigs sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med par 'gro zhing
195b8: gnas par bya ba'i phyir/ sems skad cig gi ye shes khong du chud pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub mngon par 'chang rgya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad la 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos

196a1: thams cad bstan pa dang / gzung ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gzung sna tshogs la 'jug pa'i rgyan gyi ye shes khong du chud pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni
196a2: byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes khong du chud pa rnams te/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes khong du chud pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/
196a3: rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems bskyed pa mtha' dang dbus med pa rnams ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'ad ltar sangs rgyas thams cad la sems bskyed pa chen po mtha' dang dbus med pa dang / chos/
196a4: kyi dbyings thams cad du 'jug pa la sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dbus med pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi zheng dang dus dang / chos kyi dbyings su 'jug pa la sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dbus
196a5: med pa dang / chos thams cad nam mkha' dang mnyam par bstan pa la sems bskyed pargya chen po mtha' dang dbus med pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad la rgya cher brtan pa la sems bskyed pa mtha'
196a6: dang dbus med pa dang dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas thams cad yid la bya ba la sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dbus med pa dang / las dang rnam par smin pa bsam gyis mi khyab par 'jug la sems bskyed pa rgya chen po
196a7: mtha' dang dbus med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad yongs su dag par bya ba la sems skyed pargya chen po mtha' dang dbus med pa dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad du 'jug pa la sems
196a8: bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang / dbus med pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dbyings rnam par blta ba la sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub

196b1: sems dpa' rnams kyi sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dbus med pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' dang dbus med pa thams cad kyi ye shes chen po rgya mtsho lta
196b2: bur bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gter te/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar chos thams cad la bgrang bas sbyar ba'i gter dang / chos thams cad la des par
196b3: rtogs pa'i gter dang / chos thams cad la gzungs snang ba'i gter dang / chos thams cad la so so yang dag par rig pas rab tu snang ba'i gter dang / chos thams cad la brjod du byed pa'i tshul mkhas par khong du
196b4: chud pa'i gter dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa dang / cho 'phrul thams cad la so sor rtog cing lta ba'i gter dang / chos thams cad la mnyam pa nyid du mngon par bsgrub par mkhas pa'i gter dang / sangs
196b5: rgyas thams cad mthong ba dang mi 'bral ba'i gter dang / sgyu ma lta bu'i bskal pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa yongs su grub par 'jug pa mkhas pa'i gter dang / sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la
196b6: dgal ba dang rab tu dga' ba dang / mos pa chen po rab tu rnyed pa'i gter ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gter te/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas thams
196b7: cad kyi chos kyi ye shes kyi gter bla na med pa thob pas sems can thams cad 'gul ba la brtson par byed pa dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sdom pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na
196b8: 'di ltar sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mi 'khrug mi 'khrul pa'i sdom pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad la bsam pa mi byed pa'i sdom pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la bsam pa rlabs po che'i sdom

197a1: pa dang / dge pa'i bshes gtan thams cad la bsam pa mi 'de pa'i rnal pa dang / nyan zas dang / rang sangs rgyas pan sa bya ba thams cad la yongs su mi 'gyur ba'i sdom pa dang / byang chub sems da
197a2: chung mi za ba'i lam thams cad rnam par bzlog pa'i sdom pa dang / sems can thams cad la khong khrob med pa'i sdom pa dang / dge pa'i rtsa ba brtsam pa thams cad mthar phyin par bya ba'i sdom pa dang / bdud thams
197a3: cad rab tu 'pham par bya ba'i sdom pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i sdom pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sdom pa ste/ de dag la
197a4: gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams ye shes chen po'i sdom pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang ste// bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar
197a5: bskal pa brjod du med par tshe'i tshad byin gyis rlob pas tshal dbang ba dang / ting nge 'dzin grangs med pa la ngas par rtogs par gzhal cing / ye shes kyis 'jug pa'i tshul gyis sems la dbang ba dang / 'jig rten
197a6: gyi khams thams cad rgyan rnam par dbye ba du mas rab tu brgyan par byin gyis brlab pa ston pa'i tshul gyis yo byad la dbang ba dang / dus ji lta ba bzhin du las kyi rnam par smin pa byin gyis rlob pas las la
197a7: dbang ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du skye bston pas skye ba la dbang ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sangs rgyas yongs su gang bar ltabs mos pa la dbang ba dang / dus dang zhe gang
197a8: du'adod par mngon par 'chang rgya bas smon lam la dbang ba dang / rdzu 'phrul gyis rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongs su ston pas/ rdzu 'phrul la dbang ba dang / chos kyi sgo dang sna ba mtha' dang dbus med pa

197b1: yang dag par ston pas chos la dbang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang / mi snyengs pa skad cig skad cig gis go bar yongs su ston pas ye shes la dbang ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po
197b2: de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub kyi med dang pha rol tu phyin pa/ ye shes kyis rnam par 'bral
197b3: pa blan med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ / the rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag na byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rnam par 'phrul pa rnams te/ bcwa gang zhe na 'di ltar sems can la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / shing
197b4: la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos la rnam par 'phrul pa dang // lus la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / smon lam la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / spyod yul rnam par 'phrul pa dang / ye shes la rnam par
197b5: 'phrul pa dang / mngon par shes pa la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems
197b6: dpa'i rnams kyi rnam par 'phrul pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems can la rnam par 'phrul pa gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi
197b7: sems can la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar sems can thams cad sems can med pas sgrol ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi 'du shes kyi rnam par byin gyis brlabs
197b8: pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can thams cad dus la bab na chos bstan pa rgyun mi gcod pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad du sprul pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can

198a1: kyi khams thams cad sgra'i sbubs gcig tu bcud kyang gnod par mi 'gyur ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad 'jig rten gyi khams su byin gyis brlabs te/
198a2: pha rol shes par byed pa dang yongs su ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad du brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi mgon po'i dbang yongs su ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang
198a3: sems can gyi khams thams cad du nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi gzugs dang / kha dog dang mtshan dang / cho ga dang spyod lam yongs su ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams/
198a4: cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thob pa yongs su ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du thams cad mkhyen pa'i stobs mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa'i gzugs
198a5: kyi sgra dang / mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po sna tshogs kyi rgyan yongs su ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dam par 'phrul pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcwa'o//
198a6: 'di dag na byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi zhing la rnam par 'phrul te/ bcu gang zhen 'di ltar zhing thams cad zhing gcig tu byin gyis rlob pa'i rnam par bral pa dang / 'ang thams cad sla'i sbubs su gcig tu mdzud
198a7: pa'i rnam par 'phral ba dang / zhing thams cad mi zad pa la 'jug pa'i rnam par 'phral ba dang / 'ang sa sa dang bye mo zang gcig gas rgyas par 'gengs pa'i lus gcig yongs su ston pa'i rnam par 'phral ba dang / zhing za
198a8: cadang galus su chud par yongs su ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / zhing thams cad rab tu bskyod kyang sems can 'jig rten ji 'jig 'gyur ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / zheng thams cad kyi rgyan rnam par bye bzhir gcig

198b1: tu yongs su ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul ba dang / zhing gcig gi rnam par phye bzhir thams cad kyi rgyan rnam par bye bar yongs su ston pa dang / zhing thams cad kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor kye dkyil 'khor du da ga she
198b2: pa'i sku gcig gis yongs su khyab par sems can thams cad la ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / zhing phra ba dang che ba dang yangs pa dang / rgya che ba dang zab pa dang / sbrul bzhi mnyam pa la 'jug par yongasu gzhol bas/
198b3: phyogs kyi dra ba rnam par phye ba la 'jug par sems can ma lus pa thams cad la yongs su snyan pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ kye chal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi zhing la rnam par 'phral ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i
198b4: sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ bcu gang she na 'di ltar chos thams cad chos gcig tu yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba dang / chos gcig po chos thams cad du yang
198b5: dag par gzhol bar byed kyang sems can gyi bsam pa dang mi 'gal bar rnam par dmigs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgrub par khong du chud par bya ba pha rol gyis go bar bya ba'i rnam
198b6: par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad 'du shes dang bral bar sems can mang pos khong du chud par bya ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad la tshul gcig tu 'jug cing tshul mtha' yas par ston pa'i rnam
198b7: par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad la brjod dra med par 'jug cing/ sgo brgya stong pha rol gyi rgyud du bstan pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad sgo kun nas rgyu ba'i yi ge'i tshul la mkhas par
198b8: rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad chos kyi sgo gcig dang mi 'gal ba la 'jug pa'i tshul khong du chud par ston pas bskal pa rjod du med cing mi zad par rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad sangs

199a1: rgyas byams su 'jug pa la sems can mang pa bzung ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad mtha' dang dbus ma par sangs sa son pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cadang /
199a2: chags pa med pa'i mthar phyin cing mtha' dang dbus med pa'i sgyu ma'i dra ba rnam pa tha dad pa 'jug pas bskal pa mu med par mi zad par sems can la ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa ste// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po dad/
199a3: ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos la rnam para'i phrul ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lus la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar sems can
199a4: thams cad kyi rang gi lus su byin gyis rlob cing / mos par b+ha ba la 'jug pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / rang gi lus la sems can thams cad kyi lus kyi 'du shes sa byin gyis rlob pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang sa
199a5: byas thams cad kyi sgra sangs rgyas gcig gi srung mos shing 'jug pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sangs rgyas gcig gi sasangs rgyas ma lus pa thams cad kyislar 'jugs
199a6: gzhan la yongs su ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul lab dang / zhing thams cad du rnams pa byin gyis rlos pa'i rnam par 'phrul ba dang / dris gsum thams cad chos kyi sku gcig gis yongs su rgyas par sems can
199a7: la stan pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / lus gcig tu ting nge 'dzin la mnyam par bzhag cing lus mtha' yas pa las rnam par ldang ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / waMs gtsigags mngon pa sangs byas shi
199a8: can snyed kyi lus su yongs su ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi lus sems can gcig gi lus su snyan pa'i rnam par 'brel pa dang / sems can thams cad kyil gyi ma /

199b1: rdzas kyi sgra sems can gyi lus su ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag na byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lus la rnam par 'phrul pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu pa 'di dag na byang
199b2: chub sems dpa' rnams kyi smon lam la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi smon lam rang gi smon lam du byin gyis rlob pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sa
199b3: rdzas thams cad kyi rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi smon lam gyi stobs dang / mthu mngon par rdzogs par byang rngub par yongs su ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul ba dang / sems can ster sbyin pa dang rang gi bsam pa bzhin du than
199b4: med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bya ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / bskal pa grangs med pa thams cad du smon lam rgyun mi gcod pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / rnam
199b5: par shes pa'i lus las gyen bskyed de/ ye shes kyi lus la yang mi gnas pa'i smon lam la dbang sgyur bas lus thams cad yongs su ston pa'i rnam par brdul pa dang / rang gi lus tshad du gyur pas pa ram/
199b6: gyi tshogs kyi smon lam thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i rnam par 'phrul ba dang / sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba'i smon lam las phyir mi ldog pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / bskal pa grangs pa
199b7: thams cad byung chub kyi spyod pas byas par dgod pa'i smon lam thun mi 'chad pa'i rnam par 'phrul ba dang / sgra'i sbubs gcig tu mngon par 'tshang rgyu ba'i sman lam gyi stobs kyis sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du byas
199b8: par dgang zhing 'jig rten gyi khams rjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa sems can gcig tu ston pa'i smon lam la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos kyi tshig gcig brjod pas chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad rgyas pa

200a1: bkang ste/ chas kyi sprin chen po 'byung ba las/ chos bdud rtsi 'char rab tu 'bab cang rig pa dang / rnam par thal ba'i klog snang ba dang / yang dag pa de kho na nyid kyi chos kyi 'brug sla mngon par
200a2: 'byung ba'i sems can gyis khams thams cad yongs su ngoms par bya ba'i smon lam chen po yongs su rdzogs par bya bas/ rnam par rtse ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems
200a3: dpa' rnams kyi smon lam la rnam par 'phrul pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod yul la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar kye rgyal ba'i sras
200a4: byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos dbyings kyi spyod yul dang yang ldan la sems can gyi khams kyi spyod yul du yang snang ngo / / kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi spyod yul la mngon par dga' ba
200a5: yin la bdud kyi spyod yul la gnas par yang snang ngo / / kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni ma ngan las 'das pa'i spyod yul dang yang ldan la 'khor ba'i spyod yul las kyang mi g.yo'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras
200a6: byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi spyod yul dang ldan la byang chub sems dpa'i spyod yul gi gcod do/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni zhi ba dang rab tu zhi ba dang nye bar zhi ba'i
200a7: spyo yul dang ldan la/ sems can ma zhi ba rab tu ma zhi ba nye bar ma zhi ba'i spyod yul can rnams kyang rnam par mi spong ba// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni bla na med pa dang 'dor ba med pa dang / smra
200a8: medo pa dang me 'phro ba dang / mtshan ma med pa dang dngos po med pa dang / rnam par mi dmigs pa dang / bar skang mnyam pa'i spyod yul dang / yang ldan la sems can spros pa dang / mtshan ma thams cad dmigs pa'i

200b1: skyeng dul can rnams kyi gnas 'ang snang / / kyergyal ba'i sras byang chub sams dpa' rnams ni stobs dang rnam par thar pa'i spyod yul dang yang ldan la/ phyogs cig pa'i spyod sum thams cad
200b2: 'du na / / rgyal ba'i mas byang chub sems dpa' rnam pa ni sems can med pa mtha' sbed bral dang yang ldan la/ sems can thams cad sangs su smin par bya ba yang rnam par mi sri nga/
200b3: ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni bsam gtan dang rnam par thar pa dang / rtogs pa dang mi gas dben pa'i spyod bul dang ldan la/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad duskye bar yang snang ngo // brgya ba'i sras byang
200b4: chub sems dpa' rnams ni bsam gtan dang rnam par thar pa dang / rtogs pa dang ye shes dben pa'i spyod dul dang yang ldan la/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad duskye bar yang snang ngo // kyergyal ba'i sras byang chubs sa
200b5: dpa' rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod pa dang mngon par 'tshang rgya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi rgyan dang spyod yul thams cad kyang thob la/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi spyod lam dang chog sang yongs su
200b6: ston to/ / rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod yul la rnam par 'phrul pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi legs la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ bcu
200b7: gang zhin 'di ltar sa sa yang dag par rig pa'i ye shes ma zad pa la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / rmongs pa med pa'i gzungs thams cad thob pa'i la shes rnam par 'phrul pa dang smon lam shin turnam par gdon mi zab /
200b8: pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi dbang po yongs su 'dzin pa dang / khong du chud pa'i ye shes la rnam par 'bral pa dang / rang gi sems kyi le shes pa rol gyi sems kyil shes dang / sems gakyi

201a1: las sems can thams cad kyi spad pa dang / rnam par gas par byed pa'amags la rnam par 'phrul ba dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / bag la nyal ba dang bag chags dang ta
201a2: mongs pa'i nad la gang dang 'byor pa'i sman yang dag par gtong ba'i ye shes la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rtsal skad cig gcig gis 'jug pa'i ye shes la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / dus gsum gyi bskal
201a3: pa'i grangs thams cad la chags pa med pa'i migs pa sa gags pab par byed pa'i ma gas rnam par 'phrul ba dang / thogs pa med pa'i sems kyi da cig du mngan par 'dangaHbar 'a ba thams ca
201a4: yongs su ston pa'i ye shes la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems cig gi 'du shes kyis sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi las dang bya ba la mngon sum du 'jug pa'i ye shes la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gcig gi sgra
201a5: dbyangs kyis sgra thams cad la 'jug pa yongs su ston pa'i ye shes la rnam par 'phrul bste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes la rnam par 'phrul ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu pa
201a6: 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mngon par shes pa la rnam par 'phrul ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du lus yongs su ston kyang lus gcig tu dmigs pa'i mngon par shes pa la
201a7: rnam par 'phrul pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du de bzhin gshegs pa'i thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor dang / chos bstan pa yongs su 'dzin pa'i mngon par shes pa
201a8: la rnam par 'bru' ba dang / sems can gcig gi sems la dmigs pas byang chub kyi rgya brjod du med pa rnam par 'tshang rgya zhing sems can thams cad kyi sems kyis pho bar byed pa'i mngon par shes pa la rnam par 'phru

201b1: ba dang / dbyings cig gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du go bar byed cing sgra rnams pa tha dad pa thams cad du shes par byed pas/ sems can gzhan gyi sems kyi rgud du byin par byed pa'i mngon par shes pa la
201b2: rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi sngon gyi mtha'i sngar thug pa'i skal pa sems kyi skad cig gcig gis rjes su dran zhing shes pas las kyi 'bras bu rnam par smin pa ji lta ba bzhin du mngon sum du ston cing
201b3: sems can gis go bar byed pa'i mngon par shes pa la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad brgyan par bya ba'i mngon par shes pa rnam par 'phrul pa dang / dus thams cad mnyam pa nyid du 'jug pa'i mngon
201b4: par shes pa la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub tu spyod pa'i lam yang dag par skyed pa dang / chos kyi snang ba rab tu dgye ba'i mngon par shes pa la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang
201b5: dri za dang lham yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci 'am ci dang lto 'phye chen po dang brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten gi mgon po thams cad kyis mngon par shes pa nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas dang
201b6: byang chub sems dpa' dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyis yongs su bsrungs pa'i mngon par shes pa la rnam pa 'phrul pa dang / kye rgyal ba'i sras mdor na byang chus
201b7: sems dpa' ni mngon par shes pas chos thams cad la yang dag par gzhol ba yin te/ bcu pa de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mngon par shes pa la rnam par 'phrul ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu pa 'di dgan
201b8: byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rdzu 'phrul pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa rdul shing tu phra ba gcig tu mdzad pa'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la chos kyi

202a1: dbyings thams cad dang mnyam pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su ston pa'i rdzu 'phrul rnam par 'phrul pa dang / rgya mtsho thams cad kyi chu'i phung po baspu'i khung bu gcig tu blags te/ chos kyi dbyings dang mnyam
202a2: pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams su 'gro yang sems can la gnod par mi 'gyur ba'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa rang gi lus su btsud de/ bya ba thams cad yongs su ston pa la
202a3: mkhas pa'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'khor yug dang rdo rje'i ri bsam gyis mi khyab pa thams cad bsra'i 'ad bu cig tu bres te/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'gro yang sems
202a4: can rnams sdang bar mi 'gyur ba'i rdza 'phral la rnam par 'phral pa dang / skal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa bskal pa gcig tu byin gyis brlabs te/ bskal pa gcig la brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med
202a5: pa'i bskal pa 'dra ba dang / 'jig pa ston pa kyang sems can la gnod par mi 'gyur ba'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du chus 'jig pa yongs su bstan pa dang / me dang
202a6: rlung gis 'jig pa yongs su bstan kyang sems can la gnod par mi 'gyur ba'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'tshig cing chu dang me dang rlung gis 'jig kyang longs spyod dang
202a7: nye bar spyod pa thams cad kyis yongs su gang bar byas shing sems can la kun tu ston pa'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams bsam gyis mi khyab pa lag pa'i mthil gyis blangs te/ 'jig
202a8: rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang rjod du med par bkod kyang sems can la gnod par mi 'gyur ba'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / zhing thams cad nam mkha'i rang bzhin du yongs su bstan pas

202b1: sems can go ba byed pa'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems
202b2: dpa' rnams kyi ston la rnam par 'phral pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na// 'di ltar yongs su smin par bya ba dang / 'dul ba mi gtong bas sems can gyi stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / nam mkha' brjod du byed pa'i yang brjod du med pa
202b3: thams cad rgyan rnam par bye bas rgyan par yongs su ston pas zhing gi stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / lus thams cad lus med par 'jug pas chos kyi bstobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / spyod pa rgyun mi gcod pas bska
202b4: pa'i stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / gnyis kyis log pa sangs rgyas par byed pas/ sangs rgyas kyi stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad skyed cing rab tu 'dzin pa'i phyir spyod pa dang /
202b5: stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad yang dag par sgrol bas/ sangs rgyas kyi stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad la bdag po med par mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i phyir rang byung gi
202b6: stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes ma lus par mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i phyir thams cad mkhyen pa'i stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can thams cad yongs su ma gtong bas
202b7: snying rje chen po'i stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sa sa bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi stobs kyi rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras sems can la rnam par 'phrul pa gzugs thams
202b8: cad/ stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa yan chad kyi bar tu bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems rnams kyi rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' gang gis rnam par 'phrul pa bcu po de dag thob par

203a1: gyur pa de ni 'dod na blan med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ / 'dod na mngon par 'chang mi rgya'o// 'dod na mngon par 'chang rgya la rgyal spyod pa yang d+han mi gcod do//
203a2: kyi rgyal pa'i bras ca byer zhe na/ byang chubamams dpa' rnams sngo lam tshan pa byung ba/ rlom mas pa'i rnam par 'phrul ba yongasasu ban pal pa las pa byur // pams bcu ba di
203a3: dpa 'dams kyirnam par rdzob ste/ bajug shen 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems can gyi lus la// gang gi sus byin gyis rlob pa byed kyang / sems can gyi lus byed par mabyed pa da/ rnam par ba dang po'o// rgyal
203a4: sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' zhing gi lus la sems can gyi lus byin gyis rlob kyang zhing gi lus 'dres par yang mi byed pa de ni rnam par rtse ba gnyis pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi sul
203a5: sems can gyi lus byin gyis rlob kyang sangs rgyas kyi sku dam par ma byed pa de ni rnam par rtse ba gsum pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi lus la de bzhin gshegs pa
203a6: su yongs su ston kyang nyan thas da rang sangs rgyas kyi mas rgya chen por yang mi byed pa 'di ni rnam par rtsab bzhi pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa 'aspyod pa'i bras la mngon par 'chang rgya ba'i lus yongs su
203a7: skyon kyang spyod pa'i rgyun mi gcod pa don rnam par cebs pa'o/ / kyergyal ba'i mas gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i sras la spyod po yongs su ston kyang / mngon par rdzogs pa kyang
203a8: nye bar lon pa yang mi byed pa de ni rnam par rtse ba drug pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' myang ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings su 'khor ba'i rgyun yongs su ston kyang mya ngan las 'das pa la

203b1: mngon par chags pa mi skyed pa'i di ni rnam par rtse ba bdun pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' 'khor ba la mya ngan las 'das pa la yongs su ston kyang yongs su mya ngan las 'das
203b2: shin tu mya ngan las 'da' bar mi byed pa 'di ni rnam par rtse ba brgyad pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' mnyam par bzhag bzhin du 'di lta ste/ 'ong ba dang 'gro ba dang / 'greng ba dang 'dug pa
203b3: bya ba thams cad yongs su ston kyang / ting nge 'dzin gyi mnyam pa nyid 'khrug par mi byed pa de ni rnam par rtse ba dgu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi zhabs kyi drung nas/
203b4: chos thos nas lus kyang mi snang bar byed la/ ting 'dzin gyi stobs kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa gzhan dang gzhan du lus rnam par dgod pas/ ldang yang
203b5: lus tha dad par yang mi byed/ / ting nge 'dzin tha dad par yang mi byed la de bzhin gshegs pa'i de dag las kyang chos nyan cing thos nas kyang 'dzin cing kun chub par byed la ting nge 'dzin la'ang snyoms par 'jug cing
203b6: chos dri ba gzung ba'i rgyun kyang mi gcod de/ de de ltar mnyam par bzhag pa bzhin du lus mi snang bar yang mi byed la ting nge 'dzin gyi lus dang / sgo mngon par bsgrub pa re res las kyang brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i
203b7: ting nge 'dzin gyi lus dang / sgo mngon par sgrub cig de la bu'i tshul gyis bskal pa thams cad zad par gyur kyang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo mngon par bsgrub pa'i mtha' gang yang med pa de ni rnam par
203b8: bcu pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rnam par rtse ba ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes chen pos rnam par rol pa blan

204a1: med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yul te/ bcu gang zhes na 'di ltar chos kyi dbyings mtha' yas pa'i sgo la 'jug par sems
204a2: can la yongs su ston pa'i yul dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rgyan rnam pa sna tshogs du ma mngon par bsgrub pa 'gro ba thams cad kyis rnam par dmigs par bya ba'i yul dang / sems can gyi khams thams
204a3: cad sprul pa mngon par bsgrub pa rnam par dmigs par bya ba'i yul dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku byang chub sems dpa'i lus su mngon par bsgrub pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lus de bzhin gshegs pa'i skur
204a4: mngon par bsgrub pa'i yul dang / nam mkha'i khams 'jig rten gyi khams su mngon par bsgrub pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams nam mkha'i khams su mngon par bsgrub pa'i yul dang / mya ngan las 'das pa
204a5: 'khor bar mngon par bsgrubs pa dang / 'khor ba mya ngan las 'das par mngon par bsgrub pa'i yul dang / sems can gcig gi skad du brjod pas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad bstan par sgrub pa'i phub dang /
204a6: mtha' yas pa'i sgo nas las kun tu ston cing lus cig tu byin gyis bslab pa dang / lus rnam pa tha dad pa thams cad mngon par bsgrub pa'i yul dang / lus gcig gis chos kyi dbyings thams cad du rgyas par dges
204a7: pa'i yul dang / sems can thams cad kyi sems bskyed pa'i skad cig re re la mtha' yas pa'i sgo mngon par bsgrub cing rnams par 'tshang rgya ba'i yul lo// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems
204a8: dpa' rnams kyi yul te/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes chen po'i yul bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go//

204b1: sangs rgyas cad gcad ces bya ba shan tu rgyas pa chen pa'am/ kham pa bcabargyad du/ rtsal ba'i mas pacapa 'ad dkan byang chubasapas dpa' rnams kyi stobs te/ ban ga zhan
204b2: ltar 'jog rten gyi khams thams cad 'du 'dzin med pa'i phyir bsam pa'i stobs dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la sgyid lug pa med par bya ba'i phyir lhag pa'i bsam pa'i stobs dang / byang chub sems pa'i bcoms
204b3: pa thams cad mthar phyin par bya ba yongs su bstan pa'i phyir sbyor ba'i spobs dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi sems dang / spyod pa rab tu shes par bya ba'i phyir ye shes kyi stobs dang / bsam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par
204b4: bya ba'i smon lam gyi stobs dang / phyi ma'i mtha' bur thug par tshun chad pa med par bya ba'i phyir spyod pa'i stobs dang / theg pa thams cad kyis 'byung bar kun tu bstan pa dang / theg pa chen po las par mi ldog par bya ba'i phyir theg
204b5: pa'i stobs dang / skra'i srabs gcig tu sangs rgyas 'byung ba thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams yongs su dag pa thams cad kun tu bstan pa'i phyir rnam par 'phrul pa'i stobs dang / sems bskyed pa thams cad la byang
204b6: chub tu rnam par 'tshang rgya ba dang / / mi 'bral ba'i phyir byang chub kyi stobs dang // chos kyi tshig gcig brjod pas sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / dbang po ma lus pa lhag ma med pa mtha' dag rtogs par bya
204b7: ba'i phyir chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba'i stobs te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu pa de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi stobs te/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes dang /
204b8: stobs bcu dang ldan pa'i mchog tu 'gyur 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mi 'jigs pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub

205a1: sems dpa' rnams na sa thams cad 'dzin pa'i gzungs rab tu thob pa yan te/ de 'di snyam du shar phyogs dang / byang phyogs dang nub phyogs dang / lho phyogs nas ston pa la la zhag bdag gi gan tu
205a2: byon te/ 'gro ba chen po brgya stong rab tu bshad par gyur na// bdag gis de gzung bar mi nus snyam du mi sems te/ byang chub sems dpa'i chu 'di rjes su mi mthong ngo // rgyu 'di rjes su mi mthong bas mi 'jigs pa chen po'i
205a3: dam pa thob cing brtan la zhum pa med pa'i yid kyis 'gro ba thams cad la ci 'dod pa de dris shig ces skabs 'byed pa 'di ni mi 'jigs pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni yi ge dang brjod pa dang / sba
205a4: dang skad thams cad kyi mtshams sbyor ba rab tu rtogs par bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pas dbang bskur ba'i spobs pa thogs pa med pa dam pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa thob pa yin te/ de dag 'di snyam du shar phyogs dang /
205a5: byang phyogs dang lho phyogs dang nub phyogs nas la la zhig 'ongs te// bdag la chos kyi the rtsom chen po zhig dris par gyur na/ bdag gis lan mi ljon pa snyam du mi sems te/ byang chub sems dpa' rgyu yang rjes su mi mthong
205a6: ngo / / rgyu 'di rjes su mthong bas mi 'jigs pa chen po'i dam pa thob cing 'gro ba thams cad kyi dri ba yongs su dri ba ci yod pa brtag pa dang / 'jigs shad spu ldang pa med par byos la// gang 'dod pa de dag dris shig ces skabs
205a7: 'byed pa 'di ni mi 'jigs pa gnyis pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni stong pa'i chos khong du chud par rtogs pa yin te/ bdag dang bdag gi dang / byed pa po dang byed du 'jug pa dang // tshor ba
205a8: po dang srog dang gso ba dang / gang zag dang phung po dang khams dang / skye mched du lta ba dang bral te/ sems nam mkha' dang mtshungs pa'i rjes su song ba// de dag 'di snyam du bdag la la la zhig gis lus dang / dag

205b1: dang yid kyis gnod par bya'am/ gcig tu myi 'gyur ram snyam du sems dpa' med de/ byang chub sems dpa' mtshan ma'ang rjes sa mi mthong ngo // de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar skyes bu dam pa ni bdag tu 'dzin pa dang / bdag
205b2: gang 'dzin pa dang / bral ba'i phyir te/ mtshan ma'ang rjes su mi mthong bas// ma 'jigs pa chen po dam pa thob cing / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi sngon du 'dor ba la rab tu brtan pa 'di ni mi 'jigs pa gsum
205b3: pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems pa rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis byin du brlabs te/ sangs rgyas kyi snang bas nye bar bstan cing de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod/ lam dang / spyod pa dang tshul la rab
205b4: duganas la spyod lam rnam par ma brtogs shing ji lta ba bzhin du gnas pas de dag 'di snyam du bdag gi spyod la mal la la zhig gis brgal bar mi 'gyur ram sa ma du sems te/ byang chub sems dpa' mtshan ma'ang
205b5: rjes su mi mthong ngo / / mtshan ma'ang rjes su mi mthong bas mi 'jigs pa chen po'i dam pa thob cing 'khor gyi nang du phyin nas// chos ston pa 'di ni mi 'jigs pa bzhi pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems
205b6: dpa' rnams ni lus dang ngag dang / yid shin tu dag cing yongs su dag pa dang / gtsang ba dang gtsang sbra dang / nges pa dang ldan zhing ngan par spyod pa dang ngan du byed pa dang / ngan du smra ba dang bral ba yin te/ de dag ni 'di snyam du
205b7: bdag gi las dang / ngag dang yid las la la zhig gis brgal bar ma 'gyu rar ma snyam du mi sems te/ byang chub sems dpa' mtshan ma'ang rjes su ma mthong ngo // mtshan ma'ang rjes su mi mthong bas 'jig pa dang bral zhing mi 'jigs
205b8: pachen po 'dam pa thob pas sems cad gzhan chos la sbyor ba med pa 'di ni mi 'jigs pa lnga pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni lag na rdo rje rtag tu phye bzhin 'brang bas/ yongs su bsrung ba chen po thob cing / lha

206a1: dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang dri za dang lha ma yin gis rtag tu rim gror bya ba yin/ brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang 'jig rten gyi mgon po rnams kyis rtag tu phyag bya ba yin// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rtag tu
206a2: dgongs pa yin te/ de dag 'di snyam du bdag cag la bdud dam bdud kyi ris su gtogs pa'i lha'am mu stegs can dang / mu stegs kyi spyod pa dang / kun tu rgyu ba dag gam// sems can dmigs pa la mngon par zhen pa la la
206a3: zhig 'ongs shing bar chad byed par mi 'gyur ram zhes bya bar sems pa med de/ byang chub sems dpa' mtshan ma'ang rjes su mi mthong ngo // mtshan ma rjes su mi mthong bas 'jigs pa dang bral zhing mi 'jigs pa chen
206a4: po thob pas dga' zhing yid bde ba dang ldan par byang chub sems dpa'i las thams cad nan tan du byed pa 'di ni mi 'jigs pa drug pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems 'apa' rnams ni sangs rgyas kyis bsngags
206a5: pa'i dran pa rab tu thob cing dran pa'i dbang po mchog dang ldan pas yongs su rmongs pa med pa yin te/ de dag 'di snyam du bdag cag gis chos kyi tshig dang yi ge byang chub sems dpa'i lam dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i
206a6: zhal nas byung ba la la zhig yongs su ma zin pa 'am/ chud za bar 'gyur zhing nub par gyur pa med dam zhes bya bar sems dpa' med de/ byang chub sems dpas mtshan ma 'ang rjes su mi mthong ngo // mtshan ma 'ang rjes su mi thod
206a7: pas 'jigs pa dang bral zhing 'jigs pa med pa chen po'i dam pa thob pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bstan pa yang dag par gzung ba'i phyir nan tan du byed pa 'di ni mi 'jigs pa bdun pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang
206a8: chub sems dpa' rnams ni thabs dang shes rab dang / ye shes khong du chud par rtogs shing byang chub sems dpa'i stobs kyis pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog thob pas// rgyun mi 'chad par sems can gyi khams yongs su

206b1: sbyin par byed cing de dag sangs rgyas kyi byang chub tu smon lam dang bsam pa chen po rab tu btang ste/ / sems cad rnams la snying rje chen po rab tu bskyed nas ched du bsams te/ 'jig rten gnas 'dod pa dang 'khrug pa dang /
206b2: nyon mongs pa'i rnyog pa can du skye ba bzung zhing 'dod pa'i dga' ba la rtse ba dang / 'khor gyi longs spyod chen po sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i don du bdag gis yongs su bzung ba byed kyang / de dag 'di snyam du bdag/
206b3: cag sems can gi 'du 'dzi pa'i gos pas yongs su gos par 'gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa'i lam dang ldan pa'i bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa dang / gzungs
206b4: kyi sgo dang / spobs pa'i bar chad dam gcig tu mi 'gyur ram zhes sems dpa' med de/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis rgyu yang rjes su mi mthong ngo // kye rgyal ba'i sras de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems
206b5: dpa' rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i lam la rgyun mi 'chad par spyod pa'i phyir/ chos thams cad la dbang gi pha rol tu phyin pa dam pa thob pa dag ste/ de dag gis 'jig rten gyi rnam par 'khrug pa thams
206b6: cad kyis byang chub sems dpa'i lam la rnam par 'khrug par 'gyur ba rjes su mi mthong ngo / / rjes su mi mthong bas 'jigs pa dang bral zhing mi 'jigs pa chen po'i pha rol tu phyin pa dam pa thob pas 'jig rten
206b7: gyi khams kyi gnas thams cad kyi skye ba'i skye mched thams cad du skye ba gzung bar smon lam rab tu 'debs te/ 'di ni mi 'jigs pa brgyad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni thams cad mkhyen
206b8: pa'i sems ma nyams shing byang chub sems dpa'i lam la gnas pas theg pa chen po la yang dag par gnas pa dag ste/ de dag ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems kyi stobs dang shugs la gnas shing / nyan thos dang rang

207a1: sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chog dang spyod lam yongs sa son kyang / de dag 'di snyam du bdag cag nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa 'am/ tsig gas mi 'byung bar 'gyur ram sam dris pas dpa'
207a2: med de/ byang chub sems dpa' rgyu yang rjes su mi mthong ngo // rgyu'ang rjes su mi mthong bas 'jigs pa dang bral zhing mi 'jigs pa chen po'i pha rol tu phyin pa dam pa thob pas theg pa thams cad mnyam pa nyid du ston cing /
207a3: theg pa chen po'i mnyam pa nyid yongs su rdzogs par byed pa 'di ni mi 'jigs pa dgu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba yang dag par bsdus pas dkar po'i chos yongs su 'dus
207a4: pa yi/ mngon par shes pa dad pasam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa yin// rgyun chad pa med par sangs rgyas kyi byang chub la rab tu rten pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs
207a5: pa yi/ / sangs rgyas thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes dang rdzu 'brung la mngon par dbang skur yang sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i phyir/ spyod pa nye bar blang ba de yang rgyun mo gcod de/ de dag 'di snyam du bdag
207a6: cag gis sems can yongs su smin par mi 'gyur la/ bdag cag kyang sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba ston par mi nus pa'am/ cig tu mi 'gyur ram zhes sems pa med de/ byang chub sems dpas rgyu 'ang
207a7: rjes su mi mthong ngo / / rgyu 'ang rjes su mi mthong bas 'jigs pa dang bral zhing mi 'jigs pa chen po'i pha rol tu phyin pa dam pa thob pas// sems can yongs su smin pa'i tshul ji lta ba bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi yul
207a8: yongs su ston te/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yang rgyun mi gcod la byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam chen pos skye ba yang rgyun mi gcod cing byang chub sems dpas yongs su smin par bya ba 'ang rgyun

207b1: mi gcod de/ 'di ni mi 'jigs pa bcu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mi 'jigs pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams mi 'jigs pa chen
207b2: po bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'jigs pa las kyang phyir ldog par mi 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu pa 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa'i rnams kyi byang chub sems
207b3: da pa'i chos ma 'dres pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhen kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di la byang chub sems dpa' rnams bsam gtam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnams la brtson zhing gtod pa yongs su gtod la/ 'jungs pa dang bral ba
207b4: yin/ tshul khrims yongs su dag la/ tshul khrims ngan pa thams cad rab tu bsul ba yin/ bzod pa phun sum tshogs pa la bsam pa mi skul ba yin// rtsen 'grus chen po dang ldan la dus thams cad du phyir
207b5: mi ldog pa yin/ shin tu mnyam par bzhag pa'i ye shes dang ldan la 'khrug pa thams cad yongs su spangs pa yin/ shes rab kyis shin tu byung zhing sdig pa'i lta ba dang bral ba yin te// kye rgyal ba'i sras de
207b6: ltar ma snyan par pha rol tu phyin pa la brtson pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ma 'dres pa'i chos te/ de ltar pha rol tu phyin pa'i lam dang 'thun pa de ni byang chub sems dpa'i ma 'dres pa'i chos dang po'o//
207b7: rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni sems can gyi khams yongs su sdud cing / 'jig rten gyi zang zing dang / chos kyi sbyin pa yongs su gtong ba'i ngang tshul can/ bzhin 'dzum pa snyan
207b8: par smra ba tshig 'jam pa/ sems can thams cad kyi sems mngon par dga' ba/ don yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin la rab tu sbyor ba/ sangs rgyas kyi byang chub kyi don khong du chud par

208a1: byed pa/ mi mnyam pa'i sems med pa/ sems can thams cad la snyom par don du sems dpa' dgaste// kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar ma bstan par sems can gyi khams yongs su bsdu phyi nganan tan tu byed pa de ni byang
208a2: chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ma 'dres pa ste/ de ltar 'dra ba'i dngos po'i lam dang mthun pa de na byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ma 'dres pa gnyis pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni yongs su bsngo ba'i tshul
208a3: khrims shing rnam par smin pa la re ba med par/ sangs rgyas kyi byang chub kyi rjes su song b.rayongs su sngo zhing 'jig rten gyi snyoms par thams cad la ba ldam pa med pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes la
208a4: rab tu gnas shes sems can gyi don du yongs su sngo ste/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar ma bstan par dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad brtsam pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes de ltar tshol zhing sems can gyi don yongs sa tshol ba 'di ni byang
208a5: chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ma 'dres pa ste/ / 'don byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos ma 'dres pa gsam pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni thabs mkhas pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i dam pa thob sa/
208a6: sems can thams cad kyi rjes su 'brang zhing 'dzag rten pa thams cad kyi lam la yongs su skyob med pa'i yid dang ldan te/ 'phags pa'i spyod yul la mngon du ltas la/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi
208a7: ba las phyir phyogs te/ sems can thams cad yongs su smin pa la mngon par brtson zhing / bdag gi bde ba la chags pa med de/ bsam gtan dang rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms pa la snyoms
208a8: par 'jug pa dang / rnam par ldang ba la mkhas pas rang gi dbang du gyur pa'i ting nge 'dzin thob cing 'khor bas yongs su skyo ba med pa'i sems dang ldan te// 'khor ba la bzo shing gi rab tu 'du shes chen po thob pa dang /

208b1: bdud kyi khyim thams cad na gnas pa dang / brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi mgon po thams cad kyi dbang chen po yongs su ston cing skye ba'i skye mched thams cad du gzugs brnyan byung bar gyur la/ zhags bathub
208b2: pa'i rab tu byung ba thams cad kyi lta ba dang bral te/ 'jig rten pa'i rang bzo dang / sngags dang gtsug lag dang / yi ge dang shod thabs dado// grangs dang rtsis dang / rang gi rtsed me dang / 'jig rten pa'i dga' ba thams
208b3: cad yongs su ston cing / bud med kyi cho ga dang / mtshan ma dang cha lugs dang / sku rtsa ba thams cad kyi tshul la mkhas pa/ 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos nyan pa dang / dpyad pa dang dri ba dang / btas
208b4: pa shin tu bston pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog thob pa/ 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dgos pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog thob pa/ sems can thams cad kyis dor lta ba dbang dang ldan pa dang / rang
208b5: rgyal ba thams cad kyi cho ga dang / spyod lam yongs su ston pa/ theg pa chen po la yang dag par zhugs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'tshang rgya ba skad cig tu ston pa/ spyod pa'i rgyun yongs su mi gcod pa ste/
208b6: kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar thabs mkhas pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog thob kyang bstan pa med pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ma 'dres pa'i chos te/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos ma 'dres pa
208b7: bzhi pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' zung dang snrel bzhi la mkhas shing ye shes kyi rnam par rtse ba dang / ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog thob pas/ 'di ltar mya ngan las 'das pa la
208b8: gnas kyang / 'khor ba'i sgo yongs su ston pa/ sems can med pa'i mtha'i spyod yul dang ldan yang sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba ma btang ba shin tu dral ba dang / zhi ba'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog

209a1: thob kyang / nyon mongs pa'i 'bar ba sems can la yongs su ston pa/ chos kyi ye shes gcig tu skrag pa'i lus dang ldan yang sems gi sgo mtha' yas pa yongs su ston pa/ bsam gtan chen po la bsam
209a2: gtan 'cha' yang 'dod pa'i dga' ba thams cad kyis rtse zhing longs spyod par sems can la rnam par ston pas gcig tu dga' bar bzhag cing mos pa/ khams gsum thams cad las phyir lhas kyang sems can
209a3: thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba'i bsam pa ma btang ba/ rtag tu chos kyi dga' bas dga' zhing mos kyang lhag pa'i bu mo brgya phrag stong gi sgra rab tu byung ba dang rtse ba mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang / dge ba'i mchog
209a4: brgya phrag stong gis bskrun pa'i lus dang ldan yang dbul ba thams cad kyi tshul yongs su ston pa/ rtag tu kha na ma tho ba med pa'i las dge ba spyad kyang sems can dmyal ba dang / byol song gi skye gnas dang / gshen rje'i 'dzi/
209a5: rten du skye ba yang yongs su ston pa/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog thob kyang / byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi lus las gyen du ma g.yos pa dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar byang chub sems
209a6: dpa' rnams ni ye shes mu med pa dang ldan pas/ de'i phyir de dag nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis kyang khong du chud par dka' na sems can byis pa gzhan gyis lta smos kyang ci bgos te/ 'di ni byang chub
209a7: sems dpa'i chos ma 'dres pa lnga pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni lus dang ngag dang yid ye shes sngon du 'gro ba dang ldan pa ste/ las shin tu dag par spyod cing / srog gcod pa dang bral ba
209a8: nas sdig pa'i lta ba'i bar dang bral bas byams pa phun sum tshogs shing yang dag pa'i lta ba la zhugs pa yin te/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las ye shes sngon du 'gro ba dang ldan pa 'di ni byang

209b1: chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos ma 'dres pa ste/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i chos ma 'dres pa drug pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni snying rje chen po dang ldan pas sems can thams cad
209b2: yongs su mi gtong zhing sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gi phung po rang gi lus kyi len par mkhas pas/ sems can dmyal ba dang / byol song gi ste gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi sdug bsngal gyis sem
209b3: can gyi don tu yongs su skyo ba med pa'i sems dang ldan zhing sems can gyi khams thams cad dkrol ba la zhugs pa/ / 'dod pa'i dga' ba thams cad kyis rtse zhing yongs su longs spyod pa la chags pa med pa'i yid dang
209b4: ldan pas rtag tu sems can rnams sdug bsngal gyi phung po las 'grol ba la mngon par brtson pa ste/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar snying rje chen po'i stobs yongs su mi gton pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos ma'as
209b5: ba ste/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i chos ma 'dres pa bdun pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni 'gro ba thams cad kyi yid du 'ong zhing mthong na dga' ba ste/ brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang /
209b6: 'jig rten gyi mgon po thams cad kyis phyag bya ba 'gro ba thams cad mthong bar smon pa/ sems can thams cad mngon par dga' ba'i sems dang ldan pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni byang chub sems da
209b7: rnams sun nas las kyi mtha' kha na ma tho ba med pa dang ldan zhing yongs su dag pa'i las gi tshul gi spyod pas de'i phyir de dag mthang bas/ 'gro ba thams cad mi ngoms pa yin ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bu sems can thams cad
209b8: mthong bar mngon par dga' ba de ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos ma 'dres pa ste/ 'don byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos ma 'dres pa brgyad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' lasas ni

210a1: ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems brtan pa dang ldan pa'i lhag pa'i go ca shin tu bgos pas/ de dag ji ltar nyon mongs shing byas pa'i skye bo'i 'du 'dzin dang / ji ltar bsten tam/ nyan thos
210a2: dang rang sangs rgyas kyi tshogs kyi nang du ji ltar byin kyang rung ste/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems rin po che chen po bzang po 'od dang ldan pa de 'jig par mi byed de// kye rgyal ba'i sras de ni 'di lta/ ste dper na nor bu
210a3: rin po che chen po rgyan bzang po zhes bya de chu dang bar byed pa ni pad mo'i rdzing bu ji ltar rnyogs kyang rung ste/ nang du bcug na nor bu rin po che'i 'od gsal zhing bzang po de nyid rnam par mi spong ste/ chu de thams cad kyang /
210a4: s+ho/ pa med par rab tu dang bar byed do// kye rgyal ba'i sras de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang byis pa'i skye bo'i 'du 'dzin ji ltar bsten kyang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems rin po che 'od gsal zhing snang ba
210a5: bzang po tshud zas par mi byed de sems can de dag kyang nyon mongs pa'i rnyog pa de las zlog cing thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems rin po che 'od gsal zhing snang ba de nyid la rab tu 'god do/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar ji ltar nyon
210a6: mongs par gyur kyang rung / byis pa so so skye bo'i 'du 'dzin dang / ji ltar bsten tam/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi tshogs kyi nang du ji ltar phyin kyang rung ste/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems rin po che de nyid
210a7: 'jig par mi byed pa de ni byang chub sems dpa'i chos ma 'dres pa ste/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i chos ma 'dres pa dgu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni rang gi yul gyi ye shes kyi chos la dbang /
210a8: sbyar ba'i pha rol tu phyin pa dam pa thob pa ste/ rang byung gi ye shes kyi dbang bkur bas dbang skur zhing go 'bang skyon med pa la gnas kyang dge ba'i bshes gnyen la gnas pa ring du mi spong zhing de bzhin gshegs pa la

210b1: ris gror bya ba'i rgyun mi gcod do/ / de ltar tshul phun sum tshogs pa dang // 'gro ba thams cad nga dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsten pa las byir mi ldog cing de bzhin pa la rim gror bya ba rgyun mi gcod pa de ni byang chub sem/
210b2: dpa'i chos ma 'dres pa ste/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i chos ma 'dres pa bcu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos ma 'dres pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub
210b3: sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos ma 'dres pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ro/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi las ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar
210b4: 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad yongs su sbyang ba'i las dang / sangs rgyas thams cad bsnyen bkur ba'i las dang / byang chub sems dpa'i grogs thams cad dang dge ba'i rtsa ba gcig tu bya ba'i las dang /
210b5: sems can gyi khams thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba'i las dang / ma 'ongs pa'i dus thams cad kyi byi mtha'i mur thug par yongs su gzung ba'i las dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'gro yang 'jig
210b6: rten gyi khams gcig nas mi g.yo ba'i rdzu 'phrul gyi las dang / kha dog mtha' yas pa'i 'od zer dgye ba'i chos kyi las dang / pad mo'i snying po la byang chub sems dpa'i gzugs 'khod pa yongs su bstan pa'i 'od zer
210b7: gyi las dang / mya ngan las 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bstan pa gzung bas dkon mchog gsum gi rigs rgyun mi 'chad pa'i las dang / 'jig rten thams cad du gyur zhing chos bstan pa dang /
210b8: sems can gdul bas yang dag par sgrub pa'i las dang / nam 'dod pa dang nam sems bskyed pa na smon lam yongs su rdzogs par sems can la yang dag par ston pa'i byin gyis rlabs kyi sa so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu

211a1: dag/ kya ya / dang ga dag
211a2: bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lus te/ bcu gang zhen 'di ltar 'gro ba thams cad du 'byung ba med pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni ma 'ongs pa med pa'o// 'gro ba thams cad du mi dmigs pa
211a3: med pas byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni 'ongs pa'o/ / 'jig rten thams cad kyis dmigs pa ji lta ba bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni bden pa ma yin pa'o// 'jig rten gyi bden par dmigs pa ji lta ba bzhin du byang chub
211a4: sems dpa'i lus 'ardzun pa ma yin pa'o/ / phyi ma'i mtha' mur rgyun mi 'chad pas byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni rgyun mi zad pa'o// bdud thams cad kyis mi shigs pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi las ni brtan pa'o//
211a5: bdud kyi rgol ba thams cad kyis mi skul bas byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni sra ba'o// bsod nams brgya pa'i mtshan gyis shin tu rnam par dag par snang bas byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni mtshan bzang po dang ldan pa'o//
211a6: chos kyi mtshan nyid med pa'i mthar thug pas byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni mtshan ma nyid med pa'o// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang mnyam pa nyid 'thob pas byang
211a7: chub sems dpa'i lus ni kun tu sod pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lus te/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku mi zad pa bla na med pa
211a8: thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lus kyi las te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad lus gcig gis rgyas par 'gengs pa'i lus dang /

211b1: khams can mams thams cad dum yangs saldan pa'i sras rgyalas dang / skyebamams cad gnas pa' mas thalas dang / 'gatan 'ams thams cad du ba' las byalas dang / ba
211b2: byas thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du ba'i lus kyilas dang / 'dag rten gyi khams thams cad lag pa gcig gis can tu khams par byed pa'i las dang / gakhar grag dang nga thams cad
211b3: pa cig gis nyug pa'i lus kyi las dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du rang gi lus 'jig pa dang / 'thung ba yongasu ston pa'i lus dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad lus gcig gis yongs su 'dzin pa'i lus
211b4: kyi las dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad lus med par khong du chud pas zhing yongs su dag pa dang / yongs su rdzogs pa kun tu ston pa'i lus kyi las so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa'
211b5: rnams kyi lus kyi las te/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas kyi chos 'gro ba kun gyis rnam par rig par bya ba bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni
211b6: byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rang bzhin te/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar nan tan dang ldan pas pha rol tu phyin pa'i rang bzhin dang / 'gro ba thams cad yongs su mi gtong bas// bsdu ba'i dngos po'i rang bzhin dang
211b7: sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gi phung po'i rang gi lus kyis len kyang / yongs su mi skyo bas snying rje chen po'i rang bzhin dang / 'gro ba thams cad yongasu skyob pas byams pa chen po'i rang bzhin dang /
211b8: 'gro ba thams cad nye bar 'tshe bas bsod nams kyi rang bzhin dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sku dang / gcig tu 'dres pas ye shes kyi rang bzhin dang / skye ba'i skye mched thams cad las 'das pas chos kyi

212a1: rang bzhin dang / thams cad sgo yongs su ston pas thams cad kyi rang bzhin dang / rdzu 'phrul dang rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongs su ston pas/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rang bzhin dang / nam 'dod pa
212a2: dus su mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bas/ byang chub kyi rang bzhin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rang bzhin te/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams
212a3: de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes chen po'i rang bzhin bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dag ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar sems can thams cad bde
212a4: bar byed pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni 'jam pa'o/ / sems can thams cad kyi sems sim par byed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis ngag ni snyan pa'o// yang dag par ji lta ba bzhin du go bar byed pas
212a5: byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni mi rdzun pa'o/ / rmi lam na yang log par mi smra bas byang chub sems dpa'i ngag ni bden pa'i rjes su 'brang ba'o// rgyu byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi mgon po thams
212a6: cad zil gyis gnon pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni rgya che ba'o/ / chos kyi rang bzhin ston pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni zab mo'i dbyings su sgrog pa'o// chos bstan pa thams cad mi zad pas
212a7: byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni snying po dang ldan pa'o/ / sgra ji lta ba bzhin du khong du chud par byed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni shin tu gsal ba'o// dus dang lus rnam par smin pa ji lta ba bzhin
212a8: du yongs su ston pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni rnam pa tha dad pa'o// bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par spyod pa la 'jug par byed pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni 'gro ba thams

212b1: cad la 'gro ba'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dag ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba
212b2: dag go/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa'i ngag de yang las rnams par dag pa bcus yongs su sbyangs pa yin te/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung la mos pa yongs su dag pa dang /
212b3: byang chub sems dpa'i tshig sngon ma thos pa la mngon par mos pa yongs su dag pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi yid du mi 'ong ba'i tshigs yongs su spangs pas yongs su dag pa dang / sngon gyi mthar dag gi nyes pa bzhi dang
212b4: bral bas yongs su dag pa dang / dga' ba dang mos pa chen pos de bzhin gshegs pa mngon par bstod pas yongs su dag pa dang / sgra chen pos de bzhin gshegs pa mchod par 'ongs pa yang dag par ji lta ba bzhin du/
212b5: sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang / legs pa brjod pas yongs su dag pa dang / bsam pa thag pas sems can gzhan la chos kyi sbyin pas/ sdud pa yongs su dag pa dang / glu'i dbyangs dang / rol mo brdud pa dang dkro
212b6: ba'i dbyangs kyis de bzhin gshegs pa la mngon par bstod pas yong su dag pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mngon sum du chos thos nas rang gi las 'bul bas yongs su dag pa dang / byang chub
212b7: sems dpa'i chos smra ba thams cad las chos thos nas/ rim gro bya ba'i phyir bdag 'bul zhing snying thag pa nas yongs su btong bas yongs su dag pa ste// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa'i ngag ni las rnam par
212b8: dag pa bcu po de dag gis shin tu sbyangs par 'byung ngo / / kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis dag de ltar yongs su sbyangs pa de ltar yang yongs su 'dzin pa bcus/ yongs su bzung bar 'byung ste/

213a1: bcu gang she na 'di ltar lha'i dbang po la sogs pa lha thams cad kyis yongs su bzung bar 'byung bayin/ klu'i dbang po dang / gnod sbyin gyi dbang po dang / dri za'i dbang po dang / lham yin gyi
213a2: dbang po dang / nam mkha' lding gi dbang po dang / mi'am ci'i dbang po dang / lto phye chen po'i dbang po dang / tshangs pa'i dbang po la stsogs pa tshangs pa'i ris su gartogs pa'i lha thams cad kyis
213a3: yongs su gzung bar 'gyur ba yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi dbang po la sogs pa chos sgrub thams cad kyis yongs su gzung bar 'byung ba yin te// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa'i dag ni yongs su
213a4: 'dzin pa/ bcu po dag gis shin tu bzung bar 'byung ngo // kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' dag de ltar shin tu bzung bar 'byung ba de yang dgod pa bcu yongs su grub par byed de/ bcu gang zhe na
213a5: 'di ltar sems can gyi khams mngon par dga' bar byed do/ / 'jig rten gyi khams su go bar byed do// dbang po'i khams la 'jug par byed do// mos pa'i khams rnam par byed do// nyon mongs pa'i
213a6: khams sel bar byed do/ / bag chags kyi khams spong bar byed do// bsam pa'i khams sbyor bar byed do// lhag pa'i bsam pa'i khams rnam par 'phel bar byed do// chos kyi khams rgyas par byed do//
213a7: mya ngan las 'das pa'i khams yang dag par byed de/ dgongs pa bcu pa de dag yongs su sgrub po// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems te/ bcu gang zhe na 'gro ba
213a8: thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba yang dag par 'dzin cing rtog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems ni sa lta bu'o/ / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes rgya chen po'i rgya mtsho mtha' dang dbus med pa la zhugs

213b1: bas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems dpa' ni rgya mtsho lta bu'o// 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba shin tu mtho ba la 'gro ba thams cad rab tu 'god pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'i sems ni
213b2: ri bo lta bu'o/ / kun nas nyon mongs pa med cing bsam pa dag pa dang ldan pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems ni nor bu rin po che lta bu'o// chos thams cad la rab tu rno bas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams
213b3: kyi sems ni rdo rje lta bu'o/ / bdud dang mu stegs can gzhan dang pas kyis rgol ba thams cad kyis mi skul bas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems ni ra'i rgyal po rdo rje'i khong yug shin tu brten zhing mishegs
213b4: pa lta bu'o/ / 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad kyis mi gos pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems ni pad mo lta bu'o// bskal pa thams cad du 'byung ba dang / mthong bar dka' bas byang chub sems dpa' rnams
213b5: kyi sems ni me tog u dum 'bar ra lta bu'o/ / 'gro ba thams cad kyi ma rig pa'i mun pa mun nag dang / rab rib kyis rmugs pasel ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems na nyom lta bu'o// 'gro ba thams
213b6: cad kyis brjod du med pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa'i sems ni bar snang lta bu'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems te/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin
213b7: gshegs pa'i dgongs pa rgya chen po yongs su dag pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems bskyed pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar 'gro ba
213b8: thams cad rab tu dgrol bar bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems skyed do/ / sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa stsal bar bya'o// zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems skyed do// bag chags kyi mtshams 'brel

214a1: pa thams cad ldang bar bya'o zhes byang chubasams dpa' cad/ / chas thams cad la btsam med par zab par bya zhes byang chub sems dpa' sams spyad do// sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngang
214a2: gi phung po rab tu zhi bar bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems skyed do/ / ngan song dang mi khom pa thams cad gcad par bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems skyed do// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnya
214a3: par bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems skyed do/ / byang chub sems dpa'i bslab pa thams cad la nan tan tu bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems skyed do// skra'i sbubs su 'jug par thams cad kyang ma lus
214a4: par 'gro ba thams cad du sangs rgyas thams cad byang chub tu 'tshang rgya bar bstan par bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems skyed do/ / 'gro ba ma lus pa thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / dbang po rab tu rtogs pas
214a5: 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du grags par bya bar chos kyi rnga bla na med pa brdung bar bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems skyed do/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems
214a6: bskyed pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i dgongs pa rgya chen po'i phrin las bla na med pa rtsom par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems
214a7: dpa' rnams kyi sems kyis rgyas par de gang ba ste/ bcu gang she na 'di ltar sems shin tu yangs pa dang ldan pas nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad rgyas par de gang ba dang / mtha' dang dbus med pa khong du chud pas
214a8: chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par gang ba dang / skad cig gcig tu 'dzud pas dus gsum thams cad rgyas par de gang ba dang / gshegs pa dang skye ba dang 'byung ba dang / rnam par 'tshang rgya ba dang /

214b1: chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba dang / mya ngan las 'das pa chen po mngon sum du shes pas sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad du byas par gang ba dang / bag chags dbang po nam mkha' lta bur khong du chud pas/ sems
214b2: can gyi khams thams cad du rgyas par dgang ba dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad khong du chud pa'i ye shes dang ldan pas mi yor lta bu'i ye shes kyis rgyas par dgang ba dang / sgyu ma'i dra ba rnam pa tha dad pa lta
214b3: bur khong du chud pas mtha' dang dbus med par rgyas par dgang ba dang / rang bzhin mi dmigs pas mi skye bar brgyas par dgang ba dang / rang gi sems dang gzhan gyi sems la thogs pa med pas/ chags pa med
214b4: par rgyas par dgang ba dang / sems bskyed pa thams cad la mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa yongs su ston pas dbang gis rgyas par dgang ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni
214b5: sems kyis rgyas par dgang ba ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyis rgyas par dgang ba mtha' dad dbus med pa'i rgyan bla na med pa thob par 'gyur ba dag
214b6: go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras cu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar sangs rgyas thams cad mthong ba dang / kha phyir ldog pa med pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang
214b7: po ni dga' bar byed pa'o/ / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya bar byed pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis dbang po ni mngon par mos pa'o// bya ba thams cad thogs pa med pas byang chub sems
214b8: dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ni phyir mi ldog pa'o/ / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad rgyun mi gcod pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ni gnas pa'o// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul khong du

215a1: chud par bya ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po na shin tu phrabar/ / sems can thams cad kyi dgang ba yangs su grub par byed pa'i byung / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kya pa
215a2: ni rgyun mi 'chad pa'o/ / chos thams cad la rab tu rno pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ni rdo rje lta bu'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul la snang bathob pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams
215a3: kya dbang pon rdo rje'i 'od 'phro ba ltar snang bar byed pa'o/ / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang lus gcig tu gyur pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ni tha mi dad pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs na
215a4: rjes su zhugs pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ni chags pa med pa'i mthar 'ang phyin pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ste/ de dag la gnas
215a5: shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbang po rgya chen po yongs su rdzogs pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bas
215a6: pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad kyis ma gos pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad
215a7: kyi yid la bya ba ma 'dres pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa sangs rgyas kyi byang chub kyi rjes su song ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes su 'byung
215a8: ba'i lam dang mthun pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa bdud dang mu stegs can gzhan dang / mu stegs spyod pa'i rgol ba thams cad kyis mi 'phrogs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams

215b1: kyi bas pa pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor gyis rnam par dag pas kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa chos ji skad du thos pa yongs su mi gto
215b2: bas/ shin tu zin par yang dag par 'dzin pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa skye ba'i bskye mchod thams cad kyis ma gos pas yongs su nyams pa med pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi
215b3: bsam pa legs phra ba la zhugs pa'i phyir zas pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la shin tu brtson pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams
215b4: kyi bsam pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams thams cad mkhyen pa'i dgongs pa bla na med pa yongs su rdzogs par 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub
215b5: sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad bstsogs pa la phyir mi ldog par dbang sgyur ba dang / byang chub
215b6: sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dgongs pa'i tshul bstan pa la nem nur med pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa smon lam dang /
215b7: spyod pa chen po'i rgyun yongs su 'dzin pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la 'jug par bya ba la phul du phyin pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams
215b8: lhag pa'i bsapa pa sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la dbang sgyur bas mngon sum du 'gyur ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa chos sna tshogs kyi tshul la rab tu zhugs pas/ rgya chen ma

216a1: dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa brtsams pa thams cad mthar byin par byed pas gca par 'gyur ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bas pa pating ngan
216a2: dang / snyoms par 'jug pa dang / rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyan thams cad la dbang sgyur ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa sngon gyi smon lam gyis yongs su bzung bas shin tu bstan pa dang
216a3: byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba rgyun mi gcod pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i
216a4: bsam pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas thams cad kyi lhag pa'i dgongs pa bla na med pa yongs su dag pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go//
216a5: sangs rgyas zad gcad ces bya ba'i shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// // bam po bcu dgra pa// / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sbyor ba ste// bcu gang zhe na
216a6: 'di ltar rnam par smin pa la re ba med par bdog pa thams cad yongs su gtong bas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sbyin pa'i sbyor ba dang / gzhan la brnyas pa med pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims
216a7: dang / bslabs pa dang / sbyangs pa'i yon tan dang / sdom pa dang / brtul zhugs dang bka' thub thams cad du yi dam bcas pa la nan tan byed pa'i sbyor ba dang / bdag dang pha rol kyi 'du shes med pas
216a8: byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gnod sems kyi thab dang / gshe ba thams cad rnal bzod cing sems can gyi ngan du byas pa thams cad bzod pa'i sbyor ba dang / lus dang ngag dang sems yang dag par bskul ba

216b1: brtsams pa thams cad mthar phyin par byed pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi brtson 'grus brtsams pa thams cad las phyir mi ldog pa'i spyod pa dang / 'dod pa'i 'khrug pa dang nyon mongs pa'i g.yog 'kho
216b2: yongs su spong bas/ byang chub sems dpa' dus kyi bsam gtan dang / rnams par thar pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang / snrums par 'jug pa dang / mngon par shes pa thams cad mngon par bsgrub pa
216b3: bsod nams bstsags pa thams cad la skyo ba med pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi nan tan gyi sbyor ba dang / sems can med pa la zhugs pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byams pa
